{BKŚS, 1}
mahākhātā mahāśālā puryasty ujjayinīti yā | [BKŚS, 1 1.1]
mahāmbhodhimahāśailamekhalaiva mahāmahī | [BKŚS, 1 1.2]
prāsādān yatra paśyantaḥ saṃtatān haimarājatān | [BKŚS, 1 2.1]
merukailāsakūṭebhyaḥ spṛhayanti na nāgarāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 2.2]
vedamaurvīvipañcīnāṃ dhvanayaḥ pratimandiram | [BKŚS, 1 3.1]
yatra saṃnipatanto 'pi na bādhante parasparam | [BKŚS, 1 3.2]
kṛtaṃ varṇanayā tasyā yasyāṃ satatam āsate | [BKŚS, 1 4.1]
mahākālaprabhṛtayas tyaktvā śivapuraṃ gaṇāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 4.2]
tasyām āsīn mahāseno mahāsenaḥ kṣitīśvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 1 5.1]
yasya devīsahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśa śrīpater iva | [BKŚS, 1 5.2]
ciraṃ pālayatas tasya prajāḥ śāstoktakāriṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 6.1]
gopālaḥ pālakaś ceti sutau jātau guṇāmbudhī | [BKŚS, 1 6.2]
bṛhaspatisamaś cāsya mantrī bharatarohakaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 7.1]
rohantakaḥ surohaś ca tasyāstāṃ tatsamau sutau | [BKŚS, 1 7.2]
narendramantriputrāṇāṃ caturvidyārthavedinām | [BKŚS, 1 8.1]
prayogeṣu ca daṣāṇāṃ yānti sma divasāḥ sukham | [BKŚS, 1 8.2]
atha gāṃ pālayāmāsa gopālaḥ pitṛpālitām | [BKŚS, 1 9.1]
pālako 'pi yavīyastvād yauvarājyam apālayat | [BKŚS, 1 9.2]
mantriputrau tu mantritvam atha bhūmir naveśvarā | [BKŚS, 1 10.1]
navamantrikṛtārakṣā jāyate sma punar vā | [BKŚS, 1 10.2]
gajarājam atho rājā dānarājivirājitam | [BKŚS, 1 11.1]
adhiṣṭhāya jagatsāraṃ nirjagāma bahiḥ puraḥ | [BKŚS, 1 11.2]
taddarśanāśayāyātam anekaṃ nṛkadambakam | [BKŚS, 1 12.1]
bibhyad vyāḍād gajāt tasmād itaś cetaś ca vidrutam | [BKŚS, 1 12.2]
kanyakānyatamā tatra gṛhyamāṇātha hastinā | [BKŚS, 1 13.1]
prāṃśuprākārataḥ prāṃśor agamyāṃ parikhām agāt | [BKŚS, 1 13.2]
khātapātavyathājātasaṃjñānāśāt kṣaṇaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 14.1]
taṭasthā hastipṛṣṭhasthaṃ sābhāṣata ruṣā nṛpam | [BKŚS, 1 14.2]
avadhyam avadhīr yas tvaṃ pitaraṃ tasya kiṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 1 15.1]
adhītavedaṃ yo hanti brāhmaṇaṃ tasya ke mṛgāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 15.2]
iti kanyāvacaḥ śrutvā duḥśravaṃ śvapacair api | [BKŚS, 1 16.1]
cinteṣubhinnahṛdayaḥ praviveśa niveśanam | [BKŚS, 1 16.2]
ativāhya ca duḥkhena dinaśeṣaṃ samāsamam | [BKŚS, 1 17.1]
janavādopalambhāya pradoṣe niryayau gṛhāt | [BKŚS, 1 17.2]
kālakambalasaṃvītaḥ sāsicarmāsiputrikaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 18.1]
samantrāgadasaṃnāhaḥ saṃcacāra śanaiḥ śanaiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 18.2]
atha śuśrāva kasmiṃścit devatāyatane dhvanim | [BKŚS, 1 19.1]
abhisārikayā sārdhaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāminaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 19.2]
hataṃ muṣṭibhir ākāśaṃ tuṣāṇāṃ kaṇḍanaṃ kṛtam | [BKŚS, 1 20.1]
mayā yena tvayā sārdhaṃ baddhā prītir abuddhinā | [BKŚS, 1 20.2]
iyam etāvatī velā khidyamānena yāpitā | [BKŚS, 1 21.1]
mayā tvaṃ tu gṛhād eva na niryāsi pativratā | [BKŚS, 1 21.2]
kaumāraḥ subhāgo bhartā yadi nāma priyas tava | [BKŚS, 1 22.1]
khalīkṛtaiḥ kim asmābhir vṛtheva kulaputrakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 22.2]
evamādi tataḥ śrutvā sā pragalbhābhisārikā | [BKŚS, 1 23.1]
vihasya viṭam āha sma tvādṛśā hi hatatrapāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 23.2]
nanu cittaṃ mayārādhyaṃ tasyāpi bhavataḥ kṛte | [BKŚS, 1 24.1]
na hi bhartṝn aviśvāsya ramante kulaṭā viṭaiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 24.2]
atha nirmakṣikaṃ bhadra madhu pātuṃ manorathaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 25.1]
jahi ghātaya bālaṃ me patiṃ nityapramādinam | [BKŚS, 1 25.2]
atha pāpād asi trastaḥ sphuṭaṃ nāhaṃ tava priyā | [BKŚS, 1 26.1]
nanu durvārarāgāndhaḥ sutāṃ yāti prajāpatiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 26.2]
athavālaṃ vivādena vaidharmyaṃ kiṃ na paśyasi | [BKŚS, 1 27.1]
yena rājyasukhāndhena prajāpālaḥ pitā hataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 27.2]
suduḥśravam idaṃ śrutvā gopālo durvacaṃ vacaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 28.1]
gacchann anyatra śuśrāva dhvaniṃ viprasya jalpataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 28.2]
ayi brāhmaṇi jāgarṣi nandini krandate śiśuḥ | [BKŚS, 1 29.1]
tvaritaṃ yājate dehi stanyaṃ kaṇṭho 'sya mā śuṣat | [BKŚS, 1 29.2]
iti śrutvā giraṃ bhartur vinidrā brāhmaṇī sutam | [BKŚS, 1 30.1]
pitṛghātin mriyasveti nirdayaṃ nirabhartsayat | [BKŚS, 1 30.2]
āḥ pāpe kim asaṃbaddhaṃ pitṛghātinn iti tvayā | [BKŚS, 1 31.1]
bālo 'yam uktety enaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ kupito 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 1 31.2]
kim āryaputra putreṇa yadā rājñā pitā hataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 32.1]
śrutismṛtivid ity etad uvāca brāhmaṇī patim | [BKŚS, 1 32.2]
śrutvaivamādi kaulīnaṃ praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ nṛpaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 33.1]
anayat kṣaṇadāśeṣam asaṃmīlitalocanaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 33.2]
atha gāḍhāndhakārāyāṃ velāyāṃ mantriṇau rahaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 34.1]
apṛcchat ko 'yam asmāsu pravādaḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 1 34.2]
tatas tāv ūcatus trastau satrāsaṃ nṛpacoditau | [BKŚS, 1 35.1]
kaulīnahetuśrutaye cittaṃ devāvadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 1 35.2]
sugṛhītābhidhānasya pradyotasya pitus tava | [BKŚS, 1 36.1]
āsann avyabhicārīṇy ariṣṭāny aṣṭau mumūrṣataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 36.2]
uddhārye dhavale keśe pramādāt kṛṣṇa uddhṛte | [BKŚS, 1 37.1]
uddhartāraṃ mahīpālaḥ kartayāmāsa nāpitam | [BKŚS, 1 37.2]
bhuñjānena ca pāṣāṇe daśanāgreṇa khaṇḍite | [BKŚS, 1 38.1]
kulakramāgato vṛddhaḥ sūpakāraḥ pramāpitaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 38.2]
prakṛter viparītatvaṃ jānann apy evamādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 39.1]
prabho vidher vidheyatvād brāhmaṇān apy abādhata | [BKŚS, 1 39.2]
bhartur īdṛśi vṛttānte mantrī tasyāvayoḥ pitā | [BKŚS, 1 40.1]
adṛṣṭabhartṛvyasanaḥ pūrvam evāgamad divam | [BKŚS, 1 40.2]
śrutamantrivināśas tu sa rājā rājayakṣmaṇā | [BKŚS, 1 41.1]
guruśokasahāyena sahasaivābhyabhūyata | [BKŚS, 1 41.2]
tatas tāte divaṃ yāte yātukāme ca bhūpatau | [BKŚS, 1 42.1]
prajāsu ca viraktāsu jātau svaḥ kiṃkriyākulau | [BKŚS, 1 42.2]
prāptakālam idaṃ śreya iti buddhvā prasāritam | [BKŚS, 1 43.1]
kaulīnam idam āvābhyāṃ saparyanteṣv avantiṣu | [BKŚS, 1 43.2]
krodhabādhitabodhatvād bādhamānaṃ nijāḥ prajāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 44.1]
bandhayāmāsa rājānaṃ rājaputraḥ priyaprajaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 44.2]
śṛṅkhalātantracaraṇaḥ svatantrād bhraṃśitaḥ padāt | [BKŚS, 1 45.1]
sukhasya mahato dadhyau sa rājendro gajendravat | [BKŚS, 1 45.2]
cintāmuṣitanidratvād āhāraviraheṇa ca | [BKŚS, 1 46.1]
sa kṣapāḥ kṣapayan kṣīṇaḥ saṃvatsaraśatāyatāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 46.2]
putreṇaivamavastho 'pi prajāpriyacikīrṣuṇā | [BKŚS, 1 47.1]
na mukta eva muktaś ca yāvat prāṇaiḥ priyair iti | [BKŚS, 1 47.2]
nidānam idam etasya kaulīnasya vigarhitam | [BKŚS, 1 48.1]
itarad vādhunā devaḥ prabhur ity atha bhūpatiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 48.2]
adhomukhaḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā talāhatamahītalaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 49.1]
dṛṣṭvā ca sāsram ākāśam anātha idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 1 49.2]
tulyau śukrabṛhaspatyor yuvāṃ muktvā suhṛttamau | [BKŚS, 1 50.1]
anapāyam upāyaṃ kaḥ prayuñjītaitam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 1 50.2]
kiṃ tu sattvavatām eṣa śaṅkāśūnyadhiyāṃ kramaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 51.1]
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭabhayagrastacetasāṃ na tu mādṛśām | [BKŚS, 1 51.2]
tasmāt pālayataṃ bhadrau pālakaṃ pālakaṃ buvaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 52.1]
idaṃ tv alīkakaulīnam aśakto 'ham upekṣitum | [BKŚS, 1 52.2]
tasyaivaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya vrīḍādhomukhamantriṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 53.1]
kūjan prakāśayāmāsa kṣīṇāṃ tāmraśikhaḥ kṣapām | [BKŚS, 1 53.2]
atha śuśruvire vācaḥ sūtamāgadhabandinām | [BKŚS, 1 54.1]
yaśodhavalitānantadigantodbudhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 1 54.2]
dīnadīnaṃ tad ākarṇya karṇadāraṇam apriyam | [BKŚS, 1 55.1]
pidhāya pārthivaḥ karṇāv uttamāṅgam akampayat | [BKŚS, 1 55.2]
sa cāvocat pratīhārī nivāryantām amī mama | [BKŚS, 1 56.1]
kṣate kṣārāvadekena kiṃ phalaṃ bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 1 56.2]
āsīc cāsyātha vā dhiṅ mām evam ātmāpavādinam | [BKŚS, 1 57.1]
nanu praśasyam ātmānaṃ nāham arhāmi ninditum | [BKŚS, 1 57.2]
niryantraṇavihāreṇa cirajīvini rājani | [BKŚS, 1 58.1]
rājaputreṇa laḍitaḥ kenānyena yathā mayā | [BKŚS, 1 58.2]
samucchinnadurucchedabāhyābhyantaravairiṇā | [BKŚS, 1 59.1]
varṇāśramāḥ svadharmebhyaḥ kiṃ vā vicalitā mayā | [BKŚS, 1 59.2]
avantivardhanasamo nijāhāryaguṇākaraḥ | [BKŚS, 1 60.1]
putraḥ punnarakāt trātā kasyānyasya yathā mama | [BKŚS, 1 60.2]
athavāstām idaṃ sarvam ekenaivāsmi vardhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 61.1]
naravāhanadevena jāmātrā cakravartinā | [BKŚS, 1 61.2]
eka eva tu me nāsīd guṇaḥ so 'py ayam āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 1 62.1]
prasādān mantrivṛṣayor yat tapovanasevanam | [BKŚS, 1 62.2]
iti niṣkampasaṃkalpaś codayāmāsa mantriṇau | [BKŚS, 1 63.1]
sasiṃhāsanam āsthānaṃ maṇḍape dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 1 63.2]
tayos tu gatayoḥ keśān vāpayitvā savalkalaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 64.1]
kamaṇḍalusanāthaś ca bhūpālo niryayau gṛhāt | [BKŚS, 1 64.2]
viṣādaviplutākṣeṇa vakṣonikṣiptapāṇinā | [BKŚS, 1 65.1]
dṛśyamāno 'varodhena viveśāsthānamaṇḍapam | [BKŚS, 1 65.2]
trāsamlānakapolena dṛṣṭaḥ pṛthulacakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 1 66.1]
pālakenābravīt taṃ ca sthita eva sthitaṃ sthitam | [BKŚS, 1 66.2]
prasādāt tāta tātasya vatsarājasya ca tvayā | [BKŚS, 1 67.1]
buddheḥ svasyāś ca śuddhāyāḥ kiṃ nāma na parīkṣitam | [BKŚS, 1 67.2]
ato 'nuśāsitāraṃ tvām anuśāsati bāliśāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 68.1]
yena loke ta ucyante viyātāḥ pitṛśikṣakāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 68.2]
etāvat tu mayā vācyaṃ pitryaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ tvayā | [BKŚS, 1 69.1]
varṇāśramaparitrārtham idam adhyāsyatām iti | [BKŚS, 1 69.2]
tac cāvaśyam anuṣṭheyam asmākīnaṃ vacas tvayā | [BKŚS, 1 70.1]
mādṛśāṃ hi na vākyāni vimṛśanti bhavādṛśāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 70.2]
itīdaṃ pālakaḥ śrutvā sthitvā cādhomukhaḥ kṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 1 71.1]
uttaraṃ cintayāmāsa nāsāgrāhitalocanaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 71.2]
kṛtakṛtrimaroṣas tu rājā pālakam abravīt | [BKŚS, 1 72.1]
bhoḥ siṃhāsanam āroha kiṃ tavottaracintayā | [BKŚS, 1 72.2]
kiṃ cottaraśatenāpi tvayāhaṃ sopapattinā | [BKŚS, 1 73.1]
vegaḥ prāvṛṣi śoṇasya caraṇeneva durdharaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 73.2]
iti dvijātayaḥ śrutvā purohitapuraḥsarāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 74.1]
viṣādagadgadagiraḥ pramṛjyāśru babhāṣire | [BKŚS, 1 74.2]
pālakas te niyojyatvād ājñāṃ mā sma vicārayat | [BKŚS, 1 75.1]
tvanniyogān niyoktāraḥ kasmād vayam udāsmahe | [BKŚS, 1 75.2]
dhriyamāṇe prajāpāle jyeṣṭhe bhrātari pālakaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 76.1]
mṛgendrāsanam ārohan khaṭvārūḍho bhaven nanu | [BKŚS, 1 76.2]
rājyāgnim ādadhad vāpi tvayi varṣaśatāyuṣi | [BKŚS, 1 77.1]
parivettāram ātmānam ayaṃ manyeta ninditam | [BKŚS, 1 77.2]
tasmād asmān nivartasva saṃkalpād atibhīṣaṇāt | [BKŚS, 1 78.1]
śokajāny aśruvārīṇi bhavantv ānandajāni naḥ | [BKŚS, 1 78.2]
baddhāñjalir athovāca kiṃcin namitakaṃdharaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 79.1]
alaṃ vaḥ pīḍayitvā māṃ vacobhir iti pārthivaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 79.2]
mayāyam abhyanujñāto rakṣaṇe ca kṣamaḥ kṣiteḥ | [BKŚS, 1 80.1]
khaṭvārūḍho na bhavitā ninditaḥ śabdavedibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 1 80.2]
asamarthe ca rājyāgneḥ pālane patite mayi | [BKŚS, 1 81.1]
parivettāpi naivāyaṃ bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 81.2]
yac cāpi pihitāḥ karṇā ākarṇya patitadhvanim | [BKŚS, 1 82.1]
prajābhis tac ca na mṛṣā mayā hi nihataḥ pitā | [BKŚS, 1 82.2]
tad idaṃ pātakaṃ kṛtvā yuṣmatpīḍāpraśāntaye | [BKŚS, 1 83.1]
prāyaścittaṃ vrajan kartuṃ na nivāryo 'smi kenacit | [BKŚS, 1 83.2]
mayā cātyaktadharmeṇa yat prajānāṃ kṛte kṛtam | [BKŚS, 1 84.1]
tasya pratyupakārāya pālakaḥ pālyatām ayam | [BKŚS, 1 84.2]
itīdaṃ prakṛtīr uktvā pālakaṃ punar abravīt | [BKŚS, 1 85.1]
avantivardhanaṃ putraṃ matprītyā pālayer iti | [BKŚS, 1 85.2]
vilakṣahasitaṃ kṛtvā gopālaṃ pālako 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 1 86.1]
avantivardhano rājā rājan kasmān na jāyatām | [BKŚS, 1 86.2]
satsu bhartṛṣu bhūpāla guṇavatsv api bhūbhujaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 87.1]
nikṣiptavantaḥ śrūyante putreṣv eva guruṃ dhuram | [BKŚS, 1 87.2]
gopālas tam athovāca bhaviṣyati yuvā yadā | [BKŚS, 1 88.1]
tvaṃ ca vṛddhas tadā yuktaṃ svayam eva kariṣyasi | [BKŚS, 1 88.2]
evaṃ niruttarāḥ kṛtvā prakṛtīs tāḥ sapālakāḥ | [BKŚS, 1 89.1]
sarvatīrthāmbukalaśair abhyaṣiñcat sa pālakam | [BKŚS, 1 89.2]
āropya cainaṃ tvaritaṃ siṃhāsanam udaṅmukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 90.1]
nirjagāma purāt svasmād ekarātroṣito yathā | [BKŚS, 1 90.2]
atha rājani kānanāvṛte puram āspanditalokalocanām | [BKŚS, 1 91.1]
nibhṛtaśvasitāmayadhvaniṃ mṛtakalpāṃ praviveśa pālakaḥ | [BKŚS, 1 91.2]
{BKŚS, 2}
atha bibhrad durucchedaṃ śokaṃ bhrātṛviyogajam | [BKŚS, 2 1.1]
utsṛṣṭapṛthivīcintaḥ pālakaḥ kālam akṣipat | [BKŚS, 2 1.2]
taṃ purodhaḥprabhṛtayaḥ kadācid avadan prajāḥ | [BKŚS, 2 2.1]
utsīdantīḥ prajā rājan nārhasi tvam upekṣitum | [BKŚS, 2 2.2]
bhrātuḥ puraḥ pratijñāya dūrakṣāṃ rakṣituṃ kṣitim | [BKŚS, 2 3.1]
kiṃ śocasi na śoko 'yam upāyaḥ kṣitirakṣaṇe | [BKŚS, 2 3.2]
ṣaṣṭhaṃ pāpāṃśam ādatte rakṣann api nṛpaḥ prajāḥ | [BKŚS, 2 4.1]
nikṣiptakṣitirakṣas tu sarvam eva na muñcati | [BKŚS, 2 4.2]
tasmāj jighāṃsatā pāpaṃ puṇyaṃ copacicīṣatā | [BKŚS, 2 5.1]
rājan dhanyāḥ prajāḥ kāryāḥ sukhaṃ cānububhūṣatā | [BKŚS, 2 5.2]
na ced arthayamānānāṃ vacanaṃ naḥ kariṣyasi | [BKŚS, 2 6.1]
dhruvaṃ drakṣyasi saṃkrāntā deśān rājanvataḥ prajāḥ | [BKŚS, 2 6.2]
avṛttapūrvam asmābhir udāsīne tvayi śrutam | [BKŚS, 2 7.1]
balād agnigṛhān nītaḥ puroḍāśaḥ śunā kila | [BKŚS, 2 7.2]
baṭoś ca bhrāmyato bhikṣāṃ bhikṣāpātrād anāvṛtāt | [BKŚS, 2 8.1]
baṭutvāt kṣiptacittasya hṛtaḥ kākena modakaḥ | [BKŚS, 2 8.2]
iti śrutvā sasaṃtrāso rājā tāḍitadundubhiḥ | [BKŚS, 2 9.1]
mṛgendrāsanam adhyāste sumeruṃ maghavān iva | [BKŚS, 2 9.2]
tasmin nārūḍhamātre ca samaṃ vikasitāḥ prajāḥ | [BKŚS, 2 10.1]

athāvantiṣu jantūnāṃ kṣudrāṇām api kenacit | [BKŚS, 3 1.1]
janyate sma na saṃtāpaḥ pārthive 'vantivardhane | [BKŚS, 3 1.2]
evaṃ bahuṣu yāteṣu vāsareṣu mahīpatiḥ | [BKŚS, 3 2.1]
kadācid vāhayitvāśvān nivṛtto dṛṣṭavān kvacit | [BKŚS, 3 2.2]
tamālālambidolāntar vilasantīṃ kumārikām | [BKŚS, 3 3.1]
kālindīhradasaṃkrāntāṃ lolām indukalām iva | [BKŚS, 3 3.2]
uttarīyāntasaṃsaktam ākarṣantīṃ śikhaṇḍakam | [BKŚS, 3 4.1]
nirmucyamānanirmokaṃ bhogaṃ bhogavadhūm iva | [BKŚS, 3 4.2]
dṛśyamānas tayā rājā tāṃ ca paśyan punaḥ punaḥ | [BKŚS, 3 5.1]
āvṛto hayaśālābhiḥ svaṃ viveśa niveśanam | [BKŚS, 3 5.2]
tatra saṃkṣiptam āsevya majjanādi rahogataḥ | [BKŚS, 3 6.1]
dolāyamānahṛdayo dolām eva vyacintayat | [BKŚS, 3 6.2]
mandāśanābhilāṣasya mandanidrasya bhūpateḥ | [BKŚS, 3 7.1]
mandadharmārthacintasya divasāḥ katicid gatāḥ | [BKŚS, 3 7.2]
kadācid atha velāyāṃ mandaraśmau divākṛti | [BKŚS, 3 8.1]
kṣubhitānām ivāśrauṣīt sa nirghoṣam udanvatām | [BKŚS, 3 8.2]
didṛkṣuḥ kāraṇaṃ tasya samudbhūtakutūhale | [BKŚS, 3 9.1]
prāsādatalam arohad antaḥpuracarāvṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 3 9.2]
nṛmātaṅgaturaṃgoṣṭragavājaiḍakarāsabhān | [BKŚS, 3 10.1]
saṃpramardantam adrākṣīn mātaṅgaṃ saṃghamardanam | [BKŚS, 3 10.2]

pānaprasaktamātaṅgamaṇḍalaprahitekṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 3 12.1]
mātaṅgarājam adrākṣīn mātaṅgagrāmaṇīs tataḥ | [BKŚS, 3 12.2]
ādideśa samīpasthāṃ kanyakām avilambitam | [BKŚS, 3 13.1]
hastikīṭo 'yam uddāmo durdānto damyatām iti | [BKŚS, 3 13.2]
karāmbhoruhasaṃsparśasubhagenātha sāmbhasā | [BKŚS, 3 14.1]
ārāt siṣeca kariṇaṃ kare kuñcitapuṣkare | [BKŚS, 3 14.2]
atha saṃrambhasaṃhārāt saṃvellitakaraḥ karī | [BKŚS, 3 15.1]
vavande caraṇau tasyāḥ saṃspṛśya śirasā mahīm | [BKŚS, 3 15.2]
tām avantipatir dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭapūrvāṃ tathāgatām | [BKŚS, 3 16.1]
citrīyamāṇahṛdayaś cintayāmāsa cetasā | [BKŚS, 3 16.2]

yathāhāyaṃ tathaivedaṃ viśeṣaṃ tu nibodhata | [BKŚS, 3 117.2]
nāradena purā śaptaḥ kruddhenāhaṃ yathā tathā | [BKŚS, 3 118.1]
pratyakṣam eva pūjyānāṃ divyalocanacakṣuṣām | [BKŚS, 3 118.2]
tadā mayaiṣa dīrghāyur bahukṛtvaḥ prabodhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 3 119.1]
sutā dattā mayā tubhyam upayacchasva tām iti | [BKŚS, 3 119.2]
uktaś caivam uvācāyaṃ ninditāṃ kaḥ sacetanaḥ | [BKŚS, 3 120.1]
kanyakām upayaccheta śāpadagdhāt kulād iti | [BKŚS, 3 120.2]
pratyākhyātā yadānena caṇḍasiṃhādisaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 3 121.1]
avantipataye dattā tadā surasamañjarī | [BKŚS, 3 121.2]
saṃdehaś cedamī sarve vidyādharagaṇeśvarāḥ | [BKŚS, 3 122.1]
pṛcchyantām iti pṛṣṭaiś ca tat tatheti niveditam | [BKŚS, 3 122.2]
kāśyapas tam athāvocad avasanno 'si khecara | [BKŚS, 3 123.1]
caṇḍasiṃhādibhir yasmāt pramāṇaiḥ pratipāditaḥ | [BKŚS, 3 123.2]
asya cāvinayasyedaṃ prāyaścittaṃ samācara | [BKŚS, 3 124.1]
vārāṇasyāṃ mṛtāṅgāni gaṅgāmbhasi nimajjaya | [BKŚS, 3 124.2]
pretāvāsakṛtāvāso vasānaḥ pretacīvaram | [BKŚS, 3 125.1]
bhaikṣāśanaś ca varṣānte muktaśāpo bhaviṣyasi | [BKŚS, 3 125.2]
athojjayanyāḥ kathamapy upāgatair jarāndhajātyandhajaḍārbhakair api | [BKŚS, 3 126.1]
didṛkṣubhir vatsanarendranandanaṃ tapovanaṃ sapramadais tadāvṛtam | [BKŚS, 3 126.2]
{BKŚS, 4}
atha vidyādharapatiḥ kāśyapenāryuṣā puraḥ | [BKŚS, 4 1.1]
ṛṣimātulamitrāṇāṃ pṛṣṭo bhāryāgaṇasya ca | [BKŚS, 4 1.2]
āyuṣman vayam ete ca tapovittāḥ sapālakāḥ | [BKŚS, 4 2.1]
tvatkathāśravaṇotkaṇṭhaniṣkampamanasaḥ sthitāḥ | [BKŚS, 4 2.2]
aiśvaryaṃ durlabhaṃ labdham idam āyuṣmatā yathā | [BKŚS, 4 3.1]
svīkṛtāś ca yathā vadhvas tathā naḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 3.2]
atha vidyādhareśasya pṛṣṭasyeti tapasvinā | [BKŚS, 4 4.1]
trāsāt pṛthutarākṣasya jātam acchāyam ānanam | [BKŚS, 4 4.2]
acintayac ca kaṣṭeyam āpad āpatitā yataḥ | [BKŚS, 4 5.1]
atyāsanno 'ticapalaḥ ko na dahyeta vahninā | [BKŚS, 4 5.2]
iyam api bhṛśaṃ raktā prītyāham anayāhṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 6.1]
idaṃ sacetanaḥ ko nu kathayed gurusaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 4 6.2]
śūro mayā hataḥ śatrur māṃ śūraḥ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ | [BKŚS, 4 7.1]
iti śūrakathāṃ śūraḥ kuryāt kaḥ śūrasaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 4 7.2]
anākhyāne muneḥ śāpo mahāpātakam anyathā | [BKŚS, 4 8.1]
sulabhānto varaṃ śāpo dustaraṃ na tu pātakam | [BKŚS, 4 8.2]
kṛta eva tu gauryā me prasādaḥ saṃkaṭeṣu mām | [BKŚS, 4 9.1]
smarer iti na ca nyāyyaṃ tām api smartum īdṛśi | [BKŚS, 4 9.2]
iti cintitamātraiva purastāc cakravartinaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 10.1]
abhāṣata mahāgaurī prabhopahatabhāskarā | [BKŚS, 4 10.2]
ṛṣimātulabhāryāṇāṃ suhṛdāṃ ca sabhūbhujām | [BKŚS, 4 11.1]
śrotuṃ yad ucitaṃ yasya sa tac chroṣyati netaraḥ | [BKŚS, 4 11.2]
ity uktvā vadane tasya paṭūbhūtvā sarasvatī | [BKŚS, 4 12.1]
caritaṃ kathayāmāsa sā citraṃ cakravartinaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 12.2]
munimātulamitrāṇi rājāno dayitāś ca ye | [BKŚS, 4 13.1]
ākhyāyamānaṃ caritaṃ śṛṇvantv acalacetasaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 13.2]
asti vatseṣu nagarī kauśāmbī hṛdayaṃ bhuvaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 14.1]
saṃniviṣṭānukālindi tasyām udayano nṛpaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 14.2]
manāg janapadasyāsya nagaryāḥ pārthivasya ca | [BKŚS, 4 15.1]
kathayeyaṃ yadi guṇān na kathā kathitā bhavet | [BKŚS, 4 15.2]
yo hi saptārṇavadvīpāṃ draṣṭum uccalitaḥ kṣitim | [BKŚS, 4 16.1]
ratnāni gaṇayen meroḥ kadā draṣṭā sa medinīm | [BKŚS, 4 16.2]
tasmād alaṃ prasaṅgena kathāvyāsaṅgakāriṇā | [BKŚS, 4 17.1]
kathyamānāṃ kathām eva śṛṇuta prakṛtāṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 4 17.2]
mahāvarodhanasyāpi bhāryābuddhir dvaye sthitā | [BKŚS, 4 18.1]
tasya vāsavadattāyāṃ padmāvatyāṃ ca bhūpateḥ | [BKŚS, 4 18.2]
mahāprabhāvā nṛpateḥ śārṅgapāṇer bhujā iva | [BKŚS, 4 19.1]
sakāyā iva copāyāś catvāro mitramantriṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 19.2]
ṛṣabhaś ca rumaṇvāṃś ca tathā yaugandharāyaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 20.1]
vasantakaś ceti sa taiḥ saha kālam ayāpayat | [BKŚS, 4 20.2]
kadācid āsthānagataṃ nṛpaṃ vāṇijadārakau | [BKŚS, 4 21.1]
jānuspṛṣṭamahī pṛṣṭau saṃvijñāpayatām idam | [BKŚS, 4 21.2]
devāvayoḥ pitā yātaḥ sabhayaṃ makarālayam | [BKŚS, 4 22.1]
saha tena sa potena nāgalokaṃ praveśitaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 22.2]
jyeṣṭhaś ca tanayas tasya pitṛbhaktyaiva sāgaram | [BKŚS, 4 23.1]
gatas tatraiva ca gataḥ so 'pi tātagatāṃ gatim | [BKŚS, 4 23.2]
yac ca no draviṇaṃ sāraṃ tad gṛhītvā prajāvatī | [BKŚS, 4 24.1]
sthitā na mṛgyamāṇāpi bahukṛtvaḥ prayacchati | [BKŚS, 4 24.2]
tena deva yadi nyāyyaṃ pitṛdraviṇam āvayoḥ | [BKŚS, 4 25.1]
bhrātṛjāyā tataḥ sā nau vyutthitā dāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 25.2]
atha rājāvadat pahvāṃ pratīhārīṃ yaśodharām | [BKŚS, 4 26.1]
duṣkaraṃ kulanārībhī rājāsthānapraveśanam | [BKŚS, 4 26.2]

sā yadāha sabhāyās tat samakṣaṃ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 27.2]

sā dūrād eva māṃ dṛṣṭvā pratyudgamya sasaṃbhramā | [BKŚS, 4 29.1]
svāgataṃ rājajihvāyā ity avocat kṛtasmitā | [BKŚS, 4 29.2]

sā mām āhāgame kāryam āryayā jñāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 30.2]
devādeśe tu kathite tayoktaṃ paṭulajjayā | [BKŚS, 4 31.1]
ārye sarvam idaṃ satyaṃ devarau me yad āhatuḥ | [BKŚS, 4 31.2]
kiṃtu tasyānayor bhrātur vipannaṃ vahanaṃ śrutam | [BKŚS, 4 32.1]
vahanasya punaḥ svāmī vipanna iti na śrutam | [BKŚS, 4 32.2]
sāṃyātrikāś ca bahavaḥ śrutapotavipattayaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 33.1]

tathā kadācid anayoḥ sa bhrātā vahanāpadaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 34.1]

putro me yadi jāyeta jīvan vā patir āpatet | [BKŚS, 4 36.1]
tataḥ svīkṛtasarvasvau devarau me kva yāsyataḥ | [BKŚS, 4 36.2]
etan manasi kṛtvārthaṃ dravyaṃ devarayor aham | [BKŚS, 4 37.1]
na nikṣiptavatī śeṣam āryayā jñāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 37.2]
iti śrutvā mahīpālo vāṇijāv idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 4 38.1]
kuṭumbācāracaturā yuktam āha kuṭumbinī | [BKŚS, 4 38.2]
bhrātṛvye bhavator jāte bhrātur āgamane 'thavā | [BKŚS, 4 39.1]
ubhayor nobhayorvāpi yuktaṃ bhokṣyāmahe tadā | [BKŚS, 4 39.2]

ayaṃ pāṇḍur amī cāsya tanayāḥ pañca pāṇḍavāḥ | [BKŚS, 4 52.2]

mandapuṇyena yātavyaṃ manye puṃnarakaṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 4 54.2]

nivṛtyāpaśyad āvantyāṃ mandirodyānasevinīm | [BKŚS, 4 55.2]

kva devīty uktayākhyātam udyāne putrakasya sā | [BKŚS, 4 63.1]

śrutveti vatsarājasya buddhir āsīd aho mama | [BKŚS, 4 64.1]
bhāryāṇāṃ divasā yānti saha putramanorathaiḥ | [BKŚS, 4 64.2]

na hi bhartrā na ca sutair bhavitavyaṃ tavedṛśaiḥ | [BKŚS, 4 79.2]
tvaṃ lekhābhiḥ patighnībhiḥ sakalaiva karālitā | [BKŚS, 4 80.1]

iṣṭakāloṣṭakair hanti tenāsau vāryatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 94.2]
somadattas tataḥ kruddhaḥ sutāṃ caṇḍam abhartsayat | [BKŚS, 4 95.1]
ulke piśācike gaccha śīghraṃ mama gṛhād iti | [BKŚS, 4 95.2]
sā tu tat paruṣaṃ śrutvā manasvijanaduḥśravam | [BKŚS, 4 96.1]
smarapīḍāsahatvāc ca maraṇāya mano dadhe | [BKŚS, 4 96.2]
araṇyāniṃ tato gatvā maraṇopāyakāṅkṣayā | [BKŚS, 4 97.1]
adrākṣīt kvacid uddeśe prāsādaṃ daityaghātinaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 97.2]
tasyādūre ca sarasīṃ kūjatkurarasārasām | [BKŚS, 4 98.1]
guñjanmadhukaraśreṇīm anumātavyarodhasam | [BKŚS, 4 98.2]
āsīccāsyā mayā tāvan martavyam iti niścitam | [BKŚS, 4 99.1]
upāyeṣu tu saṃdehas tatropāyo 'yam uttamaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 99.2]
devaṃ mādhavam arcantī kamalendīvarādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 4 100.1]
paṅkajāvayavāhārāt kṣīṇā tyakṣyāmi jīvitam | [BKŚS, 4 100.2]
kṛtapuṇyā mṛtā svargaṃ yāsyāmi nirupadravam | [BKŚS, 4 101.1]
narakaṃ tu na yāsyāmi strīmṛtyumṛtasaṃkulam | [BKŚS, 4 101.2]
sākarod iti niścitya yathāsaṃkalpam ādṛtā | [BKŚS, 4 102.1]
rātrau ca baddhaparyaṅkā devaṃ mādhavam asmarat | [BKŚS, 4 102.2]
māsamātre gate 'paśyat svapnānte madhusūdanam | [BKŚS, 4 103.1]
varaṃ varaya putrīti bhāṣamāṇaṃ mudāyutam | [BKŚS, 4 103.2]
sātha vyajñāpayat prahvā devaṃ viracitāñjaliḥ | [BKŚS, 4 104.1]
maraṇaṃ me jagannātha prasādaḥ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 104.2]
devas tām avadan nedaṃ devatārādhanāt phalam | [BKŚS, 4 105.1]
prāṇihatyāvipāko 'yam ātmahatyā ca ninditā | [BKŚS, 4 105.2]
tasmād anyaṃ varaṃ brūhi patiputradhanādhikam | [BKŚS, 4 106.1]
yena hīnāsi vairāgyān niryātā svagṛhād iti | [BKŚS, 4 106.2]
sābravīt kṛtapuṇyābhiḥ patyādiḥ strībhir āpyate | [BKŚS, 4 107.1]
ahaṃ tv ācaritāpuṇyā duḥkhair eva vibhāvitā | [BKŚS, 4 107.2]
tenālaṃ patiputrādicintayā phalahīnayā | [BKŚS, 4 108.1]
mṛtyunā śāntim icchāmi sā me saṃpādyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 108.2]
so 'bravīt satyam evedaṃ kiṃtu janmāntare tvayā | [BKŚS, 4 109.1]
yavāḍhakaḥ pitur gṛhe brāhmaṇāyopapāditaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 109.2]
sa ca jātaś caturvedaḥ svapuṇyair iha janmani | [BKŚS, 4 110.1]
surūpaḥ sādhuvṛttaś ca sa te bhartā bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 4 110.2]
sa ca tvām urvaśīrūpām eko drakṣyati nāparaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 111.1]
krīto yavāḍhakena tvam iti yāvan na vakṣyasi | [BKŚS, 4 111.2]
janmāntare ca pūrvasmin bhakṣayantyās tilās tava | [BKŚS, 4 112.1]
aṣṭau nipatitā vahnāv añjaler viralāṅguleḥ | [BKŚS, 4 112.2]
te te putrā bhaviṣyanti putri candranibhānanāḥ | [BKŚS, 4 113.1]
maraṇād dāruṇāt tena cittam āvartyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 113.2]
ity uktvāntarhite deve pratibuddhā dadarśa sā | [BKŚS, 4 114.1]
saśiṣyavargaṃ pitaraṃ tadgaveṣiṇam āgatam | [BKŚS, 4 114.2]
tapaḥkṛśāṃ sakaruṇaḥ pitā kāritapāraṇām | [BKŚS, 4 115.1]
śrāmyantīm anayad gehaṃ viśrāmyantīṃ tarau tarau | [BKŚS, 4 115.2]
yā sā piṅgalikā deva devam ārādhya keśavam | [BKŚS, 4 116.1]
varaṃ labdhavatī tasmāt tāṃ mām eva nibodha tām | [BKŚS, 4 116.2]
ekadā tu caturvedaḥ sāntevāsī yadṛcchayā | [BKŚS, 4 117.1]
gṛham asmākam āyātaḥ kṛtātithyo dadarśa mām | [BKŚS, 4 117.2]
mama tātaṃ tu so 'pṛcchad brahman kasyeyam ātmajā | [BKŚS, 4 118.1]
kāntininditacandrābhā yuktaṃ cet kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 118.2]
mameti kathite pitrā māṃ prārthayata sa dvijaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 119.1]
pitrā dattaṃ ca vidhivan muditaḥ pariṇītavān | [BKŚS, 4 119.2]
tataś cārabhya divasāt sa siddha iva kiṃkaraḥ | [BKŚS, 4 120.1]
na kāṃcin na karoti sma mamājñāṃ ninditām api | [BKŚS, 4 120.2]
amī cāṣṭau sutās tasmād acireṇaiva durlabhāḥ | [BKŚS, 4 121.1]
labdhā mayā sutā ye 'sya prasādāl lokadhāriṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 121.2]
iti kāle gate bhartā māṃ kadācid abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 4 122.1]
pṛṣṭhaṃ duḥkhāyamānaṃ me caṇḍi saṃvāhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 4 122.2]
anuktapūrvavacanam uktavantam athābruvam | [BKŚS, 4 123.1]
kim ahaṃ bhavatā krītā pṛṣṭhasaṃvāhiketi tam | [BKŚS, 4 123.2]
so 'bravīn nīcakais trāsād aṅguṣṭhāgreṇa gāṃ likhan | [BKŚS, 4 124.1]
ahaṃ vā kiṃ tvayā krīto yena preṣyatvam āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 4 124.2]
tato vismṛtya samayaṃ bhartāraṃ roṣadūṣitā | [BKŚS, 4 125.1]
krīto yavāḍhakenāsi mayety apriyam abruvam | [BKŚS, 4 125.2]
asāv api ca māṃ dṛṣṭvā sahajākāravañcitām | [BKŚS, 4 126.1]
saṃnikarṣād apakramya saṃbhrānta idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 4 126.2]
api kāsi kutaś cāsi kenāsi vikṛtā kṛtā | [BKŚS, 4 127.1]
kaccit piṅgalikā nāsi kaś ca nāma yavāḍhakaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 127.2]
iti tenānuyuktāhaṃ yathāvṛttam avarṇayam | [BKŚS, 4 128.1]
so 'pi saṃjātanirvedo na jāte kva palāyitaḥ | [BKŚS, 4 128.2]
tasmin deśāntaraṃ yāte tāte ca tridaśālayam | [BKŚS, 4 129.1]
pitṛbhartṛvihīnāham enaṃ deśam upāgatā | [BKŚS, 4 129.2]
svadeśaprītiyogāc ca devyā vāsavadattayā | [BKŚS, 4 130.1]
saputrānugṛhītā asmi bhaktācchādanarakṣaṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 4 130.2]
tena devena yat pṛṣṭaṃ kutas te bālakā iti | [BKŚS, 4 131.1]
evam ete mayā labdhās tuṣṭān nārāyaṇād iti | [BKŚS, 4 131.2]
iti hṛṣṭamatir niśāmya tasyāś caritaṃ putrasamūhalābhahetum | [BKŚS, 4 132.1]
sacivaiḥ sahitaś cakāra rājā sutasaṃprāptiphalaṃ kriyāvicāram | [BKŚS, 4 132.2]
{BKŚS, 5}
atha saṃpreṣitāsthānaḥ sacivān abravīn nṛpaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 1.1]
yad bravīmi nibodhantu bhavantas tat sacetasaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 1.2]
ṛṇaiḥ kila samāghrātaḥ puruṣo jāyate tribhiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 2.1]
brahmacaryeṣṭisaṃtānair ṛṣidevasvadhābhujām | [BKŚS, 5 2.2]
tatrādhigatavedo 'ham iṣṭāśeṣamahākratuḥ | [BKŚS, 5 3.1]
aputratvāt tu pitṛbhir gṛhītaḥ piṇḍabhojibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 3.2]
na ca putrāṅgasaṃsparśāt sukhahetur anuttaraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 4.1]
sukhibhiḥ sa hi nirdiṣṭaś candanād api śītalaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 4.2]
alaṃ cātiprasaṅgena sarvathā gṛhamedhinām | [BKŚS, 5 5.1]
dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasukhaprāpteḥ putrād anyan na kāraṇam | [BKŚS, 5 5.2]
tad asti yadi vaḥ kāṅkṣā niṣprajānāṃ prajāṃ prati | [BKŚS, 5 6.1]
ārabhadhvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ devatārādhanaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 5 6.2]
te tu sapramadāḥ śrutvā rājñaḥ putrārthinaḥ kathām | [BKŚS, 5 7.1]
siddhakalpātmasaṃkalpāḥ pratyūcur darśitasmitāḥ | [BKŚS, 5 7.2]
putrajanma vaṇigvadhvā yātrāyāṃ citradarśanam | [BKŚS, 5 8.1]
piṅgalīdarśanaṃ ceti prayogo 'yam anuṣṭhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 8.2]
asmābhiḥ sa ca devena tathaiva saphalīkṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 9.1]
kṛtaḥ kāle prayogo hi nāphalo jātu jāyate | [BKŚS, 5 9.2]
tena saṃkalpasadṛśīm ārabhadhvaṃ kriyām iti | [BKŚS, 5 10.1]
sacivair abhyanujñātas tatheti pratipannavān | [BKŚS, 5 10.2]
sa puṇye 'hani sampūjya devatāgnidvijanmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 11.1]
yayau nāgavanodyānaṃ sadāraḥ saha mantribhiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 11.2]
māgadhī tu kṛtotsāhā devyā vāsavadattayā | [BKŚS, 5 12.1]
alam āli tavānena khedeneti nivāritā | [BKŚS, 5 12.2]
uktā ca nanu bālāsi mṛṇālītantukomalā | [BKŚS, 5 13.1]
anubhūtasukhā cāsi bhrātur bhartuś ca veśmani | [BKŚS, 5 13.2]
duḥsahāni tu duḥkhāni mayā ninditabhāgyayā | [BKŚS, 5 14.1]
anubhūtāni tenāhaṃ śaktā duḥkham upāsitum | [BKŚS, 5 14.2]
yaś ca me bhavitā putraḥ sa bhavatyā bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 5 15.1]
kṛttikāgarbhasambhūto bhavānyā iva ṣaṇmukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 15.2]
iti tasyāṃ nivṛttāyāṃ saha vāsavadattayā | [BKŚS, 5 16.1]
tapobhir acirād rājā rājarājam atoṣayat | [BKŚS, 5 16.2]
ekadā pratibuddhau tu daṃpatī jātasaṃbhramau | [BKŚS, 5 17.1]
hā devi hāryaputreti vyāharantau parasparam | [BKŚS, 5 17.2]
athopaspṛśya nṛpatir namaskṛtvā dhanādhipam | [BKŚS, 5 18.1]
puraḥ purohitādīnām ācakhyau svapnam ādṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 18.2]
adya paśyāmy ahaṃ svapne vyomni kāmapi devatām | [BKŚS, 5 19.1]
prabhāmbhaḥsaṃtativyastanabhomaṇḍalanīlatām | [BKŚS, 5 19.2]
sā mām uktavatī vācā gambhīrasukumārayā | [BKŚS, 5 20.1]
tvām āhvayati vitteśas tadāśāṃ gamyatām ataḥ | [BKŚS, 5 20.2]
mayaum iti pratijñāte saṃdhyāraktataraṃ karam | [BKŚS, 5 21.1]
āropya prasthitā vyomni diśaṃ vitteśapālitām | [BKŚS, 5 21.2]
śarveṇeha dhṛtā gaṅgā pariṇītātra pārvatī | [BKŚS, 5 22.1]
ityādīn darśayantī nau pradeśaṃ pārvatīpituḥ | [BKŚS, 5 22.2]
nīyamānaḥ krameṇettham athāhaṃ dṛṣṭavān puraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 23.1]
candrapāṣāṇanirmāṇaprākārām alakāpurīm | [BKŚS, 5 23.2]
gaṇānāṃ pārvatībhartur gaṇair agaṇitair yutam | [BKŚS, 5 24.1]
yasyā bāhyam adṛṣṭāntaṃ kalpapādapakānanam | [BKŚS, 5 24.2]
nānāmaṇiprabhājālakalmāṣaśikharāṇy api | [BKŚS, 5 25.1]
śubhrayaty eva harmyāṇi yasyāṃ rudrenducandrikā | [BKŚS, 5 25.2]
avatārya tu māṃ dvāre guhyakeśvaraveśmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 26.1]
vadati kṣaṇam atraiva sthīyatām iti devatā | [BKŚS, 5 26.2]
sā praviśya pratīhāryā saha nirgamya bhāṣate | [BKŚS, 5 27.1]
anujñātapraveśo 'si devenāgamyatām iti | [BKŚS, 5 27.2]
bhavanānīva devānāṃ ṣaḍ atikramya saptame | [BKŚS, 5 28.1]
kakṣāntare prakṛṣṭarddhau paśyāmi draviṇeśvaram | [BKŚS, 5 28.2]
atha tatrāpsarāḥ kācit kāṃcid āha nirīkṣya mām | [BKŚS, 5 29.1]
sakhi nūnam asāv eṣa yasyāsau bhavitā sutaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 29.2]
mayā mantrayamāṇānām ṛṣīṇām agrataḥ śrutam | [BKŚS, 5 30.1]
bharatānām ayaṃ vaṃśe viśuddhe jāyatām iti | [BKŚS, 5 30.2]
na caiṣa kevalaṃ dhanyas tena putreṇa pārthivaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 31.1]
so 'pi sādhūpamānasya putraḥ pātraṃ bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 5 31.2]
tena tattādṛśaṃ putraṃ labhatām eṣa bhūpatiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 32.1]
asāv api śacīśakracaritau pitarāv api | [BKŚS, 5 32.2]
kārye guruṇi saktatvāt tṛṇīkṛtasurāṅganaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 33.1]
sakiṃkaragaṇaṃ prahvaḥ praṇamāmi dhanādhipam | [BKŚS, 5 33.2]
manuṣyadharmā tu bhujaṃ bhujageśvarapīvaram | [BKŚS, 5 34.1]
udyamyāha manuṣyendra svāgataṃ sthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 5 34.2]
āsanne ratnacaraṇe dāpite kanakāsane | [BKŚS, 5 35.1]
vyavadhāya tu mām āste devī nīcaistarāsanā | [BKŚS, 5 35.2]
svananti parivādinyas tāḍitā nāradādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 36.1]
anekākārakaraṇaḥ śrūyate puṣkaradhvaniḥ | [BKŚS, 5 36.2]
urvaśīmenakārambhācitralekhākratusthalāḥ | [BKŚS, 5 37.1]
gāyantyaḥ kuṭṭitatalā nartayante tilottamām | [BKŚS, 5 37.2]
evaṃprāye ca vṛttānte kumāro nalakūbaraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 38.1]
rājarājasutaḥ krīḍann āyātaḥ saha bālakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 38.2]
merusāramahāratnasaṃghātakṛtasaṃhatim | [BKŚS, 5 39.1]
krīḍāśakaṭikāṃ karṣann itaś cetaś ca gacchati | [BKŚS, 5 39.2]
atha skhalitacakrāyās tasyāḥ kusumasaṃcaye | [BKŚS, 5 40.1]
utplutya patitaṃ ratnaṃ vaiḍūryakṣodakuṭṭime | [BKŚS, 5 40.2]
atha prasāritakaraḥ kubero nalakūbaram | [BKŚS, 5 41.1]
mahyam etad dadasveti tad ratnam udayācata | [BKŚS, 5 41.2]
nyastaṃ ca rājaputreṇa rājarājakarodare | [BKŚS, 5 42.1]
ratnaṃ paṅkajagarbhasthabandhūkam iva rājate | [BKŚS, 5 42.2]
duṣṭalakṣaṇamuktānāṃ muktānāṃ parivāritam | [BKŚS, 5 43.1]
ṣaḍviṃśatyā padmarāgam aṣṭāśri bahalaprabham | [BKŚS, 5 43.2]
vittādhipatinā mahyaṃ dattaṃ devyai ca tan mayā | [BKŚS, 5 44.1]
stanayor antare nyastam anayāpi sphuranmudā | [BKŚS, 5 44.2]
siṃhaśāvas tato bhūtvā cañcadvāladhikeśaraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 45.1]
vidārya dakṣiṇaṃ kukṣim etasyāḥ praviśaty asau | [BKŚS, 5 45.2]
tadavasthām imāṃ dṛṣṭvā hā devīti vadann aham | [BKŚS, 5 46.1]
pratibuddha iti svapnam ācaṣṭe sma narādhipaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 46.2]
atha nakṣatraśāstrajñaḥ siddhādeśaḥ sasaṃmadaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 47.1]
ādityaśarmā svapnasya dvijaḥ phalam avarṇayat | [BKŚS, 5 47.2]
vijayasva mahārāja putreṇa dviṣatāṃ gaṇam | [BKŚS, 5 48.1]
samādhineva balinā rāgādīnāṃ balīyasām | [BKŚS, 5 48.2]
vimānaghanasaṃghātasthagitendudivākaraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 49.1]
vidyādharasamūhendraḥ putras tava bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 5 49.2]
yās tā muktāparīvārās tasya ṣaḍviṃśati maṇeḥ | [BKŚS, 5 50.1]
mahākulā bhaviṣyanti bhāryās tava sutasya tāḥ | [BKŚS, 5 50.2]
ye cāṣṭāv aśrayo ratnaṃ parito lakṣitās tvayā | [BKŚS, 5 51.1]
vidyās tā viddhi putrasya bhaviṣyantī bhaviṣyataḥ | [BKŚS, 5 51.2]
evaṃ ca sthāpite svapne rājakīye dvijanmanā | [BKŚS, 5 52.1]
svasvapnaḥ kathitas tatra devyā vāsavadattayā | [BKŚS, 5 52.2]
āryaputreṇa yo dṛṣṭaḥ sa eva sakalo mayā | [BKŚS, 5 53.1]
kukṣau vidāryamāṇe ca hāryaputreti bhāṣitam | [BKŚS, 5 53.2]
iti śrutavataḥ svapnau tulyāv ādityaśarmaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 54.1]
bhaviṣyadviṣaye jñāne dṛḍhatāṃ niścayo gataḥ | [BKŚS, 5 54.2]
atha vijñāpayāmāsa rumaṇvān medinīpatim | [BKŚS, 5 55.1]
dṛṣṭaḥ svapno mayā yaḥ sa śravaṇenānugṛhyatām | [BKŚS, 5 55.2]
deve saniyame jāte cedivatsaniveśinaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 56.1]
devasyāpatyalābhāya sarve saniyamāḥ sthitāḥ | [BKŚS, 5 56.2]
tatrāham adya paśyāmi svapne garuḍavāhanam | [BKŚS, 5 57.1]
mārgitaś ca mayā dehi svāmine naḥ prajā iti | [BKŚS, 5 57.2]
sa vihasyoktavān pūrṇaḥ svāminas te manorathaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 58.1]
tavāpi pūrayāmīti mahyaṃ bāṇaṃ vitīrṇavān | [BKŚS, 5 58.2]
sapraṇāmaṃ tam ādāya hṛdaye nidadhāmi ca | [BKŚS, 5 59.1]
akālakaumudīṃ cemāṃ paśyāmi pratibodhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 59.2]
eṣo 'pi sthāpitaḥ svapnaḥ prītenādityaśarmaṇā | [BKŚS, 5 60.1]
yādṛśo 'sya suto bhavī tādṛśaḥ śrūyatām iti | [BKŚS, 5 60.2]
sāyako hi guṇenārthī tasmād asya bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 5 61.1]
putraḥ ṣāḍguṇyatattvajño yuktaś cāyaṃ guṇair guṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 5 61.2]
paratantragatisthānaḥ khagāmī ca yataḥ śaraḥ | [BKŚS, 5 62.1]
tena rājasutapraiṣyaḥ khecaraś ca bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 5 62.2]
athākathayad ātmīyaṃ svapnaṃ yaugandharāyaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 5 63.1]
mamādyaikonapañcāśan maruto darśanaṃ gatāḥ | [BKŚS, 5 63.2]

{BKŚS, 7}
tatas tātaḥ sabhāṃ dṛṣṭvā tathā saṃjātasaṃpadam | [BKŚS, 7 1.1]

tatrāyaṃ svasutaḥ prītyā bālaḥ saṃskriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 7 3.2]

gāṃ spṛśañ jānuśirasā sa mām idam abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 9 77.2]
vidyādharo 'mṛtagatiḥ kauśikasya muneḥ sutaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 78.1]
sarvavidyādhareśena praṇaman dṛśyatām iti | [BKŚS, 9 78.2]
ehīha ca mayāhūya spṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣṭhe nirāmayaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 79.1]
suhṛddṛṣṭyā ca dṛṣṭaḥ san prahṛṣṭaḥ samupāviśat | [BKŚS, 9 79.2]
tato hariśikhenoktam uktaṃ vṛṣasutena yat | [BKŚS, 9 80.1]
satyaṃ tat priyasaṃbhāṣo mahānāgarako hy ayam | [BKŚS, 9 80.2]
idaṃ śrutvāmitagatir idam asmān abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 9 81.1]
nedaṃ nāgarakatvaṃ me śrūyatāṃ ca kathā yathā | [BKŚS, 9 81.2]
asti prāleyaśailasya manonayanahāriṇi | [BKŚS, 9 82.1]
śikhare kauśiko nāma munis tulyāśmakāñcanaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 82.2]
taṃ ca bindumatī nāma tyaktanandanakānanā | [BKŚS, 9 83.1]
ārādhitavatī yatnāt sudīrghaṃ kālam apsarāḥ | [BKŚS, 9 83.2]
ekadā kauśikenoktā varaṃ brūhīti sābravīt | [BKŚS, 9 84.1]
yadi me bhagavān prītaḥ tato 'patyaṃ dadātv iti | [BKŚS, 9 84.2]
tena cotpāditaṃ tasyām apatyayugalaṃ kramāt | [BKŚS, 9 85.1]
ahaṃ ca putraḥ putrī ca matsvasā matsanāmikā | [BKŚS, 9 85.2]
so 'haṃ saṃvardhitas tena nāsti tad yan na śikṣitam | [BKŚS, 9 86.1]
dhārayāmi ca tadvidyās tena vidyādharo 'bhavam | [BKŚS, 9 86.2]
ekadā pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā rudantam aham abruvam | [BKŚS, 9 87.1]
mādṛśaṃ putram utpādya kiṃ roditi bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 9 87.2]
tenoktaṃ cakravartitvaṃ na te paśyāmi putraka | [BKŚS, 9 88.1]
aṅgād aṅgān madīyāt tu vṛthā jāto bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 9 88.2]
mayoktaṃ mama yaḥ svāmī sa mahyaṃ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 9 89.1]
tenoktaṃ cakravartī yaḥ sa cāpy anviṣyatām iti | [BKŚS, 9 89.2]
mayoktaṃ cakravartitvaṃ yaiś cihnair avagamyate | [BKŚS, 9 90.1]
dṛṣṭvā tāni dhiyā mahyam ācaṣṭāṃ bhagavān iti | [BKŚS, 9 90.2]
tenoktaṃ śatruṇā baddhaṃ yas tvāṃ śaṅkubhir āyasaiḥ | [BKŚS, 9 91.1]
jīvayiṣyati jānīyāt svāminaṃ taṃ bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 9 91.2]
mama tv aṅgārako nāma vyālakaś cābhavat suhṛt | [BKŚS, 9 92.1]
saudaryo gamayāmi sma tābhyāṃ kālaṃ sukhaṃ saha | [BKŚS, 9 92.2]
atha vāyupatho nāma rājā tena sahāgamam | [BKŚS, 9 93.1]
kāśyapasthalakaṃ nāma puraṃ mānasalobhanam | [BKŚS, 9 93.2]
tatraikadā vicaratā mayopavanacāriṇī | [BKŚS, 9 94.1]
dṛṣṭā kanyāparivārā kanyakā kusumālikā | [BKŚS, 9 94.2]
praśasyavarṇasaṃsthānā sā me buddhau sthirā sthitā | [BKŚS, 9 95.1]
praśastir iva vinyastā bhittau vindhyaśilābhṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 95.2]
tām ādāya tayā sārdhaṃ suhṛdbhyāṃ ca manoharāḥ | [BKŚS, 9 96.1]
rataye saṃcarāmi sma saridgiritarusthalīḥ | [BKŚS, 9 96.2]
aṅgārakam athāpaśyaṃ paśyantaṃ kusumālikām | [BKŚS, 9 97.1]
rāgād apatrapātrāsaṃ vakragrīvānirīkṣitam | [BKŚS, 9 97.2]
lakṣito 'ham aneneti lakṣayitvā sahānujaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 98.1]
anāmantryaiva māṃ nīco nīcair utthāya yātavān | [BKŚS, 9 98.2]
ahaṃ tu jātavailakṣyāt saṃraktāc ca tatas trasan | [BKŚS, 9 99.1]
na jānāmi kva yāmīti cakitaḥ saha kāntayā | [BKŚS, 9 99.2]
adya cemāṃ samāsādya ramaṇīyāṃ nagāpagām | [BKŚS, 9 100.1]
avatīrṇo 'smi puline komalāmalavāluke | [BKŚS, 9 100.2]
suratānubhave yogyaṃ dṛṣṭvā tac ca susaṃvṛtam | [BKŚS, 9 101.1]
latāgṛham ahaṃ prāptaḥ phullaśyāmālatāvṛtam | [BKŚS, 9 101.2]
yac ca śeṣam aśeṣaṃ tat kathitaṃ gomukhena vaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 102.1]
tasmād āptopadeśo 'yaṃ na nāgarakatā mama | [BKŚS, 9 102.2]
ko hi vidyādharair baddham avidyādharasainyapaḥ | [BKŚS, 9 103.1]
mocayen mādṛśaṃ tasmāt tathedam ṛṣibhāṣitam | [BKŚS, 9 103.2]
sevante sevakāḥ sevyān prajñāprāṇadhanādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 9 104.1]
yena tenātmarakṣārthaṃ madvidyā gṛhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 9 104.2]
sadyaḥ kṛtopakāreṇa mayā mandādareṇa ca | [BKŚS, 9 105.1]
na gṛhītābruvaṃ cainam anugaccha priyām iti | [BKŚS, 9 105.2]
abravīc ca dinād asmāt pareṇāham aharniśam | [BKŚS, 9 106.1]
apramatto bhaviṣyāmi bhavato deharakṣaṇe | [BKŚS, 9 106.2]
smartavyaḥ saṃkaṭe cāham ity uktvā naḥ praṇamya ca | [BKŚS, 9 107.1]
vegenākāśam utpatya prāgād aṅgārakaṃ prati | [BKŚS, 9 107.2]
ādityaśarmavacanaṃ vacanaṃ ca yakṣyā yānaṃ pradakṣiṇam iṣoś ca marunmṛgāṇām | [BKŚS, 9 108.1]
prahlādināmitagateḥ kathitena jātam utkhātasaṃśayakalaṅkatayā viśuddham | [BKŚS, 9 108.2]
{BKŚS, 10}
atha sampāditaṃ tatra yātrāsthena rumaṇvatā | [BKŚS, 10 1.1]
aśitvodāram āhāraṃ yātrāyai gantum ārabhe | [BKŚS, 10 1.2]
ukṣavṛndārakair yuktam āsthāya syandanaṃ sukham | [BKŚS, 10 2.1]
haṃsair iva śaśāṅkābhair vimānaṃ yādasāṃ patiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 2.2]
akhaṇḍaśaśibimbābhaṃ gomukhaś chatram agrahīt | [BKŚS, 10 3.1]
mṛṣṭahāṭakadaṇḍaṃ ca cāmaraṃ marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 3.2]
rathāgrāvasthito raśmīn ālambata tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 4.1]
ātatajyadhanuṣpāṇiḥ pārśvaṃ hariśikho 'bhavat | [BKŚS, 10 4.2]
āśitaṃ mṛdughāsānāṃ śeṣaṃ snāpitapāyitam | [BKŚS, 10 5.1]
mandam mandaṃ ca naḥ sainyaṃ syandanaṃ parito 'gamat | [BKŚS, 10 5.2]
evaṃprāye ca vṛttānte cāmaraṃ calayan manāk | [BKŚS, 10 6.1]
dṛṣṭvā hariśikhaṃ vākyam avocan marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 6.2]
caratā mṛgayākrīḍām aryaputreṇa pāpikām | [BKŚS, 10 7.1]
pradāya prāṇinaḥ prāṇān dharmaḥ prāpto mahān iti | [BKŚS, 10 7.2]
tenoktaṃ kim ihāścaryam anupāsitasādhunā | [BKŚS, 10 8.1]
śramavyāyāmasāreṇa bhāṣitaṃ yat tvayedṛśam | [BKŚS, 10 8.2]
bhūmimitrahiraṇyānāṃ mitram evātiricyate | [BKŚS, 10 9.1]
tanmūlatvād itarayos tasmān mitram upārjitam | [BKŚS, 10 9.2]
tayoḥ saṃjalpator evam ahaṃ gomukham abruvam | [BKŚS, 10 10.1]
dharmādīnāṃ pradhānaṃ yat tad ācaṣṭāṃ bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 10 10.2]
tenoktaṃ dharmamitrārthā yataḥ kāmaprayojanāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 11.1]
prādhānyaṃ tena kāmasya kāmaś cecchāsukhātmakaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 11.2]
puline hi padaṃ dṛṣṭvā pūrvam icchā prabhor abhūt | [BKŚS, 10 12.1]
yenedam iha vinyastaṃ taṃ paśyeyaṃ kathaṃ nv iti | [BKŚS, 10 12.2]
taṃ ca dṛṣṭvāryaputreṇa sukham āsāditaṃ yataḥ | [BKŚS, 10 13.1]
tan na mitraṃ na dharmārthau kiṃ tu kāmo 'yam arjitaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 13.2]
anyo 'py asti mahākāmaḥ sa yuṣmākaṃ na gocaraḥ | [BKŚS, 10 14.1]
yūyaṃ hi sarvakāmibhyo bāhyā dārumanuṣyakāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 14.2]
nirdiṣṭāḥ kāmaśāstrajñaiḥ puruṣās tu caturvidhāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 15.1]
uttamā madhyamā hīnāś caturthās tu nakecana | [BKŚS, 10 15.2]
uttamo gomukhas teṣām aryaputras tu madhyamaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 16.1]
adhamān kathayiṣyāmi bhavantas tu nakecana | [BKŚS, 10 16.2]
tataḥ krodhād vihasyedam avocan marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 17.1]
aho nāgarakatvaṃ te niṣpannam anujīvinaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 17.2]
api bālabalīvarda satyam evāsi gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 18.1]
ko nāma mānuṣamukhaḥ sann aśuddham udāharet | [BKŚS, 10 18.2]
uttamo gomukhas teṣām aryaputras tu madhyamaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 19.1]
prabhor adhikam ātmānam itthaṃ kaḥ kathayed iti | [BKŚS, 10 19.2]
tenoktaṃ dṛḍhamūḍho 'si na kiṃcid api budhyase | [BKŚS, 10 20.1]
na hi prabhutvamātreṇa bhavaty uttamakāmukaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 20.2]
yaḥ kāmyate ca kāmī ca sa pradhānam ahaṃ yathā | [BKŚS, 10 21.1]
akāmī kāmyate yas tu madhyo 'sāv aryaputravat | [BKŚS, 10 21.2]
yas tu kāmayate kāṃcid akāmāṃ so 'dhamaḥ smṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 22.1]
te nakecana bhaṇyante ye na kāmyā na kāminaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 22.2]
itīdaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yeṣāṃ tān vijānīta kāminaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 23.1]
nakecana bhavantas tu yena nirlakṣaṇā iti | [BKŚS, 10 23.2]
atha cāmaram ujjhitvā sphuṭann iva kutūhalāt | [BKŚS, 10 24.1]
apṛcchad garjitamukhaṃ gomukhaṃ marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 24.2]
yoṣin madhukarī yāsāv upabhoktuṃ vyavasyati | [BKŚS, 10 25.1]
svāmino yauvanamadhu kvāsau kathaya tām iti | [BKŚS, 10 25.2]
tenoktam aryaputrāya bravīmi yadi pṛcchati | [BKŚS, 10 26.1]
na tubhyaṃ sthalamaṇḍūka na hi bhasmani hūyate | [BKŚS, 10 26.2]
atha baddhāñjaliḥ prahvo māvocan marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 27.1]
pṛcchyatāṃ sthiragarvo 'yaṃ prasādaḥ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 10 27.2]
icchatāpi tam ālāpaṃ lajjāṃ bhāvayatā mayā | [BKŚS, 10 28.1]
apratyākhyātakathitaṃ kathayety anumoditam | [BKŚS, 10 28.2]
athānandāśrutimire netre saṃmṛjya gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 29.1]
saṃkāsya śuddhakaṇṭhaś ca ramyām akathayat kathām | [BKŚS, 10 29.2]
athāham aryaputreṇa yauvarājye vibhūṣite | [BKŚS, 10 30.1]
abhivādayituṃ devyau narendrāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ | [BKŚS, 10 30.2]
tatra citraṃ mayā dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭaṃ divyamānuṣaiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 31.1]
varṇakramaviśuddhyā yad rājyam asyeva bhūpateḥ | [BKŚS, 10 31.2]
padmāvatyā ca pṛṣṭo 'haṃ kim asmin putra gomukha | [BKŚS, 10 32.1]
paśyasīti tato devi trayam ity aham uktavān | [BKŚS, 10 32.2]
kiṃ punas trayam ity ukte devyai kathitavān aham | [BKŚS, 10 33.1]
ṛddhiṃ vaḥ śilpināṃ śilpaṃ bahuratnāṃ ca gām iti | [BKŚS, 10 33.2]
atha devyā vihasyoktaṃ cetasyaḥ khalu gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 34.1]
acetasyo hi puruṣaḥ katham evaṃ vaded iti | [BKŚS, 10 34.2]
āsīc ca mama tac chrutvā saṃdehādhyāsitaṃ manaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 35.1]
cetasyaḥ kiṃ nu guṇavān āhosvid doṣavān iti | [BKŚS, 10 35.2]
na ca pṛṣṭā mayā devī sasaṃdehe 'pi cetasi | [BKŚS, 10 36.1]
mā sma budhyata sā bālam acetasyaṃ ca mām iti | [BKŚS, 10 36.2]
apṛṣṭaḥ ko nu kathayec cetasyam iti cintayan | [BKŚS, 10 37.1]
saṃcaran mandiraṃ ahaṃ nirgato rājaveśmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 37.2]
paśyāmi sma rathaṃ yuktaṃ citracāmaramaṇḍanaiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 38.1]
nirantarakhuranyāsaiḥ pārasīkais turaṃgamaiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 38.2]
rathasya prājitā tasya puruṣo māṃ vinītavat | [BKŚS, 10 39.1]
pratodagarbham ādhāya mūrdhany añjalim abravīt | [BKŚS, 10 39.2]
bhartṛdāraka vijñāpyam asmin rājakule vayam | [BKŚS, 10 40.1]
kulakramāgatā bhṛtyā rathavāhanajīvinaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 40.2]
so 'ham ājñāpito rājñā yathaite pṛṣṭhavāhinaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 41.1]
acirād bhavatā rathyāḥ kriyantāṃ turagā iti | [BKŚS, 10 41.2]
mayā caite yathāśakti skandhadāntās tvarāvatā | [BKŚS, 10 42.1]
na tu saṃbhāvayāmy etān kuśalair aparīkṣitān | [BKŚS, 10 42.2]
tad evaṃ ratham āruhya parīkṣyantām amī tvayā | [BKŚS, 10 43.1]
padavākyapramāṇārthacatureṇa āgamā iva | [BKŚS, 10 43.2]
idamādi tataḥ śrutvā kṣaṇam ānamitānanaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 44.1]
upacāro bhaved eṣa satyam evety acintayam | [BKŚS, 10 44.2]
lambakarṇam athāpaśyaṃ vinītaṃ lambaśāṭakam | [BKŚS, 10 45.1]
kāyasthaṃ samaṣīpātraṃ lekhanīkarṇapūrakam | [BKŚS, 10 45.2]
so 'bravīn mahati kleśe pātitāḥ prabhuṇā vayam | [BKŚS, 10 46.1]
sarvathā dhig imāṃ kṣudrāṃ śvavṛttim anujīvinaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 46.2]
pṛthivyāṃ santi yāvantaś cetasyāḥ puruṣottamāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 47.1]
acetasyāś ca kartavyaṃ teṣāṃ lekhyaṃ mayā kila | [BKŚS, 10 47.2]
na caikam api paśyāmi yuktaṃ cetasyalakṣaṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 48.1]
acetasyās tu sakalāṃ kṣobhayanti mahīm iti | [BKŚS, 10 48.2]
pustakadvayahastena tatra caikena bhāṣitam | [BKŚS, 10 49.1]
prasāritāṅgulīkena mām uddiśya sakautukam | [BKŚS, 10 49.2]
āgatyāryākṛtim amuṃ nirdākṣiṇyaṃ na paśyasi | [BKŚS, 10 50.1]
ājīvārthacikitsākaṃ cikitsakam ivādhanam | [BKŚS, 10 50.2]
ayaṃ tāvad acetasyapustakādau niveśyatām | [BKŚS, 10 51.1]
ya evam anunīto 'pi rathaṃ nāroḍhum icchati | [BKŚS, 10 51.2]
aprārthito 'pi yaḥ kaścid ārohati sa likhyatām | [BKŚS, 10 52.1]
cetasyapustakasyādau namaskārād anantaram | [BKŚS, 10 52.2]
tataś cetasyatālobhād dūram utplutya satvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 10 53.1]
mā smānyaḥ kaścid ārohad ity āroham ahaṃ rathaṃ | [BKŚS, 10 53.2]
tena vegavatā gacchann apaśyaṃ gajam agrataḥ | [BKŚS, 10 54.1]
sukhāyamānaṃ madhurair ālāpaiḥ parikarmiṇām | [BKŚS, 10 54.2]
hastyārohaṃ rathāroho vidhārya ratham uktavān | [BKŚS, 10 55.1]
anyato naya mātaṅgaṃ mā cetasyarathaṃ rudhaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 55.2]
tenoktam anyato yātu cetasyādhyāsito rathaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 56.1]
vihantum aham etasya necchām icchāmi dantinaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 56.2]
apravṛttamadasyāsya madaḥ sāntvaiḥ pravartate | [BKŚS, 10 57.1]
icchāyāś cāvighātena tena naḥ kṣamyatām iti | [BKŚS, 10 57.2]
avocam atha yantāraṃ na nāma yadi necchati | [BKŚS, 10 58.1]
ādhoraṇaḥ pathānyena rathaḥ prasthāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 10 58.2]
evaṃ nāmeti coktvā saḥ parivartitavān ratham | [BKŚS, 10 59.1]
cetasyāvāsamadhyena tvāṃ nayāmīti coktavān | [BKŚS, 10 59.2]
āsīc ca mama dīrghāyur ayaṃ bhavatu kuñjaraḥ | [BKŚS, 10 60.1]
rundhatā yena me mārgaṃ cetasyā darśitā iti | [BKŚS, 10 60.2]
paśyāmi sma ca vistīrṇaśilātaladharātalam | [BKŚS, 10 61.1]
mālyabhūṣaṇadhūpādiprāyapaṇyaṃ vaṇikpatham | [BKŚS, 10 61.2]
tam atikramya ramyāgrā harmyamālāḥ saniṣkuṭāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 62.1]
saśarīrā iva nyastā vāstuvidyākṛtāṃ dhiyaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 62.2]
utkaṭākāracaritāḥ samadāḥ pramadāḥ kvacit | [BKŚS, 10 63.1]
tādṛśān eva puruṣān sevamānāḥ parāṅmukhān | [BKŚS, 10 63.2]
pṛṣṭhato 'nunayantaṃ ca yuvānaṃ yuvatiṃ kvacit | [BKŚS, 10 64.1]
tayā nirbhartsyamānaṃ ca vākyair madhuradāruṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 10 64.2]
ayi ballavakāpehi kiṃ mā chupasi durbhagām | [BKŚS, 10 65.1]
bahuballavakacchuptāṃ chupaballavikām iti | [BKŚS, 10 65.2]
calayantīṃ kvacit kāṃcid vipañcīm añcitāṅgulim | [BKŚS, 10 66.1]
kāṃcit koṇaparāmarśaśiñjānaparivādinīm | [BKŚS, 10 66.2]
iti saṃcaramāṇo 'haṃ rathena mṛdugāminā | [BKŚS, 10 67.1]
paṭhantīḥ paṭṭikā vyagrāḥ paśyāmi sma kumārikāḥ | [BKŚS, 10 67.2]
kaḥ punaḥ syād ayaṃ grantha iti śrotuṃ mayecchatā | [BKŚS, 10 68.1]
dūrāt prahitakarṇena sphuṭam ākarṇitaṃ yathā | [BKŚS, 10 68.2]
sametya pūrvaṃ na svapyāt suptaṃ ca na parityajet | [BKŚS, 10 69.1]
prāṇāpānau ca yatnena samaṃ saṃdhārayed iti | [BKŚS, 10 69.2]
āsīc ca mama kā etā viṭaśāstram adhīyate | [BKŚS, 10 70.1]
manye sārathinopāyair ahaṃ veśaṃ praveśitaḥ | [BKŚS, 10 70.2]
kāmadevālayaṃ cānyaḥ kurvan ko 'pi pradakṣiṇam | [BKŚS, 10 71.1]

yā svābhāvikarūpakhaṇḍitajagadrūpābhimānā priyā śṛṅgārādirasaprayogasubhagā jāyeta sā kīdṛśī | [BKŚS, 10 274.1]
ity adhyāsitacetasā katham api prakrāntayā cintayā paryaṅkāṅkavivartinārtatanunā nītā triyāmā mayā | [BKŚS, 10 274.2]
{BKŚS, 11}
atha nāgarakākāras tadākārasuhṛdvṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 1.1]
saṃprasthāpya manaḥ pūrvaṃ nṛpāsthānam agām aham | [BKŚS, 11 1.2]
tatra puṣpakasaṃsthānamañcasthānaṃ mahīpatim | [BKŚS, 11 2.1]
praṇamya tadanujñātaṃ mañcāntaram aseviṣi | [BKŚS, 11 2.2]
raṅgāṅgaṇam athālokya kuśalaprekṣakākulam | [BKŚS, 11 3.1]
nṛtyācāryau namaskṛtya mahīpālam avocatām | [BKŚS, 11 3.2]
rājann upāntanepathye bhṛtye vaḥ samupāgate | [BKŚS, 11 4.1]
draṣṭum icchatha yāṃ pūrvam ājñāpayata tām iti | [BKŚS, 11 4.2]
so 'bravīn nṛtyagītādikalāśāstraviśāradaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 5.1]
gomukhaḥ sa ca yām āha sā pūrvaṃ nṛtyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 5.2]
tābhyām āgatya pṛṣṭaś ca kā pūrvaṃ nṛtyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 6.1]
sa suyāmunadanteti tadupādhyāyam ādiśat | [BKŚS, 11 6.2]
tatas tasyāṃ pranṛttāyāṃ pranṛttā nṛtyavedinaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 7.1]
raṅgaśeṣas tu niśceṣṭaḥ suṣuptāvasthāṃ gataḥ | [BKŚS, 11 7.2]
pratyāhṛtya tataś ceto hriyamāṇaṃ balāt tayā | [BKŚS, 11 8.1]
manonetrāṅgasaṃcārair anāhāryair acintayam | [BKŚS, 11 8.2]
nānugantum alaṃ rambhā nṛttam asyāḥ samenakā | [BKŚS, 11 9.1]
kuta eva parājetum abalā bālikā priyā | [BKŚS, 11 9.2]
rājahaṃsaḥ pipāsāndhaḥ prāptaḥ paṅkajinīṃ yathā | [BKŚS, 11 10.1]
paṅkāvilajalāṃ paśyet tathādhyāsam ahaṃ priyām | [BKŚS, 11 10.2]
avocaṃ gomukhaṃ cedaṃ jīyamānāṃ priyām aham | [BKŚS, 11 11.1]
aśaktaḥ prekṣituṃ tena raṅgān nirgamyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 11.2]
tenoktam icchayā gantum āgantuṃ vā na labhyate | [BKŚS, 11 12.1]
vatsarājakulāt tena muhūrtaṃ sthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 12.2]
viratāyāṃ tatas tasyāṃ purāṇārkarucāv iva | [BKŚS, 11 13.1]
jīvalokam iva jyotsnā priyā raṅgam arañjayat | [BKŚS, 11 13.2]
apṛcchaṃ gomukhaṃ cāsāṃ katamā padmadevikā | [BKŚS, 11 14.1]
mudrikālatikā ceti sa vihasyedam abravīt | [BKŚS, 11 14.2]
kīrtikāntyor iyaṃ madhye yā lakṣmīr iva rājate | [BKŚS, 11 15.1]
eṣā naḥ svāminī devī vāmato mudrikālatā | [BKŚS, 11 15.2]
na ceyaṃ śakyate jetum alaṃ vaḥ śaṅkayā yataḥ | [BKŚS, 11 16.1]
dṛṣṭā kena śarajjyotsnā khadyotaprabhayā jitā | [BKŚS, 11 16.2]
mayā vijayamāneyam anekaṃ nartakīśatam | [BKŚS, 11 17.1]
dṛṣṭā saṃbhāvayāmy asyās tena nṛttaguṇān iti | [BKŚS, 11 17.2]
gomukhābhimukho yāvat sāvadhānaṃ śṛṇomy aham | [BKŚS, 11 18.1]
tāvaj jaya jayety uccair vimuktaḥ prekṣakair dhvaniḥ | [BKŚS, 11 18.2]
raṅgād dṛṣṭā ca niryāntī bādhyamāneva sā mayā | [BKŚS, 11 19.1]
dainyavepathuvaivarṇyaviṣādaiḥ sahajair iva | [BKŚS, 11 19.2]
tato visarjitāsthānaṃ namaskṛtya mahīpatim | [BKŚS, 11 20.1]
svam āvāsaṃ vrajāmi sma kāntācintāpuraḥsaraḥ | [BKŚS, 11 20.2]
gomukhaṃ cābravaṃ kasmān mām idānīm upekṣase | [BKŚS, 11 21.1]
na hy ādeśam upekṣante tvādṛśā mādṛśām iti | [BKŚS, 11 21.2]
tenoktam aparaḥ kaścit pratyayārthaṃ visarjyatām | [BKŚS, 11 22.1]
śraddhāsyati na me vākyaṃ vipralabdhā hi sā mayā | [BKŚS, 11 22.2]
eṣām anyatamaṃ yāhi gṛhītveti mayodite | [BKŚS, 11 23.1]
marubhūtika evātra yogya ityayam uktavān | [BKŚS, 11 23.2]
ayaṃ hariśikhas tāvan nītyā vakragatiḥ kṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 24.1]
apāyaśatam ālokya kadācij jālam ālikhet | [BKŚS, 11 24.2]
kathaṃ kaṣṭatame bālo vyasanānāṃ catuṣṭaye | [BKŚS, 11 25.1]
yatpradhānastriyas tatra rājaputraḥ pravartyate | [BKŚS, 11 25.2]
evam aṅgulibhaṅgena vicāryālīkapaṇḍitaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 26.1]
vihanyād api naḥ kāryaṃ tasmād eṣa na yujyate | [BKŚS, 11 26.2]
tapantako 'pi bālatvān mūḍhaḥ śūnyamukho yataḥ | [BKŚS, 11 27.1]
tasmād evaṃvidhe kārye niyogaṃ nāyam arhati | [BKŚS, 11 27.2]
vikramaikarasatvāc ca samartho marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 28.1]
abhyastasāhasas tasmād eṣa prasthāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 28.2]
tatas tau sahitau yātau cirāt tu marubhūtikam | [BKŚS, 11 29.1]
prāptaṃ hariśikho 'pṛcchat kiṃ vṛttaṃ bhavator iti | [BKŚS, 11 29.2]
tenoktam āvayos tāvad veśamadhyena gacchatoḥ | [BKŚS, 11 30.1]
āyāty abhimukhī yaiva saiva yāti parāṅmukhī | [BKŚS, 11 30.2]
bhañjantī cāṅgulīḥ krodhād vadaty āraktalocanā | [BKŚS, 11 31.1]
na spraṣṭavyo na saṃbhāṣyo gomukhaḥ pāpavān iti | [BKŚS, 11 31.2]
kruddhadauvārikākrāntahāṭakastambhatoraṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 11 32.1]
kakṣyādvāraiḥ praviṣṭau svaḥ sthānam aryasutāsthitam | [BKŚS, 11 32.2]
tatraikā dārikāvocad dārikāḥ paśyatādbhutam | [BKŚS, 11 33.1]
dhūrtenānena cāturyād gomayaṃ pāyasīkṛtam | [BKŚS, 11 33.2]
aparādho 'yam etāvat sarpaḥ prāṇaharaḥ kṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 34.1]
tam eva paśyatānena vācālena guṇīkṛtam | [BKŚS, 11 34.2]
vandamāno yadā kopāt svāminyā nābhinanditaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 35.1]
saṃbhrāntaś ca vilakṣaś ca tadā tām āha gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 35.2]
manye niṣkāraṇaṃ kopaṃ devyāḥ ko nāma mādṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 36.1]
sevakaḥ paricittajñaḥ svāminaṃ kopayed iti | [BKŚS, 11 36.2]
tathānyatamayā kopāt tālavṛntabhṛtoditam | [BKŚS, 11 37.1]
kathaṃ niṣkāraṇo nāma kim idaṃ laghu kāraṇam | [BKŚS, 11 37.2]
utkaṇṭhādarśam icchantī kasyāpi cirakāṅkṣitam | [BKŚS, 11 38.1]
tvayā nartayatā kāntā kim iyaṃ sukham āsitā | [BKŚS, 11 38.2]
athavā tad gataṃ nāma svāmī kiṃ karaṇaṃ tvayā | [BKŚS, 11 39.1]
paśyann abhimukhaṃ prītyā sa tathā vimukhīkṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 39.2]
bhavān paśyatu vā mā vā tvadvidheyo yuvā janaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 40.1]
tvam icchasi jayaṃ yasyāḥ kim asau na parājitā | [BKŚS, 11 40.2]
tato bhiyāvanamitaṃ mukham unnamya gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 41.1]
uktavān paśyatānarthaṃ doṣo bhūto guṇo 'pi naḥ | [BKŚS, 11 41.2]
yadi prāk svāminī nṛtyet tayā rājā sutoṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 42.1]
kadācid itarāṃ naiva paśyed vṛttakutūhalaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 42.2]
tadā ca guṇavidveṣī jano vaktā bhaved yathā | [BKŚS, 11 43.1]
pakṣapātān narendreṇa dṛṣṭā madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 11 43.2]
itarā yadi nṛtyantī tena dṛṣṭā bhavet tadā | [BKŚS, 11 44.1]
norvaśīm api paśyet saḥ kuto madanamañjukām | [BKŚS, 11 44.2]
prītyā yaś conmukhaḥ paśyan kṛtaḥ svāmī parāṅmukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 45.1]
mayopāyaḥ prayukto 'sau katham ity avadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 11 45.2]
na suyāmunadantāyāḥ śakyaḥ kartuṃ parābhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 46.1]
kṛtānukaraṇaiḥ sākṣād bharatenāpi nṛtyatā | [BKŚS, 11 46.2]
aryaputre tu vimukhe yuṣmābhiḥ sā parājitā | [BKŚS, 11 47.1]
sahajair iva vaivarṇyavivādasvedavepanaiḥ | [BKŚS, 11 47.2]
tena bravīmi sevāpi yāti yady aparādhatām | [BKŚS, 11 48.1]
bhaktyārādhitabhartāraḥ sevakā hanta duḥsthitāḥ | [BKŚS, 11 48.2]
athavā sāparādho 'pi dūtaḥ saṃmānam arhati | [BKŚS, 11 49.1]
saṃdeśaśravaṇāt tena saṃmānayata mām iti | [BKŚS, 11 49.2]
atha sātra parāvṛtya prasādaviśadānanā | [BKŚS, 11 50.1]
īṣadvihasitajyotsnā salilasnapitādharā | [BKŚS, 11 50.2]
ayi candramukhaṃ mā sma gomukhaṃ puruṣaṃ vada | [BKŚS, 11 51.1]
na hi vatseśvarāsannāḥ śrūyante strīsuhṛddruhaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 51.2]
anālāpena yac cāsi kṣaṇam āyāsito mayā | [BKŚS, 11 52.1]
tat kṣamasva na hi svāsthā bādhante tvādṛśām iti | [BKŚS, 11 52.2]
tataḥ sā gomukhenoktā draṣṭum icchati vaḥ priyaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 53.1]
saṃdehaś ced iyaṃ mudrā tadīyā dṛśyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 53.2]
tayoktaṃ kumbhakārāṇāṃ koṭir vasati vaḥ pure | [BKŚS, 11 54.1]
koṭiḥ kim iti nānītā na hi te kṣīṇamṛttikāḥ | [BKŚS, 11 54.2]
tenoktaṃ kena vānītā mudrā vā mṛttikāmayī | [BKŚS, 11 55.1]
na hy ārabhyamahākāryāḥ pramādyanti sacetasaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 55.2]
yaugandharāyaṇasutaḥ priyaṃ mitraṃ priyasya vaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 56.1]
svāminā preṣitaḥ prītyā dṛśyatāṃ marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 56.2]
atha devī namaskṛtya prītā vijñāpitā mayā | [BKŚS, 11 57.1]
yat saṃdiśati naḥ svāmī yuṣmabhyaṃ tan niśāmyatām | [BKŚS, 11 57.2]
preritaḥ tvām ahaṃ draṣṭuṃ yena lakṣmīm ivālasaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 58.1]
krīḍatāsmadvidhair eṣa vilakṣaḥ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 58.2]
prasthitāyāṃ tato devyām āha māṃ padmadevikā | [BKŚS, 11 59.1]
iyaṃ prasādhyate yāvat tāvad āstāṃ bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 11 59.2]
devyā saha praviśyāntar muhūrtād iva sā tataḥ | [BKŚS, 11 60.1]
āha prakṛṣṭapramudā praphullanayanotpalā | [BKŚS, 11 60.2]
mayā kaliṅgasenāyai tayā gatvā rumaṇvate | [BKŚS, 11 61.1]
tenāpi bhūmipataye vṛttānto 'yaṃ niveditaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 61.2]
tenoktaṃ kim ihākhyeyaṃ taruṇo nanu dārakaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 62.1]
jīvalokasukhāny eṣa tasmād anubhavatv iti | [BKŚS, 11 62.2]
seyaṃ rājñābhyanujñātā guruṇā manmathena ca | [BKŚS, 11 63.1]
iyam āyāti te paścād yātu tāvad bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 11 63.2]
atha praviśya saṃbhrāntā pratīhārī nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 11 64.1]
sayāno gomukhaḥ prāha laghu śrāvaya mām iti | [BKŚS, 11 64.2]
mayoktaṃ gomukhas tāvad ekākī praviśatv iti | [BKŚS, 11 65.1]
sa praviśyoktavān dvāre devī kiṃ vidhṛteti mām | [BKŚS, 11 65.2]
ajñātapramadāsaṅgam ākulībhūtamānasam | [BKŚS, 11 66.1]
kuru nāgarakaṃ tāvat tvaṃ mām ity aham uktavān | [BKŚS, 11 66.2]
tenoktaṃ yuddhavelāyāṃ damyante turagā iti | [BKŚS, 11 67.1]
yad etad ghuṣyate loke tad etat tathyatāṃ gatam | [BKŚS, 11 67.2]
na nāgarakatāṃ prāptum upadeśena śakyate | [BKŚS, 11 68.1]
iyaṃ hi mokṣavidyeva prayogāvṛttisādhanā | [BKŚS, 11 68.2]
saṃkṣepatas tu vakṣyāmi yad yad devī kariṣyati | [BKŚS, 11 69.1]
tat tad evānukuryās tvaṃ dakṣo hi labhate śriyam | [BKŚS, 11 69.2]
anuśiṣya sa mām evaṃ niryāyānīya ca priyām | [BKŚS, 11 70.1]
sukhaṃ supyāstam ity uktvā yathāsvaṃ sasuhṛdgataḥ | [BKŚS, 11 70.2]
tataḥ praviśya dayitā mām ardhākṣṇā niraikṣata | [BKŚS, 11 71.1]
kṛtaṃ tathaiva ca mayā vanditena ca vanditā | [BKŚS, 11 71.2]
sarvathā yad yad evāham anayā kāritas tadā | [BKŚS, 11 72.1]
tad evānukaromi sma nartanācāryaśiṣyavat | [BKŚS, 11 72.2]
atha buddhvānukūlaṃ mām iyam anvarthavedinam | [BKŚS, 11 73.1]
smitvā sotkamparomāñcaṃ gāḍham aṅgam apīḍayat | [BKŚS, 11 73.2]
tato 'ham anapekṣyaiva tatkṛtānukṛtakramam | [BKŚS, 11 74.1]
aśarīrasya kasyāpi gato bhūtasya vaśyatām | [BKŚS, 11 74.2]
strīpuṃsatām āgatayor anabhipretanidrayoḥ | [BKŚS, 11 75.1]
pradoṣa eva kṣaṇadā kṣīṇā kṣaṇavad āvayoḥ | [BKŚS, 11 75.2]

dineṣu mama samprāptaḥ senānīr idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 11 77.2]

tenaiva sahitā yūyaṃ gantāraḥ śanakair iti | [BKŚS, 11 81.2]

abravīd gomukho vakti kiṃ mayātaḥ prayojanam | [BKŚS, 11 93.2]

tato hariśikhenoktaḥ kruddhena marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 95.1]
preryamāṇaṃ galāṣṭrābhiḥ śīghram ānaya taṃ śaṭham | [BKŚS, 11 95.2]
