athavālaṃ pralāpena mahīpālaṃ tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 100.1]
vijñāpayatu tenāsya dattaḥ pūrvam ayaṃ varaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 100.2]
aprasaṅge 'pi bhavatā kāryā vijñāpinā mayi | [BKŚS, 11 101.1]
siddhiṃ yāsyati cāvaśyaṃ mā sma śaṅkāṃ karod iti | [BKŚS, 11 101.2]
itīmām anukūlābhir vāgbhir āśvāsya gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 102.1]
mātur evānayan mūlaṃ prāviśāma tataḥ purīm | [BKŚS, 11 102.2]
kumāravaṭakāsthena mayānūktas tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 103.1]
gomukhena yad ākhyātaṃ tat kāryaṃ sādhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 103.2]
tapantakas tu sāsphoṭam idaṃ siddhim iti bruvan | [BKŚS, 11 104.1]
gatvā rājakulaṃ tasmād āgatyedam abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 11 104.2]
rājapādair ahaṃ pṛṣṭas tāta kiṃ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 105.1]
śālīnena mayāpy uktaṃ modako dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 11 105.2]
evaṃ mālāphalādīni niḥsārāṇi tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 11 106.1]
yācate sma prahīṇatvād gatvā gatvā mahīpatim | [BKŚS, 11 106.2]
iti saśarīrayā kṣaṇam iva kṣaṇadāḥ kṣapayan saha viśarīrayā dayitayā virasān divasān | [BKŚS, 11 107.1]
dinarajanīvihāraviparītam aham caritai rathacaraṇāhvayasya caritāni viḍambitavān | [BKŚS, 11 107.2]
{BKŚS, 12}
atha māṃ kṛtakartavyaṃ sukhāsīnam aharmukhe | [BKŚS, 12 1.1]
vādī jita ivācchāyas trapayā gomukho 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 12 1.2]
aham aryasutāṃ nītvā gṛhaṃ svagṛham āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 12 2.1]
tato 'pi vandituṃ devyau narendrāntaḥpuraṃ gataḥ | [BKŚS, 12 2.2]
vanditā ca vihasyāha devī padmāvatī yathā | [BKŚS, 12 3.1]
kiṃkāraṇaṃ vadhūr adya nāsmān āyāti vanditum | [BKŚS, 12 3.2]
bhrātrā te kiṃ na muktaiva na vādyāpi vibudhyate | [BKŚS, 12 4.1]
kopitā vā bhaved bhartrā śiṣṭā duścaritair iti | [BKŚS, 12 4.2]
athāgāt hatoraskā krandantī padmadevikā | [BKŚS, 12 5.1]
nāsti naḥ svāminīty uktvā devyor nipatitā puraḥ | [BKŚS, 12 5.2]
tato devyau tataḥ śeṣam aśeṣam avarodhanam | [BKŚS, 12 6.1]
rājā ca śrutavṛttāntaḥ sāsthāno dhairyam atyajat | [BKŚS, 12 6.2]
tataḥ prāpyācirāt saṃjñāṃ māgadhyā padmadevikā | [BKŚS, 12 7.1]
kathaṃ jānāsi nāstīti pṛṣṭācaṣṭa niśāmyatām | [BKŚS, 12 7.2]
yathaiva gomukhenāsau svam āvāsaṃ praveśitā | [BKŚS, 12 8.1]
tathaiva kagiti ghrāto gandho 'smābhir amānuṣaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 8.2]
akasmāc ca kṣaṇaṃ nidrāṃ gacchāmaḥ pratibudhya ca | [BKŚS, 12 9.1]
śūnyām īkṣāmahe śayyām aśrīkāṃ nalinīm iva | [BKŚS, 12 9.2]
tato hā heti vikruśya samūrchāḥ kṣaṇam āsmahe | [BKŚS, 12 10.1]
na kvacic ca vicinvatyaḥ paśyāmaḥ svāminīm iti | [BKŚS, 12 10.2]
kaliṅgasenayā tv atra śokagadgadayoditam | [BKŚS, 12 11.1]
idaṃ tad āgataṃ manya durvidyādharaceṣṭitam | [BKŚS, 12 11.2]
bālikām aham ādāya pūrvaṃ madanamañcukām | [BKŚS, 12 12.1]
harmyāgre krīḍayāmi sma candrikāsaṅgaśītale | [BKŚS, 12 12.2]
ehi vidyādharā ehi gṛhāṇemāṃ surūpikām | [BKŚS, 12 13.1]
ekām eva mayā labdhāṃ sutāṃ durlabhikām iti | [BKŚS, 12 13.2]
tataś carmāsikeyūrahārādikarabhāsuraḥ | [BKŚS, 12 14.1]
avātarad divaḥ ko 'pi divyagandhasragambaraḥ | [BKŚS, 12 14.2]
dūrād eva ca māṃ bhītāṃ mā bhaiṣīr iti sāntvayan | [BKŚS, 12 15.1]
gambhīradhvanivitrastatanayām idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 12 15.2]
yadi mahyam iyaṃ dattā satyena tanayā tvayā | [BKŚS, 12 16.1]
tato muñca nayāmy enāṃ nyāsabhūtā hi kanyakā | [BKŚS, 12 16.2]
nāmnā mānasavego 'haṃ vidyādharagaṇādhipaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 17.1]
sarvavijñeyavijñānamanojvalitadhīr iti | [BKŚS, 12 17.2]
anicchantī tatas tasya saṃnidhau ciram āsitum | [BKŚS, 12 18.1]
prayatnād dhairyam ādhāya pragalbheva tam abravam | [BKŚS, 12 18.2]
arhaty avaśyam eveyam īdṛśī tvādṛśaṃ patim | [BKŚS, 12 19.1]
na punar dīyate tāvad bālikā śaiśavād iti | [BKŚS, 12 19.2]
atha mām abhivādyāsāv ulkāsaṃghātabhāsuraḥ | [BKŚS, 12 20.1]
dṛśyamāno mahāvegaḥ kṣaṇenāntarhito 'bhavat | [BKŚS, 12 20.2]
tena bravīmi tenādya tat smṛtvā kṣudrabuddhinā | [BKŚS, 12 21.1]
vidyādharādhamenāsau nītā yadi bhaved iti | [BKŚS, 12 21.2]
sarvathā dṛśyate neha devī madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 12 22.1]
yad atrānantaraṃ nyāyyaṃ tad anuṣṭhīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 22.2]
tataḥ samutpatann eva śokaḥ krodhena māmakaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 23.1]
preritaḥ pavaneneva prabalena balāhakaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 23.2]
strītaskara durācāra mūḍha mānasavegaka | [BKŚS, 12 24.1]
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha kva yāsīti prālapaṃ gaganonmukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 24.2]
yugapat krodhaśokābhyāṃ śoṣito 'haṃ krameṇa ca | [BKŚS, 12 25.1]
yathānilatuṣārābhyāṃ śiśire kamalākaraḥ | [BKŚS, 12 25.2]
gomukhas tu nṛpāhutaḥ pratyāgatyedam abravīt | [BKŚS, 12 26.1]
kim etad iti pṛṣṭena vṛttānto 'yaṃ mayoditaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 26.2]
tataḥ saṃbhramavisrastam ākarṣann uttarāmbaram | [BKŚS, 12 27.1]
viṣādākulito rājā prasthito yuṣmadantikam | [BKŚS, 12 27.2]
antare ca rumaṇvantam āha keyaṃ pramāditā | [BKŚS, 12 28.1]
sarvathā khyāpitaṃ lokair bhavatāṃ nītikauśalam | [BKŚS, 12 28.2]
yuktaṃ tadā yadālocya mahat sīdat prayojanam | [BKŚS, 12 29.1]
vipralabdho 'smi yuṣmābhir devyā vāsavadattayā | [BKŚS, 12 29.2]
adhunā dhriyamāṇe 'pi samarthasacive mayi | [BKŚS, 12 30.1]
apanītā vadhūḥ kasmād bālān mama sutād iti | [BKŚS, 12 30.2]
sa tam āha nivartadhvam alaṃ tatra gatena vaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 31.1]
yuṣmān dṛṣṭvā hi sa śiśuḥ prāṇān api parityajet | [BKŚS, 12 31.2]
ājñāpayatha māṃ yac ca yac ca vijñāpayāmi vaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 32.1]
āsīnān āsane tena nivṛtya sthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 32.2]
upaviṣṭāya cācaṣṭa sphuṭaṃ divyena sā hṛtā | [BKŚS, 12 33.1]
anāthāpi na vaḥ kācit kenacit paribhūyate | [BKŚS, 12 33.2]
yāvad antaḥpurāṭavyau yāvac ca gṛhapakṣiṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 34.1]
nāsty asau yo na cāsmābhir īkṣitaś cāracakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 12 34.2]
ākāśe tu na me prajñā kramate divyagocare | [BKŚS, 12 35.1]
tena vidyādhareṇāsau hṛteti hṛdaye mama | [BKŚS, 12 35.2]
athavā bhavatūdyāne yuvarājaḥ parīkṣatām | [BKŚS, 12 36.1]
kadācit kupitā bhartre tatrāsīta vadhūr iti | [BKŚS, 12 36.2]
kupitānāṃ hi bhartṛbhyaḥ śrūyante kulayoṣitām | [BKŚS, 12 37.1]
sādhubhiḥ kathyamānāni pañca sthānāni tad yathā | [BKŚS, 12 37.2]
śvaśrūbhrātṛnanāndṛṇāṃ bhartṛmitrasya vā gṛham | [BKŚS, 12 38.1]
duṣṭasaṃcāraśūnyāni mandiropavanāni vā | [BKŚS, 12 38.2]
atrāntare kathitavān ākhyānaṃ marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 39.1]
prastāve yan mayā pūrvaṃ śrutaṃ tad avadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 12 39.2]
aṣṭāvakrasya duhitā sāvitrī nāma kanyakā | [BKŚS, 12 40.1]
āsīd yā caritākāraiḥ sāvitrīm atiricyate | [BKŚS, 12 40.2]
aṣṭāvakram ayāciṣṭa kadācid ṛṣir aṅgirāḥ | [BKŚS, 12 41.1]
brahmann akṛtadāro 'smi sutā me dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 41.2]
so 'bravīd bhavataḥ ko 'nyas trailokye 'pi varo varaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 42.1]
kiṃ tu datteyam anyasmai kṣamatāṃ bhagavān iti | [BKŚS, 12 42.2]
tasya bhrātā vṛṣo nāma sa cāṅgirasam abravīt | [BKŚS, 12 43.1]
amṛtā nāma duhitā mama sā gṛhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 43.2]
pariṇīya tu tāṃ kanyām amṛtām amṛtopamām | [BKŚS, 12 44.1]
ātmānam aṅgirā mene pītāmṛtam ivāmṛtam | [BKŚS, 12 44.2]
sā kadācit kathaṃcit taṃ kāraṇe 'lpe 'pi pīḍitā | [BKŚS, 12 45.1]
upālabdhavatī nātham ṛṣiputrasya vallabhā | [BKŚS, 12 45.2]
cakṣūraktena bhavatā sāvitrī svayam arthitā | [BKŚS, 12 46.1]
ahaṃ tv anicchate tubhyaṃ pitrā dattā balād iti | [BKŚS, 12 46.2]
nānāvidhaiḥ sa śapathair amṛtāṃ parisāntvayan | [BKŚS, 12 47.1]
kaṃcid abhyanayat kālam ekadāstaṃgate ravau | [BKŚS, 12 47.2]
paścāt sandhyām upāsīnam āsīnaṃ maunadhāriṇam | [BKŚS, 12 48.1]
apṛcchad amṛtāgatya kiṃ dhyāyati bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 12 48.2]
tena vanditasaṃdhyena cirād uktaṃ nanu priye | [BKŚS, 12 49.1]
devīṃ vihāya sāvitrīṃ kim anyac cintayāmy aham | [BKŚS, 12 49.2]
atha sā śrutam ity uktvā svasminn āśramapādape | [BKŚS, 12 50.1]
devatābhyo namaskṛtya śarīram udalambayat | [BKŚS, 12 50.2]
ākṛṣṭakaṇṭhapāśā ca puraḥ praikṣata devatām | [BKŚS, 12 51.1]
vidyutpiṅgajaṭābhārāṃ sākṣamālākamaṇḍalum | [BKŚS, 12 51.2]
tato dantaprabhājālaprabhāsitatapovanā | [BKŚS, 12 52.1]
devatāvocad amṛtām amṛteneva siñcatī | [BKŚS, 12 52.2]
putri mā sma tyaja prāṇān dustyajān dharmasādhanān | [BKŚS, 12 53.1]
straiṇam ajñānam āśritya saṃtuṣṭo hi patis tvayā | [BKŚS, 12 53.2]
nāṣṭāvakrasya duhitā sāvitrī tena cintitā | [BKŚS, 12 54.1]
kiṃtv ahaṃ brahmarudrādisaptalokanamaskṛtā | [BKŚS, 12 54.2]
sarvathā matprasādāt te putri putro bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 12 55.1]
balena tapasā yasya na samāno bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 12 55.2]
iti dattvā varaṃ tasyai sāvitrī divam āśrayat | [BKŚS, 12 56.1]
amṛtāpi gatāśaṅkā bhartrā saha sameyuṣī | [BKŚS, 12 56.2]
tena bravīmi kupitā kadācid amṛteva sā | [BKŚS, 12 57.1]
udyānaṃ praviśet tatra svayam anviṣyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 57.2]
athāhaṃ śibikārūḍhaḥ prasthito veśam asmṛtiḥ | [BKŚS, 12 58.1]
cakṣuścetoharākārāḥ paśyan veśyāḥ samūhaśaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 58.2]
āsīc ca mama devībhyāṃ prayogo 'yam anuṣṭhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 59.1]
api nāmāsya kasyāṃcit striyāṃ bhāvo bhaved iti | [BKŚS, 12 59.2]
tadāyaṃ mohasaṃkalpo na hi saṃkalpajanmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 60.1]
rater anyāsu saṃkalpaḥ pramadāsu pravartate | [BKŚS, 12 60.2]
tataḥ saṃkalpayann evam acandrikam ivāmbaram | [BKŚS, 12 61.1]
kāntāmātur gṛhaṃ kāntaṃ kāntāśūnyam upāgamam | [BKŚS, 12 61.2]
prakāśān aprakāśāṃś ca pradeśān bahuśo bahūn | [BKŚS, 12 62.1]
anviṣyanto bhramāma sma na cāpaśyāma tatra tām | [BKŚS, 12 62.2]
gomukhoddiṣṭamārgaś ca praviśya gṛhakānanam | [BKŚS, 12 63.1]
pṛcchāmi sma priyāvārttāṃ sākṣiśākhāmṛgāṇḍajān | [BKŚS, 12 63.2]
kebhyaścit kupitaḥ śāpān kebhyaścid vitaran karān | [BKŚS, 12 64.1]
viḍambayann aśāstrajñam ity utkaṭarasaṃ naṭam | [BKŚS, 12 64.2]
athopagamya tvaritaḥ prahṛṣṭo marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 65.1]
aryaputrāryaduhitā mayā dṛṣṭety abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 12 65.2]
tatas tasya parāmṛjya pāṇinā vikasanmukham | [BKŚS, 12 66.1]
api satyam idaṃ saumya syāt krīḍety aham abravam | [BKŚS, 12 66.2]
so 'bravīt satyam apy etat krīḍā yaiṣātiharṣajā | [BKŚS, 12 67.1]
asatye hy atra yā krīḍā tad unmattavijṛmbhitam | [BKŚS, 12 67.2]
athavālaṃ vimarśena mahābhyudayavairiṇā | [BKŚS, 12 68.1]
tvaritaṃ gamyatāṃ yasmān nārtaḥ kālam udīkṣate | [BKŚS, 12 68.2]
paśyāmi sma tato gacchann aśokaśiśum agrataḥ | [BKŚS, 12 69.1]
raktaṃ kusumasaṃghātam ayam ā bhūmipallavam | [BKŚS, 12 69.2]
akāle kim aśokasya kusumānīti cintayan | [BKŚS, 12 70.1]
tasya skandhe hriyālīnam apaśyaṃ prāṇadāyinīm | [BKŚS, 12 70.2]
āsīc ca mama kiṃ citraṃ yat pādasparśadohadaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 71.1]
sadyaḥ kusumito 'śokaḥ prāpya sarvāṅgasaṃgatim | [BKŚS, 12 71.2]
idam atra mahaccitraṃ yadālokitam etayā | [BKŚS, 12 72.1]
vanadevatayodyānaṃ sakalaṃ na vijṛmbhitam | [BKŚS, 12 72.2]
sarvathācetanā vṛkṣāḥ kāntāyā darśane sati | [BKŚS, 12 73.1]
subhage nirvikāratvād aṅgāratuṣabhasmavat | [BKŚS, 12 73.2]
athāliṅgitum ārabdhaḥ sānurāgam ahaṃ ca tām | [BKŚS, 12 74.1]
tayā cāṅgāni saṃhṛtya mā tāvad iti vāritaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 74.2]
tataḥ prasarabhaṅgena vilakṣam upalakṣya mām | [BKŚS, 12 75.1]
sābravīd aparodho 'yam aryaputreṇa mṛṣyatām | [BKŚS, 12 75.2]
ārādhitavatī yakṣam ahaṃ kanyā satī yathā | [BKŚS, 12 76.1]
aryaputrasya bhūyāsaṃ dayitā paricārikā | [BKŚS, 12 76.2]
tubhyaṃ kārye ca saṃsiddhe śamīlājasugandhinā | [BKŚS, 12 77.1]
pānaṃ hastena dāsyāmi prasīdatu bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 12 77.2]
sa ca tasya prasādān me yātaḥ siddhiṃ manorathaḥ | [BKŚS, 12 78.1]
āyācitaṃ tu yakṣāya na mayā pratiyācitam | [BKŚS, 12 78.2]
tenāhaṃ pānaśauṇḍena nītā dhanapateḥ sabhām | [BKŚS, 12 79.1]
vṛttāntaḥ kathitaś cāyam athokto dhanadena saḥ | [BKŚS, 12 79.2]
āyācitam iyaṃ tubhyam acireṇaiva dāsyati | [BKŚS, 12 80.1]
nītvā samarpaya kṣipraṃ dārakāya vadhūm iti | [BKŚS, 12 80.2]
tena cāham ihānītā gaganāgamanāc ca me | [BKŚS, 12 81.1]
śarīraṃ paruṣībhūtaṃ vāritā stha tato mayā | [BKŚS, 12 81.2]
tasmai yakṣāya yuṣmābhiḥ sa me saṃpādyatām iti | [BKŚS, 12 82.2]
athāsyai gaṇikādhyakṣo rājādeśaṃ nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 12 83.1]
adyārabhya kulastrītvaṃ bhavatīnāṃ bhavatv iti | [BKŚS, 12 83.2]
taṃ cākarṇya mahāmanoratham idaṃ pūrṇaṃ cirāt kāṅkṣitaṃ naiva prītivikāsihārihasitaṃ dhatte sma kāntāmukham | [BKŚS, 12 84.1]
yācñāvṛttikadarthitair bahubhir apy āptair na hi prārthakāḥ prītiṃ yānti tathā yathā tanubhir apy arthaiḥ sukhābhyāgataiḥ | [BKŚS, 12 84.2]
{BKŚS, 13}
tato divasam āsitvā kāntāmātur ahaṃ gṛhe | [BKŚS, 13 1.1]
priyāṃ navavadhūveṣāṃ pradoṣe pariṇītavān | [BKŚS, 13 1.2]
prasādād aryapādānāṃ kulastrītvam upāgatām | [BKŚS, 13 2.1]
tām ādāya svam āvāsaṃ pravṛttotsavam āgamam | [BKŚS, 13 2.2]
tatra sā sadhanādhyakṣaṃ taṃ yakṣaṃ kusumādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 13 3.1]
abhyarcya pānadānena sudustoṣam atoṣayat | [BKŚS, 13 3.2]
padmarāgamayīṃ śuktiṃ padmarāgadravatviṣaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 4.1]
ādāya madhunaḥ pūrṇāṃ tato mām abravīt priyā | [BKŚS, 13 4.2]
maṅgalānāṃ pradhānatvāt kāryasaṃsiddhidāyinī | [BKŚS, 13 5.1]
eṣā dhanapateḥ śeṣā svādur āsvādyatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 5.2]
mayoktam ananujñātas tātapādair guṇān api | [BKŚS, 13 6.1]
nāhaṃ sevitum icchāmi kiṃ punar vyasanaṃ mahat | [BKŚS, 13 6.2]
tataḥ sā dṛḍhasaṃrambhā śapathair avyatikramaiḥ | [BKŚS, 13 7.1]
cirān niruttarīkṛtya mām anicchum apāyayat | [BKŚS, 13 7.2]
pītaikamadhuśuktiṃ ca māṃ sāpṛcchat kṛtasmitā | [BKŚS, 13 8.1]
kimāsvādam idaṃ pānam iti pratyabravaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 13 8.2]
āpāne madhurāsvādam anusvāde tu tiktakam | [BKŚS, 13 9.1]
kṣaye kaṣāyakaṭukam avacchede manāg iti | [BKŚS, 13 9.2]
sābravīd vyaktam adyāpi na jānītha rasaṃ punaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 10.1]
pīyatām iti pītaṃ ca punas tadvacanānmayā | [BKŚS, 13 10.2]
idaṃ kīdṛśam ity asyai pṛcchatyai kathitaṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 13 11.1]
kim artham api me cittaṃ gatam asvasthatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 11.2]
tayoktam aparāpy ekā śuktir āsvādyatāṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 13 12.1]
gamiṣyaty acirād eva cittaṃ te svasthatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 12.2]
tasyām api ca pītāyām apaśyaṃ vegavadbhramān | [BKŚS, 13 13.1]
taruprāsādaśailādīn sthāvarān api jaṅgamān | [BKŚS, 13 13.2]
yathā cāhaṃ tayopāyair agrāmyaiḥ śapathādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 13 14.1]
anicchan pāyitaḥ pānaṃ tathā tām apy apāyayam | [BKŚS, 13 14.2]
balavadbhyām athākramya madena madanena ca | [BKŚS, 13 15.1]
yad eva rucitam tābhyāṃ tat taivāsmi pravartitaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 15.2]
yaḥ saṃtoṣayituṃ yakṣaṃ vivāhaḥ kṛtrimaḥ kṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 16.1]
tena kṛtrimam evāsau kanyātvaṃ pratipāditā | [BKŚS, 13 16.2]
tataḥ prātar upāgamya madhugandhādhivāsitam | [BKŚS, 13 17.1]
ghrātvā hariśikho veśma saṃbhrāntamatir uktavān | [BKŚS, 13 17.2]
apūrva iva gandho 'yam aryaputra vibhāvyate | [BKŚS, 13 18.1]
manye 'ryaputrayā yūyam anicchāḥ pāyitā iti | [BKŚS, 13 18.2]
sa mayoktaḥ sakhe sakhyā tavāhaṃ pāyito balāt | [BKŚS, 13 19.1]
bhavatāpi rucau satyāṃ sthīyatāṃ pīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 19.2]
so 'bravīd vyasanagrāmagrāmaṇyaṃ bhavatām api | [BKŚS, 13 20.1]
pānaṃ sādhu na paśyāmi kiṃ punar mantriṇām iti | [BKŚS, 13 20.2]
mayoktam aryapādeṣu samitreṣu samāśatam | [BKŚS, 13 21.1]
pālayatsu kim asmākam ātmabhir vañcitair iti | [BKŚS, 13 21.2]
tenoktaṃ mantrisacivair vijñāpyaṃ kāryam āgatam | [BKŚS, 13 22.1]
anuṣṭhāne punas tasya svātantryaṃ svāminām iti | [BKŚS, 13 22.2]
taṃ pibantaṃ sahāvābhyām ālokya marubhūtikaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 23.1]
niḥśaṅkaḥ pātum ārabdhas taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 23.2]
rājamānas tato raktair aṅgarāgasragambaraiḥ | [BKŚS, 13 24.1]
punar uktapriyālāpo mām avandata gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 24.2]
tam atyāsannam āsīnam atimātrapriyaṃvadam | [BKŚS, 13 25.1]
pādau saṃvāhayantaṃ me kruddho hariśikho 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 13 25.2]
unmatta kim asaṃbaddhaṃ bhāṣamāṇaḥ puraḥ prabhoḥ | [BKŚS, 13 26.1]
udvejayasi bhartāram apasṛtyāsyatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 26.2]
tenoktaṃ mūrkha naivedaṃ madasāmarthyajṛmbhitam | [BKŚS, 13 27.1]
svāmino niḥsapatnau tu pādāv icchāmi sevitum | [BKŚS, 13 27.2]
yadā tūbhayavaitarddhabhartṛmūrdhabhir arcitau | [BKŚS, 13 28.1]
bhaviṣyatas tadāsmākaṃ sasapatnau bhaviṣyataḥ | [BKŚS, 13 28.2]
vaitarddhanāmagrahaṇāt tato madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 13 29.1]
smitasaṃdarśitaprītir abravīt sāśrulocanā | [BKŚS, 13 29.2]
aho cāturyamādhuryapradhānaguṇabhūṣaṇāḥ | [BKŚS, 13 30.1]
ālāpā nirgatāḥ saumyād gomukhasya mukhād iti | [BKŚS, 13 30.2]
mayoktaṃ bhaṇa paśyāmas tvayā kasmāc ciraṃ sthitam | [BKŚS, 13 31.1]
ko vā tavedam ākāram ujjvalaṃ kṛtavān iti | [BKŚS, 13 31.2]
tenoktaṃ vayam āhūya māgadhyā rājasaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 13 32.1]
ājñāpitās tava bhrātrā pānam āsevitaṃ niśi | [BKŚS, 13 32.2]
tena pānagṛhāt pānaṃ svādyamānaṃ svadeta yat | [BKŚS, 13 33.1]
svayam āsvādya tad bhrātre tvayā prasthāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 13 33.2]
so 'haṃ devīdvayenāpi maṇḍayitvā svapāṇibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 13 34.1]
pānāgārāya gamitaḥ pānādhyakṣapuraḥsaraḥ | [BKŚS, 13 34.2]
tatra cāsvādayann eva tat tat pānaṃ manāṅ manāk | [BKŚS, 13 35.1]
matto 'haṃ preṣayāmi sma yuṣmabhyam api saṃtatam | [BKŚS, 13 35.2]
tasmāt pibata niḥśaṅkāḥ kāpiśāyanam āsavam | [BKŚS, 13 36.1]
anujñātāḥ sahāmātyair gurubhir muditair iti | [BKŚS, 13 36.2]
sevamānas tataḥ pānaṃ sakāntāmitramaṇḍalaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 37.1]
divasān gamayāmi sma prahṛṣṭaparicārakaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 37.2]
kadācid ekaparyaṅkasthitā madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 13 38.1]
yuṣmābhiḥ sukhasuptāhaṃ na draṣṭavyety abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 13 38.2]
mama tv āsīt kim ity eṣā nivārayati mām iti | [BKŚS, 13 39.1]
yat satyaṃ sutarāṃ cetaḥ kutūhalataraṅgitam | [BKŚS, 13 39.2]
kadācid ardharātre 'haṃ sthāvarākārajaṅgame | [BKŚS, 13 40.1]
pāne pariṇatiṃ yāti pratibuddhaḥ pipāsitaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 40.2]
tataḥ parijanaṃ dṛṣṭvā prasuptam abhavan mama | [BKŚS, 13 41.1]
na yuktaṃ sukhasuptasya śatror api nibodhanam | [BKŚS, 13 41.2]
bhāryā punaḥ śarīrārdham ato madanamañjukām | [BKŚS, 13 42.1]
pratibodhya jalaṃ yāce taddhi me na virūpyate | [BKŚS, 13 42.2]
iti nirdhārya tasyāṃ ca mayā dṛṣṭir nipātitā | [BKŚS, 13 43.1]
yāvad anyaiva sā kāpi nārīrūpaiva candrikā | [BKŚS, 13 43.2]
āsīc ca mama kiṃ yakṣī kiṃ gandharvī kim apsarāḥ | [BKŚS, 13 44.1]
mānuṣī syāt kulastrī syād gaṇikā syād iyaṃ na hi | [BKŚS, 13 44.2]
yasmād anyatamāpy āsāṃ lakṣaṇair nopapadyate | [BKŚS, 13 45.1]
tasmād vidyādharī prāptā kāpi kenāpi hetunā | [BKŚS, 13 45.2]
iti nirṇīya nipuṇaṃ kariṇītālukomalau | [BKŚS, 13 46.1]
gāḍhaṃ saṃvāhayāmi sma tasyāś caraṇapallavau | [BKŚS, 13 46.2]
sā tu saṃtyājitā nidrāṃ sadyaś caraṇapīḍayā | [BKŚS, 13 47.1]
mām ālokya tathābhūtaṃ bhītā bhūmāv upāviśat | [BKŚS, 13 47.2]
abravīc ca na kartavyam aryaputreṇa sāhasam | [BKŚS, 13 48.1]
tvādṛśām anukampyo hi balināṃ pramadājanaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 48.2]
tataḥ śrutveti yat satyam ātmany evāsmi lajjitaḥ | [BKŚS, 13 49.1]
evaṃ kāriṇam apy eṣā saṃbhāvayati mām iti | [BKŚS, 13 49.2]
sā māṃ lajjitam ālokya jānusaṃnihitānanam | [BKŚS, 13 50.1]
lajjām apaharantīva tvaritedam abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 13 50.2]
śrūyatāṃ cāpriyaṃ sā te priyā madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 13 51.1]
tvadguṇasmaraṇavyagrā nayate divasān iti | [BKŚS, 13 51.2]
āsīn me manasi hṛtā na sā mṛtā sā yā dṛṣṭer vrajati na gocaraṃ priyā me | [BKŚS, 13 52.1]
jyotsnā hi sphuṭadhavalāpi kaumudīndor andhānāṃ bahalatamomalīmasaiva | [BKŚS, 13 52.2]
{BKŚS, 14}
tatas tām abravaṃ bhīru tvam eva hi mama priyā | [BKŚS, 14 1.1]
tathāpi tu vinodena tiṣṭhāmaḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 1.2]
grahītavyāni nāmāni gurudevadvijanmanām | [BKŚS, 14 2.1]
yasmāt tena viśuddhyarthaṃ svānam ācaritaṃ tayā | [BKŚS, 14 2.2]
asti merugiriprāṃśur āṣāḍho nāma parvataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 3.1]
śūrapaṇḍitavittāḍhyavidyādharakulālayaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 3.2]
tatra vidyādharasvāmī vedavān vegavān iti | [BKŚS, 14 4.1]
yaḥ kuberādhikasvo 'pi niḥsva eva dinātyaye | [BKŚS, 14 4.2]
tasyāpi pṛthivī nāma mahiṣī prāṃśuvaṃśajā | [BKŚS, 14 5.1]
tṛṇāya manyate sthairyād yā devīṃ pṛthivīm api | [BKŚS, 14 5.2]
tau ca putram avindantau ciraṃ duḥkham atiṣṭhatām | [BKŚS, 14 6.1]
prauḍhāyā iva kanyāyāḥ pitarau sadṛśaṃ varam | [BKŚS, 14 6.2]
tau manaḥputrikāṃ nāma kulavidyāṃ sutārthinau | [BKŚS, 14 7.1]
ārādhayitum ārabdhau tayā coktaṃ prasannayā | [BKŚS, 14 7.2]
sarvavidyādharotkṛṣṭavidyādharaparākramaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 8.1]
bhavitā bhavatoḥ putraḥ putrakau duḥkham ujhatam | [BKŚS, 14 8.2]
ekā ca duhitā yasyāḥ kalāśālī bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 14 9.1]
śūraḥ sāṅga ivānaṅgo vidyādharapatiḥ patiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 9.2]
kāle kvacid atīte ca prasūtā pṛthivī sutam | [BKŚS, 14 10.1]
trivargam akṣataṃ devī pṛthivīva surakṣitā | [BKŚS, 14 10.2]
manaḥputrikayā dattaḥ sa yasmāt kulavidyayā | [BKŚS, 14 11.1]
tasmān mānasavegākhyaḥ putraḥ pitrā prasādhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 11.2]
saṃvatsaratraye 'tīte jātāyā duhituḥ kṛtam | [BKŚS, 14 12.1]
nāma vegavatātmīyam asau vegavatī tataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 12.2]
labdheṣṭatanayau tau ca modamānāv aharniśam | [BKŚS, 14 13.1]
nītavantau ciraṃ kālam ekāharniśasaṃmitam | [BKŚS, 14 13.2]
vegavān ekadā snātaḥ prīṇitāgnisuradvijaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 14.1]
bhadrāsanastham ātmānaṃ dadarśa ādarśamaṇḍale | [BKŚS, 14 14.2]
atha haṃsam ivāsīnam añjanācalamūrdhani | [BKŚS, 14 15.1]
mṛṇāladhavalaṃ keśaṃ dṛṣṭavān ātmamūrdhani | [BKŚS, 14 15.2]
tato bhadrāsanaṃ tyaktvā vasudhāsthaṇḍile sthitaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 16.1]
pṛṣṭo mānasavegena kim etad iti vegavān | [BKŚS, 14 16.2]
tenoktaṃ palitaṃ dṛṣṭvā manaḥputrikavaṃśajāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 17.1]
tapāṃsi vā niṣevante vedāntavihitāni vā | [BKŚS, 14 17.2]
tat prajāḥ pālayeḥ putra prajās tvāṃ pālayantu ca | [BKŚS, 14 18.1]
pālitair hi mṛgendro 'pi kānanair eva pālyate | [BKŚS, 14 18.2]
atha mānasavegena krośantīṣu prajāsu ca | [BKŚS, 14 19.1]
rājā mandasukhotkaṇṭhaḥ pratiyātas tapovanam | [BKŚS, 14 19.2]
bhartrā nivartyamānāpi vacobhiḥ sopapattibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 20.1]
na nivṛttā yadā devī tadopāyaṃ prayuktavān | [BKŚS, 14 20.2]
adyaivāhaṃ cyuto rājyād adyaiveyaṃ pativratā | [BKŚS, 14 21.1]
na me sampādayaty ājñām aho dharmaḥ satām iti | [BKŚS, 14 21.2]
tato hrītā ca bhītā ca sāśruśreṇiḥ savepathuḥ | [BKŚS, 14 22.1]
pādayoḥ patitā patyur vyajñāpayad asau śanaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 22.2]
yadā tarhi mayā yūyaṃ pāvayantas tapovanam | [BKŚS, 14 23.1]
upāsyāḥ pāvanatamaṃ sa kālaḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 23.2]
so 'bravīd durlabhaṃ putraṃ sthirasiṃhāsanāsthitam | [BKŚS, 14 24.1]
bhartāraṃ vegavatyāś ca dṛṣṭvā draṣṭāsi mām iti | [BKŚS, 14 24.2]
evaṃ caiva ca kalyāṇi pitā vijñāpyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 25.1]
uktā vegavatī mātrā pitaraṃ praṇatābravīt | [BKŚS, 14 25.2]
tāta tvayi vanaṃ yāte ko me dāsyati modakān | [BKŚS, 14 26.1]
kalpavṛkṣaprasūtāni phalāni kusumāni vā | [BKŚS, 14 26.2]
tenoktaṃ yena yenārtho durlabhenāpi kenacit | [BKŚS, 14 27.1]
tat tan mānasavegas te bhrātā dātāsyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 27.2]
iti rājyakalatramitraputrān gṛhadhāmaṃ ca tṛṇāya manyamānaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 28.1]
gurusattvarajastamaḥkalaṅkāṃ prakṛtiṃ hātum agād vanaṃ narendraḥ | [BKŚS, 14 28.2]
śriyaṃ mānasavego 'pi kadalīdalacañcalām | [BKŚS, 14 29.1]
śaktitrayaprayogajñaḥ kṛtavān acalācalām | [BKŚS, 14 29.2]
atha yāte kvacit kāle mātaṅgādhipateḥ sutā | [BKŚS, 14 30.1]
āṣāḍhaṃ vāyumukteti sakhīparivṛtāgamat | [BKŚS, 14 30.2]
sā sma vegavatīm āha rājaputri kim āsyate | [BKŚS, 14 31.1]
uttiṣṭhākāśamārgeṇa gacchāmo malayācalam | [BKŚS, 14 31.2]
śṛṅgakuñjanitambeṣu tasya ramyeṣu ramyatām | [BKŚS, 14 32.1]
netrāpidhānikākhyānaputrikākandukair iti | [BKŚS, 14 32.2]
tayoktaṃ nāsti me śaktir gantum ākāśavartmanā | [BKŚS, 14 33.1]
alabdhakulavidyāyāḥ sakhi tan mṛṣyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 33.2]
upahasya tatas tās tām uccais tāḍitapāṇayaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 34.1]
ādhatāmbarapakṣāḥ khaṃ haṃsakanyā ivāsthitāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 34.2]
bhrātur antikam āyātā sāvegā vegavatyapi | [BKŚS, 14 35.1]
tena coktāṅkam āropya mātaḥ kiṃ dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 35.2]
tayoktaṃ dehi me vidyāṃ mahārāja sasādhanām | [BKŚS, 14 36.1]
siddhavidyābhir adyāhaṃ sakhībhir hāsitā yataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 36.2]
acireṇaiva dāsyāmi mātar ity abhidhāya sā | [BKŚS, 14 37.1]
bhrātā visarjitāsārabālālaṅkāravañcitā | [BKŚS, 14 37.2]
ekadā gaurimuṇḍasya bhaginī gaurimadyaśāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 38.1]
gatā vegavatīṃ draṣṭum āṣāḍhaṃ sasakhī sakhīm | [BKŚS, 14 38.2]
upahasya ca tāṃ sāpi vipakṣām iva sārasīm | [BKŚS, 14 39.1]
sapakṣā rājahaṃsīva gatā prati himācalam | [BKŚS, 14 39.2]
vegavatyapi sāsthānaṃ gatvā bhrātaram abravīt | [BKŚS, 14 40.1]
kim ayaṃ kṣipyate kālo vidyā me dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 40.2]
tenoktam api dāsyāmi tvarase kim akāraṇam | [BKŚS, 14 41.1]
gurukāryakriyāvyagraṃ kiṃ na paśyasi mām iti | [BKŚS, 14 41.2]
sā gatvā manyubhāreṇa sphurantīva tvarāvatī | [BKŚS, 14 42.1]
apatan mātur utsaṅge saṃtapteva vaśā hrade | [BKŚS, 14 42.2]
pṛthivī tu samāhūya sacivau bhartur abravīt | [BKŚS, 14 43.1]
acireṇa pitur mūlaṃ dārikāṃ nayataṃ yuvām | [BKŚS, 14 43.2]
antaraṅgo hi saṃbandhaḥ putraiḥ pitror akṛtrimaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 44.1]
bhrātaras tu dviṣanty eva bhrātṝn ekodarān api | [BKŚS, 14 44.2]
tau tām ākāśamārgeṇa nītavantau tapovanam | [BKŚS, 14 45.1]
mārgāyatanamārgeṣu sāmbhaḥsu gamitaśramām | [BKŚS, 14 45.2]
athāsthimayakāyānāṃ taḍidbabhrujaṭābhṛtām | [BKŚS, 14 46.1]
te 'paśyaṃs tatra vṛndāni tāpasānāṃ tapasyatām | [BKŚS, 14 46.2]
pṛcchanti sma ca tatraikam abhivādya tapasvinam | [BKŚS, 14 47.1]
brahman brūhi tam uddeśaṃ yatrāste vegavān iti | [BKŚS, 14 47.2]
so 'bravīt parvatāgre 'sāv aṅguṣṭhāgreṇa tiṣṭhati | [BKŚS, 14 48.1]
anugacchati gacchantam aṃśumantaṃ ca cakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 14 48.2]
parṇaśālā ca tasyeyaṃ yasyāḥ siṃhamataṅgajau | [BKŚS, 14 49.1]
aṅgaṇe krīḍataḥ prītāv imau ca śikhipannagau | [BKŚS, 14 49.2]
āsannāgamanaś cāsau dagdhaṃ hi kaṭhinaiḥ karaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 50.1]
tasyāhlādayituṃ cakṣur eṣa mandāyate raviḥ | [BKŚS, 14 50.2]
tapastāntaṃ tataḥ kāyaṃ sakāyam iva vegavān | [BKŚS, 14 51.1]
kāyakleśaṃ vahann āgād vaikhānasamṛgāvṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 51.2]
atha vegavatī dṛṣṭvā vegavantaṃ tathāvidham | [BKŚS, 14 52.1]
abravīn mantriṇau nāyaṃ mama tātaḥ sa vegavān | [BKŚS, 14 52.2]
tasya candraprabhacchattraprabhāḥ samukuṭaprabhāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 53.1]
prabhāsayanti dhāvantīṃ puraḥ sāmantasantatim | [BKŚS, 14 53.2]
ayaṃ tu siṃhamātaṅgaśārdūlamṛgatāpasaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 54.1]
tyaktavairaiḥ sahāyāti nūnaṃ ko 'pīndrajālikaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 54.2]
tābhyām uktaṃ sa evāyaṃ tathā cetthaṃ ca dṛśyate | [BKŚS, 14 55.1]
tādṛśā eva dṛśyante tathā cetthaṃ ca sādhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 55.2]
vandyatāṃ ca pitety uktā vandamānārdracakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 14 56.1]
aṅkam āropitā pitrā rūḍhadarbhāṅkuravraṇam | [BKŚS, 14 56.2]
mantriṇāv api bhartāram ucitāntaravartinau | [BKŚS, 14 57.1]
śirovāgbhir avandetām atha vegavatoditau | [BKŚS, 14 57.2]
āgaccha taṃ mamābhyāśam alaṃ sthitvātidūrataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 58.1]
janarañjanamātraṃ hi gataṃ tad rājyanāṭakam | [BKŚS, 14 58.2]
āsannasthaṇḍilasthau tau pṛṣṭavān atha vegavān | [BKŚS, 14 59.1]
rājño mānasavegasya rājyaṃ no varṇyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 59.2]
tābhyām uktam aśakyaṃ tad guṇāḍhyenāpi śaṃsitum | [BKŚS, 14 60.1]
tam apekṣya tu rājānaḥ śeṣāś chattraviḍambakāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 60.2]
iyaṃ māṇavikā kasmād ānīteti ca pṛcchate | [BKŚS, 14 61.1]
vidyālābhārtham ity uktaṃ tasmai tābhyāṃ savistaram | [BKŚS, 14 61.2]
tenoktam acirād eṣā labdhavidyā gamiṣyati | [BKŚS, 14 62.1]
yuvābhyāṃ nītipannābhyāṃ sa bālaḥ pālyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 62.2]
vegavatyapi sotsāhā karoti sma mahat tapaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 63.1]
kalpitāhārakartavyā phalamūlajalānilaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 63.2]
jalāharaṇasaṃmārgakusumapracayādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 64.1]
ārādhayad durārādhān asau vaikhānasān api | [BKŚS, 14 64.2]
uccinvantī kadācit sā phullāṃ kānanamallikām | [BKŚS, 14 65.1]
hā sarpeṇāsmi daṣṭeti sākrandāgamad āśramam | [BKŚS, 14 65.2]
yathāsaṃnihitais tatra vaikhānasakumārakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 66.1]
mā rājadārike bhaiṣīr ity uktvā parivāritā | [BKŚS, 14 66.2]
kvāsau kvāsau khalaḥ sarpa iti pṛṣṭā kumārakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 67.1]
amuṣmin mallikāgulma iti tebhyo nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 14 67.2]
te tv ālokya tam uddeśam avocann uccakaistarām | [BKŚS, 14 68.1]
rājaputri na sarpo 'yam ayaṃ sarpāntakaḥ śikhī | [BKŚS, 14 68.2]
dṛṣṭvā prasāritāṃ grīvām utphaṇāśīviṣopamām | [BKŚS, 14 69.1]
tvayā sarpa iti jñātaṃ tasmād āśvasyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 69.2]
uṭajāṅgaṇam ānītaḥ sa mayūraḥ kumārakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 70.1]
vicitrair nartito mārgais tayā kuṭṭitatālayā | [BKŚS, 14 70.2]
prekṣaṇīyaṃ ca tad draṣṭum adṛṣṭaṃ vanavāsibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 71.1]
militāḥ sarva evāsthus tapovananivāsinaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 71.2]
etasminn eva vṛttānte vegavantam upāgatam | [BKŚS, 14 72.1]
viśrāntam upagamyedam avocaṃs taṃ tapasvinaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 72.2]
rājadārikayā rājaṃs tapas taptaṃ sudustapam | [BKŚS, 14 73.1]
vayam ārādhitāḥ prītās tadvidyāṃ labhatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 73.2]
tenoktaṃ yadi ca prītā no bhavanto 'nujānate | [BKŚS, 14 74.1]
tato gṛhṇātv iyaṃ vidyāḥ pañcāṅgaparivāritāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 74.2]
anayā yat tapas taptam asmābhiś cedam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 14 75.1]
tad asyāḥ kulavidyānām alaṃ bhavatu siddhaye | [BKŚS, 14 75.2]
yac ca mānasavegasya vidyāsiddhiprabhāvitam | [BKŚS, 14 76.1]
balaṃ caturguṇaṃ tasmād bāleyaṃ pratipadyatām | [BKŚS, 14 76.2]
yaś cāsyāḥ ko 'pi dīrghāyur grahīṣyati varaḥ karam | [BKŚS, 14 77.1]
rājyasya daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ sa madīyasya bhokṣyati | [BKŚS, 14 77.2]
evam uktvā tatas tasyās tat sarvaṃ kṛtavān pitā | [BKŚS, 14 78.1]
sāpi labdhābhyanujñānā vegenodapatan nabhaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 78.2]
tataḥ kanakalekheva bhāsā kaṣaśilām asau | [BKŚS, 14 79.1]
piśaṅgabhavatī yāntī śyāmalām ambarasthalīm | [BKŚS, 14 79.2]
dṛṣṭā mānasavegena saṃbhramabhrāntacakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 14 80.1]
avātarat tadāsthāne haṃsīvāmbhojakānane | [BKŚS, 14 80.2]
kathaṃcit pratyabhijñāya lajjiteneva tena sā | [BKŚS, 14 81.1]
āliṅgyotsaṅgam āropya gamitā mātur antikam | [BKŚS, 14 81.2]
mātāpi duhitṛsneham anādṛtyaiva satvarā | [BKŚS, 14 82.1]
apṛcchad api kalyāṇi kuśalī vegavān iti | [BKŚS, 14 82.2]
kiṃ vāphalapralāpena sāram evāvadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 14 83.1]
yāsau vegavatī sāhaṃ tasya vegavataḥ sutā | [BKŚS, 14 83.2]
atīte tu kvacit kāle saśarīreva cārutā | [BKŚS, 14 84.1]
nītā mānasavegena kāpi bhūmau varāṅganā | [BKŚS, 14 84.2]
sā ca tadguṇabhūyiṣṭhāṃ dṛḍhaṃ dveṣṭi kathām api | [BKŚS, 14 85.1]
kṣīṇadoṣaguṇā sādhvī kāmastutikathām iva | [BKŚS, 14 85.2]
sa kadācit kvacit kāṃcid dṛṣṭvā tāpasakanyakām | [BKŚS, 14 86.1]
balād bhoktum upakrāntas tayā coktaṃ sphurad ruṣā | [BKŚS, 14 86.2]
yuktaṃ śāpāgninā dagdhuṃ tvādṛśaṃ pāpacetasam | [BKŚS, 14 87.1]
kiṃtu vegavataḥ sādhoḥ putratvaṃ tena mucyase | [BKŚS, 14 87.2]
sarvathā śāpanāmānaṃ pratīcchatu varaṃ bhavān | [BKŚS, 14 88.1]
adhīrahṛdayāḥ prāyas trāsagamyā bhavādṛśāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 88.2]

bhavataḥ śatadhā mūrdhā dagdhabuddheḥ sphuṭed iti | [BKŚS, 14 89.2]
tatas trastas tataḥ śāpād akāmāṃ kāminīm asau | [BKŚS, 14 90.1]
api notsahate draṣṭuṃ kuta eva niṣevitum | [BKŚS, 14 90.2]
sa tu mām abravīn mātas tathā madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 14 91.1]
protsāhyatāṃ yathā kṣipram upasarpati mām iti | [BKŚS, 14 91.2]
atha bālasvabhāvena sakutūhalayā mayā | [BKŚS, 14 92.1]
aśokavanikāmadhye dṛṣṭā madanamañjukā | [BKŚS, 14 92.2]
saṃkṣiptam adhitiṣṭhantī rūḍhaparṇalatoṭajam | [BKŚS, 14 93.1]
mlānacampakamāleva purāṇakadalīpuṭam | [BKŚS, 14 93.2]
parṇaśayyāśirobhāge nihitaḥ saṃpidhānakaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 94.1]
uṭajābhyantare nyastaḥ sajalaḥ kalaśas tayā | [BKŚS, 14 94.2]
atha lambhitaviśrambhāṃ mañjukām aham abravam | [BKŚS, 14 95.1]
kas te mānuṣakeṇārthaḥ kuru vidyādharaṃ patiṃ | [BKŚS, 14 95.2]
mugdhe mānuṣakās tāvad bahurogādyupadravāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 96.1]
vidyādharās tu vidyānāṃ prabhāvān nirupadravāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 96.2]
rājā mānasavegas tu bhartā te varṇyatāṃ katham | [BKŚS, 14 97.1]
yo vidyādhararājānāṃ rājā sphītaśriyām iti | [BKŚS, 14 97.2]
doṣān api manuṣyāṇāṃ gṛhṇāmi sma yathā yathā | [BKŚS, 14 98.1]
tathā tathābhavat tasyāḥ prītisphītākṣam ānanam | [BKŚS, 14 98.2]
guṇān vidyādharāṇāṃ tu gṛhṇāmi sma yathā yathā | [BKŚS, 14 99.1]
tathā tathābhavat tasyāḥ krodhajihmākṣam ānanam | [BKŚS, 14 99.2]
āgantukau yadā caināṃ prītikrodhāv amuñcatām | [BKŚS, 14 100.1]
gṛhṇāti sma tadā śokaḥ saniśvāsāsravepathuḥ | [BKŚS, 14 100.2]
athāsyāḥ parimṛjyāsram aśītasparśam abravam | [BKŚS, 14 101.1]
alaṃ bhagini saṃtapya jīvitaṃ rakṣyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 101.2]
tayā tūktaṃ mayā nedam ātmaduḥkhena rudyate | [BKŚS, 14 102.1]
aśakyaṃ tu bhayaṃ bhīmam āhṛtaṃ mandayā mayā | [BKŚS, 14 102.2]
sarvavidyākalābhijñaḥ sarvarūpavatāṃ tulā | [BKŚS, 14 103.1]
kulavidyādhanair yaś ca tuṅgair api na mādyati | [BKŚS, 14 103.2]
sa madvṛttāntam ajñātvā daśāṃ yāsyati kāmapi | [BKŚS, 14 104.1]
tataḥ sāntaḥpurāmātyarāṣṭraḥ somānvayo nṛpaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 104.2]
kiṃ tu pratyāśayā prāṇān ekayā dhārayāmy aham | [BKŚS, 14 105.1]
yad ādiṣṭaḥ sphuṭādeśair asau vidyādharādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 105.2]
vidyālavaviṣādhmātān vidyādharabhujaṅgakān | [BKŚS, 14 106.1]
vidyādharanarendro 'yaṃ kartā vāntaviṣān iti | [BKŚS, 14 106.2]
tataḥ śrutveti yat satyaṃ jātāhaṃ jātasaṃśayā | [BKŚS, 14 107.1]
vidyādharanarendraḥ syād uta na syād asāv iti | [BKŚS, 14 107.2]
kiṃ kācid dūtikā yātu sāpy asaktā parīkṣitum | [BKŚS, 14 108.1]
dūtikā matsamā nāsti svayam eva vrajāmy ataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 108.2]
tataḥ svārthāhitotsāhā pṛcchāmi sma tava priyām | [BKŚS, 14 109.1]
tava priyāya kiṃ vārtā tvadīyā dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 14 109.2]
atha kṣaṇam iva dhyātvā tayoktaṃ smayamānayā | [BKŚS, 14 110.1]
tulyam evāvayoḥ kāryaṃ śaktau satyāṃ kim āsyate | [BKŚS, 14 110.2]
idaṃ hi guru kartavyaṃ kṣiptakālaṃ ca sīdati | [BKŚS, 14 111.1]
īdṛśaṃ tvādṛśī karma kāryate katham anyathā | [BKŚS, 14 111.2]
iyaṃ maṇḍalitā veṇī mayā sakhi tavāgrataḥ | [BKŚS, 14 112.1]
daṣṭukāmeva capalā bhīṣaṇāśīviṣāṅganā | [BKŚS, 14 112.2]
dāhyā vā dahaneneyaṃ mocyā vā gṛdhrajambukaiḥ | [BKŚS, 14 113.1]
aryaputreṇa vā dagdha dāruṇā gatidāruṇā | [BKŚS, 14 113.2]
gatvā cāgaccha doleva na sthātavyaṃ kvacic ciram | [BKŚS, 14 114.1]
asaṅgā hi gatiḥ sakhyāḥ kāntaṃ yāntyāḥ smṛter iva | [BKŚS, 14 114.2]
ity uktājjukayā kṣipraṃ nabhasāham ihāgatā | [BKŚS, 14 115.1]
apaśyam aryaputraṃ ca hā kvāsīti pravādinam | [BKŚS, 14 115.2]
aninditam upāyaṃ ca vicintyātmasamarpaṇe | [BKŚS, 14 116.1]
ajjukārūpayā tubhyam ātmā saṃdarśito mayā | [BKŚS, 14 116.2]
nivāritāś ca yad yūyaṃ tadāliṅganalālasāḥ | [BKŚS, 14 117.1]
sa doṣaḥ kanyakātvasya viśuddhakulajanmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 117.2]
yac cāyācitadānāya vivāhaḥ kārito mayā | [BKŚS, 14 118.1]
sa ca saṃskartum ātmānaṃ kvātra yakṣaḥ kva cājjukā | [BKŚS, 14 118.2]
yac ca pātum anicchantaḥ pāyitāḥ stha balān madhu | [BKŚS, 14 119.1]
tatra yat kāraṇaṃ tac ca prāyaḥ pratyakṣam eva ca | [BKŚS, 14 119.2]
na draṣṭavyāsmi supteti pratiṣiddhāḥ stha yan mayā | [BKŚS, 14 120.1]
tat kutūhalavṛddhyarthaṃ vāmaśīlā hi bālatā | [BKŚS, 14 120.2]
sarvathā vistareṇālam ajjukā madamañjukā | [BKŚS, 14 121.1]
nītā mānasavegena lakṣmīr iva durātmanā | [BKŚS, 14 121.2]
tad ājñāpaya māṃ kṣipram imāṃ madanamañjukām | [BKŚS, 14 122.1]
ānayāmi parair nītāṃ śuddhā nītir iva śriyam | [BKŚS, 14 122.2]
āsīc ca mama na nyāyyaṃ praiṣaṇīyajanocitam | [BKŚS, 14 123.1]
bhartuḥ kārayituṃ karma bhāryāṃ tuṅgakulodbhavām | [BKŚS, 14 123.2]
athainām abruvaṃ caṇḍi śrutam ehi śayāvahai | [BKŚS, 14 124.1]
na hi tāmraśikhaṇḍānām adyāpi sphurati dhvaniḥ | [BKŚS, 14 124.2]
aham api dhavalenduvaṃśajanmā kuliśakaṭhorakaniṣṭhikāprakoṣṭhaḥ | [BKŚS, 14 125.1]
priyasamaraparāvarodharuddhān ahataripuḥ katham āhareya dārān | [BKŚS, 14 125.2]
{BKŚS, 15}
paripāṭyā tataḥ prāptās trayo hariśikhādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 1.1]
prabhāte mām avandanta na tu vegavataḥ sutām | [BKŚS, 15 1.2]
gomukhas tv acirāt prāptaḥ prathamaṃ mām avandata | [BKŚS, 15 2.1]
asmadāsannam āsīnāṃ bhaktyā vegavatīṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 15 2.2]
asau hariśikhenoktaḥ suṣṭhu khalv asi paṇḍitaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 3.1]
vandyāvandyavicāre hi paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 3.2]
athoktaṃ tena matto 'sti bhavān evātipaṇḍitaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 4.1]
vandyalakṣaṇayuktāṃ yo vandyām api na vandate | [BKŚS, 15 4.2]
bhaṇa kena na pūjyeyaṃ yā naḥ pūjyena pūjitā | [BKŚS, 15 5.1]
nanu mandamate lokaḥ pūjyapūjitapūjakaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 5.2]
svāminī svāmisaṃbandhāt svāmīvārhati vandanām | [BKŚS, 15 6.1]
candrāsannair hi nakṣatrair lokaḥ kāryāṇi kāryate | [BKŚS, 15 6.2]
ityādi vadatas tasya pakṣam utkarṣayann iva | [BKŚS, 15 7.1]
ahaṃ vegavatīvṛttaṃ tadvarṇitam avarṇayam | [BKŚS, 15 7.2]
vidyādharakumārīṇāṃ pravṛttāvartanīti te | [BKŚS, 15 8.1]
vandato muditā gatvā senābhartre nyavedayan | [BKŚS, 15 8.2]
tenāpi tātapādebhyas tair ambābhyāṃ niveditam | [BKŚS, 15 9.1]
harṣadundubhivṛndais tu nadadbhir vṛtraśatrave | [BKŚS, 15 9.2]
gambhīrotpātajīmūtasaṃpātahrādabhīṣaṇe | [BKŚS, 15 10.1]
pramodadhvanite yātaṃ tanyamāne divāniśam | [BKŚS, 15 10.2]
atha senāpatiḥ prāptaḥ prātar mām idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 15 11.1]
idānīm eva devībhyāṃ devo vijñāpito yathā | [BKŚS, 15 11.2]
dvitīyayā vadhukayā gṛhīto dārakaḥ svayam | [BKŚS, 15 12.1]
kasyāścid api nāsmābhir dṛṣṭaḥ pariṇayotsave | [BKŚS, 15 12.2]
tena prasādo yady asti vegavatyā tataḥ saha | [BKŚS, 15 13.1]
naravāhanadattasya vivāhaḥ kāryatām iti | [BKŚS, 15 13.2]
devena tu vihasyoktam evam astu kim āsyate | [BKŚS, 15 14.1]
mamāpi hi manasy āsīd ayam eva manorathaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 14.2]
kiṃ tu mātā varasyātra devī bhavatu māgadhī | [BKŚS, 15 15.1]
pitāhaṃ varapakṣe 'sya samastam avarodhanam | [BKŚS, 15 15.2]
astu vāsavadattāyāḥ sutā vegavataḥ sutā | [BKŚS, 15 16.1]
rumaṇvadādayaḥ pakṣe tasyā evaṃ bhavantv iti | [BKŚS, 15 16.2]
athāntaḥpuram ambāyāḥ padmāvatyāḥ suhṛdvṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 17.1]
nīto 'haṃ citravinyāsaratnamaṅgalamaṇḍalam | [BKŚS, 15 17.2]
sabhartṛbahuputrābhir nārībhir vegavatyapi | [BKŚS, 15 18.1]
jyeṣṭhāmbābhavanaṃ nītā kelikolāhalākulam | [BKŚS, 15 18.2]
tapantakas tu māgadhyā preṣitaḥ prekṣituṃ vadhūm | [BKŚS, 15 19.1]
maṣīkālamukhoraskaḥ kārito jyeṣṭhayāmbayā | [BKŚS, 15 19.2]
kampamānaś ca kopena tataḥ pratyāgato 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 15 20.1]
aryaputra khalīkāraṃ paśyatemaṃ mamedṛśam | [BKŚS, 15 20.2]
śvaśrūs te māṃ khalīkṛtya sāntarhāsam avocata | [BKŚS, 15 21.1]
kva yāsi jālma labdho 'si preṣitas tvaṃ caraḥ kila | [BKŚS, 15 21.2]
ekaiva mama bāleyam āyācitaśatārjitā | [BKŚS, 15 22.1]
asyāḥ saubhāgyam utpādyam avaśyaṃ kārmaṇair mayā | [BKŚS, 15 22.2]
mātā jāmātṛkasyaiva mahākārmaṇakārikā | [BKŚS, 15 23.1]
yayā hastatale bhartā gurudhairyo 'pi nartitaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 23.2]
vardhayantyāś ciraṃ putraṃ tasyāḥ kārmaṇamālayā | [BKŚS, 15 24.1]
kiṃ mayā preṣitaḥ kaścid bhavān iva caras tayā | [BKŚS, 15 24.2]
ity uktvālambhito bhīmām ardhacandraparaṃparām | [BKŚS, 15 25.1]
devyāḥ niṣkramitaḥ svasmād aham antaḥpurād iti | [BKŚS, 15 25.2]
tapantakena yā prāptā tatra gatvā viḍambanā | [BKŚS, 15 26.1]
tām anekaguṇāṃ prāpañ jyeṣṭhāmbāpreṣitāś carāḥ | [BKŚS, 15 26.2]
iti pravṛttavṛttānte matte 'ntaḥpurasāgare | [BKŚS, 15 27.1]
mayā vegavatīpāṇir gṛhīto mantrasaṃskṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 27.2]
atha gatvā svam āvāsaṃ vāsāvāsaṃ praviśya ca | [BKŚS, 15 28.1]
anyādṛśaprapañceva dṛṣṭā vegavatī mayā | [BKŚS, 15 28.2]
vyāhṛtā vacanaṃ nādād agād ālambitāṃśukā | [BKŚS, 15 29.1]
śayanaṃ ca navoḍheva sevate sma parāṅmukhī | [BKŚS, 15 29.2]
upasṛtya śanaiś caināṃ bravīmi sma vilakṣakaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 30.1]
vrīḍākrīḍākṛtā pīḍā durbhagā tyajyatām iti | [BKŚS, 15 30.2]
tayā tu katham apy uktaṃ sphuṭitasmitacandrikam | [BKŚS, 15 31.1]
aryaputra kutaḥ krīḍā gurvājñeyaṃ garīyasī | [BKŚS, 15 31.2]
mayā hi śvaśurādeśād asmin vivāhanāṭake | [BKŚS, 15 32.1]
duṣkarā kṣiptavelāpi vadhūkābhūmikā kṛtā | [BKŚS, 15 32.2]
tathā nāṭayitavyeyam ujjvalā jāyate yathā | [BKŚS, 15 33.1]
tasmād guruniyogo 'yam alaṅghyaḥ kṣamyatām iti | [BKŚS, 15 33.2]
tayā saha visarpantyā vivāhakathayānayā | [BKŚS, 15 34.1]
anayaṃ kṣaṇasaṃkṣiptām āyātām api yāminīm | [BKŚS, 15 34.2]
gate tu nātisaṃkṣipte kāle caṭulasambhramaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 35.1]
tvarāvān skhaladālāpo mām avocat tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 35.2]
aryaputra mayā dṛṣṭāś catasraḥ puradevatāḥ | [BKŚS, 15 36.1]
bhrāmyatā nagarodyāne dainyamlānānanendavaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 36.2]

na dṛṣṭāv evamākārau sagoyūthau dvijāv iti | [BKŚS, 15 138.2]
tenoktaṃ na mayā dṛṣṭau tau mahāpāpakāriṇau | [BKŚS, 15 139.1]
yau tvāṃ pātālagambhīre kūpe bhrātaram aujhatām | [BKŚS, 15 139.2]
praṣṭavyāv api na kṣudrau draṣṭavyāv api na tvayā | [BKŚS, 15 140.1]

tam uvāca tritaḥ krodhād dhūrtaṃ kaluṣamānasam | [BKŚS, 15 141.1]
duṣṭamaskariṇaṃ dhik tvāṃ sādhunindāviśāradam | [BKŚS, 15 141.2]
jñānendukiraṇavyastasaṃmohadhvāntasaṃcayāḥ | [BKŚS, 15 142.1]
tādṛśā eva jānanti sādhavaṃ na bhavādṛśāḥ | [BKŚS, 15 142.2]
tatas tasya parivrājaḥ śucitāmraghaṭāruṇam | [BKŚS, 15 143.1]
jātaṃ vikasitajyotiḥ kirīṭābharaṇaṃ śiraḥ | [BKŚS, 15 143.2]
śarīraṃ ca sahasrākṣaṃ karaṃ ca kuliśākulam | [BKŚS, 15 144.1]
kṛtaivamādikākāraḥ sa jātaḥ sarvathā hariḥ | [BKŚS, 15 144.2]
varaṃ brūhīti tenoktas tritas tuṣṭas tam abravīt | [BKŚS, 15 145.1]
bhrātarau me sapāpau ced apāpau bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 15 145.2]
punar brūhīti tenoktaḥ punar apy abravīt tritaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 146.1]
gurū me gurave gās tāḥ prītau vitaratām iti | [BKŚS, 15 146.2]
punaḥ prītatamenoktaṃ hariṇā yācyatām iti | [BKŚS, 15 147.1]
paryāptam iti tenokte prītaḥ śakro divaṃ yayau | [BKŚS, 15 147.2]
evaṃ mahendradaivatyām iṣṭiṃ nirvartya mānasīm | [BKŚS, 15 148.1]
tasmāt pātālagambhīrād avaṭād utthitas tritaḥ | [BKŚS, 15 148.2]

yājakais tu vinā yajñaṃ kṣatriyasya virudhyate | [BKŚS, 15 149.2]
tasmād asmād upāyena kenottiṣṭheyam ity aham | [BKŚS, 15 150.1]
iti ceti ca nirdhārya smṛtyāmitagatiṃ gataḥ | [BKŚS, 15 150.2]
śaṅkubandhanamuktena tenāhaṃ yācitas tadā | [BKŚS, 15 151.1]
kaṣṭām āpadam āpanno vidhaye māṃ smarer iti | [BKŚS, 15 151.2]
asoḍhaprārthanāduḥkhaṃ varaṃ tyaktaṃ śarīrakam | [BKŚS, 15 152.1]
na tu pratyupakārāśā rujājarjaritaṃ dhṛtam | [BKŚS, 15 152.2]
evaṃ ca cintayann eva kūpe kūpataros tale | [BKŚS, 15 153.1]
apaśyam aham ātmānaṃ taṃ cāmitagatiṃ puraḥ | [BKŚS, 15 153.2]
māṃ cāvocat sa vanditvā harṣaghargharayā girā | [BKŚS, 15 154.1]
yuṣmatsmaraṇapūto 'yaṃ janaḥ kiṃ kurutām iti | [BKŚS, 15 154.2]
khe saṃgrāmayamāṇāyāḥ saha bhrātrā balīyasā | [BKŚS, 15 155.1]

kartum icchati yo mohān mahāgaurīṃ sa rakṣati | [BKŚS, 15 156.2]
ājñā tu prathamaṃ dattā kartavyaivānujīvinā | [BKŚS, 15 157.1]

śatror galadgalasirārudhireṇa mūrdhnā nābhyarcitaṃ madasilūnaśirodhareṇa | [BKŚS, 15 158.2]

athāsau mām avanditvā nistriṃśakarakaṅkaṭaḥ | [BKŚS, 16 1.1]

kiṃ kadācit tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ śruto vā kaścid īdṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 16 15.1]
evaṃ vā praviśan dhīraṃ dharaṇīdhīradhīr iti | [BKŚS, 16 15.2]
tenoktam ananujñātaṃ bhartrā nāradam apy aham | [BKŚS, 16 16.1]

ayaṃ tu dhriyamāṇo 'pi digdantigatidhīrataḥ | [BKŚS, 16 17.1]
praviśaty eva pāruṣyamātrasārā hi mādṛśāḥ | [BKŚS, 16 17.2]
atha niṣkāraṇotkaṇṭhākaram udyānamandiram | [BKŚS, 16 18.1]
prāviśaṃ nisvanadvīṇaṃ vinītāṇḍajavānaram | [BKŚS, 16 18.2]
tatrāsīnaṃ śilāpaṭṭe citrapaṭṭopadhānake | [BKŚS, 16 19.1]
apaśyam amarākāraṃ naraṃ nāgarakeśvaram | [BKŚS, 16 19.2]

mukhasya gandharāgau ca tāmbūlenodapādayam | [BKŚS, 16 80.2]
evaṃ ca sukham āsīno vīṇādattakam abravam | [BKŚS, 16 81.1]
vīṇonmattir iyaṃ kasmāc campāyāṃ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 16 81.2]
tenoktam iha campāyāṃ sānudāso vaṇikpatiḥ | [BKŚS, 16 82.1]
tasya gandharvadatteti sutā trailokyasundarī | [BKŚS, 16 82.2]
sa ca tāṃ dhriyamāṇo 'pi varair varaguṇākaraiḥ | [BKŚS, 16 83.1]
abhiprāyeṇa kenāpi na kasmaicit prayacchati | [BKŚS, 16 83.2]
pratyākhyātum aśaktena yācitena kṣaṇe kṣaṇe | [BKŚS, 16 84.1]
tena śulkam upanyastaṃ duḥsaṃpādaṃ surair api | [BKŚS, 16 84.2]
apūrvaṃ kila gāyantyās tasyāḥ kim api gītakam | [BKŚS, 16 85.1]
yo 'nuvādayitā vīṇāṃ pariṇetā sa tām iti | [BKŚS, 16 85.2]
mayeyaṃ pariṇetavyā mayeyam iti nistrapaḥ | [BKŚS, 16 86.1]
na kaścid yo na campāyāṃ vīṇayonmattakaḥ kila | [BKŚS, 16 86.2]
puro nāgarakāṇāṃ ca catuḥṣaṣṭes tadarthinām | [BKŚS, 16 87.1]
ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe gate māse sā tad gāyati gītakam | [BKŚS, 16 87.2]
anena ca prakāreṇa yātaḥ kālo mahān ayam | [BKŚS, 16 88.1]
na cāpi vīṇayā kaścid anugacchati tām iti | [BKŚS, 16 88.2]
etatkathāvasāne ca puruṣau śrotriyākṛtī | [BKŚS, 16 89.1]
vīṇādattakam abrūtāṃ sthavirau vetradhāriṇau | [BKŚS, 16 89.2]
śreṣṭhinā preṣitāv āvāṃ saṃdeśena tvadantikam | [BKŚS, 16 90.1]
yadi sajjā suhṛdgoṣṭhī samasyā kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 16 90.2]
tenoktaṃ suhṛdaḥ sajjā yadi vaḥ susthitā gṛhāḥ | [BKŚS, 16 91.1]
kalyā gandharvadattā vā sva eva kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 16 91.2]
tatas taṃ pṛṣṭavān asmi mahotsāhena cetasā | [BKŚS, 16 92.1]
rūpaṃ gandharvadattāyāḥ kīdṛg ity atha so 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 16 92.2]
tasyāḥ svakāntipariveṣapaṭāpidhānaṃ netraprabhāprakarasāritaharmyagarbham | [BKŚS, 16 93.1]
utkṛṣṭavismayavimohitamānasena rūpaṃ nirūpayitum eva mayā na śakyam | [BKŚS, 16 93.2]
{BKŚS, 17}
atha gandharvadattāyās tāṃ guṇākārasaṃpadam | [BKŚS, 17 1.1]
samākarṇyaiva karṇābhyāṃ mano nītaṃ vidheyatām | [BKŚS, 17 1.2]
pṛcchāmi sma ca bhūyas tam api śakyā bhaven mayā | [BKŚS, 17 2.1]
draṣṭuṃ gandharvadatteti tena coktaṃ na śakyate | [BKŚS, 17 2.2]
agāndharveṇa sā draṣṭuṃ devenāpi na śakyate | [BKŚS, 17 3.1]
yadi cecchatha tāṃ draṣṭuṃ gāndharvaṃ śikṣyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 3.2]
mayoktaṃ nāradīye 'pi nivṛtte kila labhyate | [BKŚS, 17 4.1]
gāndharvaśabdas tat tasmād asmākaṃ kāryatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 4.2]
tato vyāharitas tena vīṇācāryaḥ kharasvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 17 5.1]
naṣṭaśrutisvarajñāno bhūtiko nāma durbhagaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 5.2]
āsīc ca mama taṃ dṛṣṭvā vikṛtaṃ naravānaram | [BKŚS, 17 6.1]
alaṃ me nāradīyena kṛtaṃ gandharvadattayā | [BKŚS, 17 6.2]
īdṛśaḥ śiṣyatāṃ gatvā rājyalābho 'pi garhati | [BKŚS, 17 7.1]
anyāyāgatam aiśvaryaṃ nindanty eva hi sādhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 7.2]
abhyutthānābhivādābhyāṃ taṃ vīṇādattakādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 8.1]
apūjayan mayā cāsau na draṣṭum api pāritaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 8.2]
atha ruṣṭakaṭākṣeṇa lohitākṣaḥ sa vīkṣya mām | [BKŚS, 17 9.1]
vīṇādattakadattāyāṃ pīṭhikāyām upāviśat | [BKŚS, 17 9.2]
abravīd dattakas taṃ ca yakṣībhartur dvijanmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 10.1]
bhavān asyopapannasya nāradīyaṃ karotv iti | [BKŚS, 17 10.2]
tenoktaṃ sābhimānatvād ayaṃ mām avamanyate | [BKŚS, 17 11.1]
na ca pārayate dātuṃ dāridryāt kākaṇīm api | [BKŚS, 17 11.2]
guruśuśrūṣayā vidyā puṣkalena dhanena vā | [BKŚS, 17 12.1]
na cāsminn ekam apy asti yady asti pratipadyatām | [BKŚS, 17 12.2]
dattakenoktam ācārya virūpaṃ mantritaṃ tvayā | [BKŚS, 17 13.1]
ko yakṣīkāmukaṃ śakto daridram iti jalpitum | [BKŚS, 17 13.2]
yasya dāsaḥ sadāso 'haṃ tvaṃ jānāsy eva mādṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 14.1]
sa yakṣīkāmukaḥ kasmād daridra iti bhaṇyate | [BKŚS, 17 14.2]
suvarṇānāṃ śataṃ vāpi gṛhyatāṃ tvād.śocitam | [BKŚS, 17 15.1]
patite droṇamegho 'pi na tiṣṭhati jalaṃ sthale | [BKŚS, 17 15.2]
nāradādiparīvārāṃ sa cābhyarcya sarasvatīm | [BKŚS, 17 16.1]
durvyavasthitatantrīkāṃ vīṇāṃ mahyam upānayat | [BKŚS, 17 16.2]
mayā tu sā viparyaksthā sthāpitāṅke yadā tadā | [BKŚS, 17 17.1]
bhūtiko māṃ dhig ity uktvā vīṇādattakam uktavān | [BKŚS, 17 17.2]
na yakṣīkāmuko mandaḥ śakyaḥ śikṣayituṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 17 18.1]
vīṇāgrahaṇam apy eṣa na jānāti sukhaiditaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 18.2]
na nāma svayam etena yadi vīṇā na vāditā | [BKŚS, 17 19.1]
ālekhyavādakāḥ ke 'pi na dṛṣṭ naṣṭadṛṣṭinā | [BKŚS, 17 19.2]
iti saṃtakṣya māṃ vāgbhir ātodyaṃ parivartya ca | [BKŚS, 17 20.1]
sa niṣādo niṣādaṃ me ṣaḍja ityupadiṣṭavān | [BKŚS, 17 20.2]
athāmarṣaparītena dṛḍhaṃ tāḍayatā mayā | [BKŚS, 17 21.1]
catasraḥ pañca vā tantryaś chinnāś caḍ iti visvarāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 21.2]
athokto dattakas tena tantrīvartakasaṃgraham | [BKŚS, 17 22.1]
akṛtvā kiṃ karoty asya nāradīyaṃ bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 17 22.2]
ahaṃ tu vismṛtacchadmā chinnatantrīm api kṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 17 23.1]
śrutivāsitakarṇatvān mṛdu vīṇām avādayam | [BKŚS, 17 23.2]
atha visphāritair netrair utkarṇā dattakādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 24.1]
kim etad iti jalpanto mām aikṣanta savismayāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 24.2]
bhūtikas tu bhayakrodhalajjāvismayaniṣprabhaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 25.1]
kākatālīyam ity uktvā gata eva sadakṣiṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 25.2]
evaṃ ca divasaṃ nītvā kṛtaprādoṣikāśanaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 26.1]
āvasaṃ śayanāvāsaṃ mālādhūpādhivāsitam | [BKŚS, 17 26.2]
haṃsapakṣāṃśukaprāyakomalāstaraṇāstṛtam | [BKŚS, 17 27.1]
bhāsvadvajraśilāpādam āseve śayanaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 27.2]
rūpākṛṣṭajagannetre yuvatī sārabhūṣaṇe | [BKŚS, 17 28.1]
rūpājīve śanaiḥ pādau samavāhayatāṃ mama | [BKŚS, 17 28.2]
sahajāhāryamādhuryaramaṇīyatarākṣaraiḥ | [BKŚS, 17 29.1]
vacobhiḥ kila te cittaṃ madīyaṃ hartum aicchatām | [BKŚS, 17 29.2]
vegavatyā vimuktaṃ ca pratibhānti sma tāni mām | [BKŚS, 17 30.1]
rāsabhīrasitānīva virasāni svakarṇayoḥ | [BKŚS, 17 30.2]
tāni cāśrotukāmena nidrāvyājaḥ kṛto mayā | [BKŚS, 17 31.1]
atha prasupta evāsmi nirāśe te ca jagmatuḥ | [BKŚS, 17 31.2]
ardhe yāte ca yāminyāḥ śvāsānumitacetane | [BKŚS, 17 32.1]
dṛṣṭatattva ivāvidyāṃ nidrām atyajam utkaṭām | [BKŚS, 17 32.2]
citrapaṭṭapidhānāyāṃ tiṣṭhantyāṃ nāgadantake | [BKŚS, 17 33.1]
vīṇādattakavīṇāyāṃ tato dṛṣṭiṃ nyapātayam | [BKŚS, 17 33.2]
mama tv āsīd avaśyaṃ māṃ netā śvas tatra dattakaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 34.1]
vīṇā ca vādanīyā syāc cirotsṛṣṭā ca sā mayā | [BKŚS, 17 34.2]
vidyā cārādhyamānāpi duḥkhena paricīyate | [BKŚS, 17 35.1]
bhaktyā mātuḥ sapatnīva nisargakuṭilā hi sā | [BKŚS, 17 35.2]
vīṇā saṃnihitā ceyaṃ velā ceyaṃ nirākulā | [BKŚS, 17 36.1]
jijñāse tāvad ity enāṃ vicāryāhaṃ gṛhītavān | [BKŚS, 17 36.2]
utkarṣann apakarṣaṃś ca kāścit kāścin manāṅ manāk | [BKŚS, 17 37.1]
vyavasthāpayituṃ tantrīḥ karaśākhābhir aspṛśam | [BKŚS, 17 37.2]
athāśṛṇavam ālāpān svasmād vāsagṛhād bahiḥ | [BKŚS, 17 38.1]
samudrasena godatta dhāva dhāva sakhe drutam | [BKŚS, 17 38.2]
vīṇādattakabhadrasya gṛheṣu kṛtakarmaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 39.1]
sarasvatī bhagavatī vīṇāṃ sārayati svayam | [BKŚS, 17 39.2]
vīṇāyāḥ sāryamāṇāyāḥ svanasyodaya īdṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 40.1]
samāptasāraṇāyās tu kīdṛṅ nāma bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 17 40.2]
tasmāt sarasvatīvīṇe dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca saṃhate | [BKŚS, 17 41.1]
netraśrotrāṇi no yānti pavitrakaratām iti | [BKŚS, 17 41.2]
athāvalambayat tāṃ vīṇāṃ tvarayā nāgadantake | [BKŚS, 17 42.1]
prāvṛtya saśiraḥpādaṃ kāyaṃ nidrāṃ kilāgamam | [BKŚS, 17 42.2]
nāgarās tu nyavartanta jalpanto dīnacetasaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 43.1]
kathaṃ sarasvatī kṣudrair dṛśyate 'smadvidhair iti | [BKŚS, 17 43.2]
yāpitāyāṃ tu yāminyāṃ kṛtapūrvāhṇikakramam | [BKŚS, 17 44.1]
mām anulbaṇaveṣaṃ ca vanditvā dattako 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 17 44.2]
amī nāgarakāḥ prāptāś citrayānaprasādhanāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 45.1]
tad gandharvasamasyāyai yuṣmābhir api gamyatām | [BKŚS, 17 45.2]
ājñāpayata yānaṃ ca kareṇuturagādikam | [BKŚS, 17 46.1]
yena vo rocate gantuṃ tena prasthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 46.2]
mayoktaṃ gacchatu bhavān vāhanena yathāsukham | [BKŚS, 17 47.1]
ahaṃ tu pādacāreṇa gacchāmi śanakair iti | [BKŚS, 17 47.2]
athāsmadanurodhena māṃ purodhāya dattakaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 48.1]
prasthitaḥ pādacāreṇa sanāgarakamaṇḍalaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 48.2]
amantrayanta yāntaś ca kruddhā nāgarakā mithaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 49.1]
yakṣīkāmukarūpo 'yam anartho 'smān upāgataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 49.2]
vayam asya prasādena tyaktamaṇḍitavāhanāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 50.1]
āśādīrghāsu rathyāsu caraṇaiḥ saṃcarāmahe | [BKŚS, 17 50.2]
meror droṇīr ivākraman viśikhā vistṛtāyatāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 51.1]
apaśyaṃ veśmanāṃ mālās tasyaiva sirasām iva | [BKŚS, 17 51.2]
prāsādeṣu ca jalpantīr gavākṣapreritekṣaṇāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 52.1]
kokilāsubhagālāpāḥ śṛṇomi sma kulāṅganāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 52.2]
ayi māgadhi vaidehi malayāvati yāvani | [BKŚS, 17 53.1]
yakṣīkāmukam āyātuṃ sakhyaḥ paśyata dhāvata | [BKŚS, 17 53.2]
khalayā kila yakṣyāyam īrṣyāmuṣitacetasā | [BKŚS, 17 54.1]
ākāśāt pātitaḥ prāpto dattakena sujanmanā | [BKŚS, 17 54.2]
dhruvaṃ sā rākṣasī yakṣī yadi vā mṛttikāmayī | [BKŚS, 17 55.1]
kruddhayā mugdhayā vāpi yayā svārtho na cetitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 55.2]
athavā sarvam evedam alīkaṃ pratibhāti mām | [BKŚS, 17 56.1]
kva yakṣīkāmikaḥ kvāyaṃ kāmaḥ kāmī rater iva | [BKŚS, 17 56.2]
iti nirdiśyamāno 'ham aṅgulībhir itas tataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 57.1]
nayanotpalamālābhir arcyamānaś ca yātavān | [BKŚS, 17 57.2]
atha nāgarakāḥ prāpan sudhāṃ gṛhapater gṛham | [BKŚS, 17 58.1]
aṅgaṃ gandharvadattāyās teṣām iva manorathāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 58.2]
maṇihāṭakadantādyair aṅgais tair eva kalpitam | [BKŚS, 17 59.1]
sphuraddivyaprabhāvāt tu na vidma kiṃmayair iti | [BKŚS, 17 59.2]
tataḥ prathamakakṣāyām apaśyaṃ saṃnidhāpitām | [BKŚS, 17 60.1]
āsanānāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ mahāpaṭṭorṇaveṣṭitam | [BKŚS, 17 60.2]
teṣu nāgarakaḥ kaścit kāṃścid āha sma sasmitam | [BKŚS, 17 61.1]
aho mahākhalīkāro yakṣīkāmukam āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 61.2]
sānudāsābhyanujñātāḥ suhṛdo dattakādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 62.1]
samāyātāś catuḥṣaṣṭis tāvanty evāsanāny api | [BKŚS, 17 62.2]
yakṣīkāmukam ālokya pañcaṣaṣṭam anāsanam | [BKŚS, 17 63.1]
yat satyaṃ lajjito 'smīti tataś coktam ṛjur bhavān | [BKŚS, 17 63.2]
āyatto dattako yasya saputrapaśubāndhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 64.1]
tena gandharvadattāpi sulabhā kim utāsanam | [BKŚS, 17 64.2]
pañcaṣaṣṭam adṛṣṭvā tu nikṣiptaṃ tatra dattakaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 65.1]
dattavān svayam ākṛṣya mahyam ātmīyam āsanam | [BKŚS, 17 65.2]
te 'pi nāgarakāḥ śeṣāḥ sthite tiṣṭhati dattake | [BKŚS, 17 66.1]
tiṣṭhanti sma sthitā eva bhṛtakā iva bhartari | [BKŚS, 17 66.2]
athānyad āsanaṃ dattaṃ dattakāyojjvalaprabham | [BKŚS, 17 67.1]
sa tad adhyāsta śeṣāś ca yathāsanam upāviśan | [BKŚS, 17 67.2]
tatas triṃśacchataṃ tasmād gaṇikānāṃ vinirgatam | [BKŚS, 17 68.1]
gṛhād asurakanyānāṃ mahāsurapurād iva | [BKŚS, 17 68.2]
āttaśṛṅgārabhṛṅgārā kācid āvarjayaj jalam | [BKŚS, 17 69.1]
tāsāṃ pratyekam ekaikā teṣāṃ pādān adhāvata | [BKŚS, 17 69.2]
madīyas tu yayā pādaḥ pāṇibhyām avalambitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 70.1]
tayā svedajalenaiva dhautaḥ ślathaśarīrayā | [BKŚS, 17 70.2]
āvarjitavatī yā ca jalaṃ lulitalocanā | [BKŚS, 17 71.1]
visrastahastayā hastād bhṛṅgāraḥ pātitas tayā | [BKŚS, 17 71.2]
praviśan dhautapādaś ca śṛṇomi sma prajalpitāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 72.1]
prāṃśuprākāragarbhasthāḥ śrutihārigiraḥ striyaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 72.2]
anartho 'yam upanyastaḥ sānudāsena dāruṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 73.1]
śulkaṃ gandharvadattāyā vīṇāvādananāmakam | [BKŚS, 17 73.2]
yadi rūpam upanyasyec chulkaṃ gṛhapatis tataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 74.1]
na yakṣīkāmukād anyaṃ prāpnuyād bhartṛdārikā | [BKŚS, 17 74.2]
vīṇāyāṃ tu prayuktāyāṃ bhagno 'yaṃ no manorathaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 75.1]
hyo yasmād bhūtikenāsya nāradīyaṃ kṛtaṃ kila | [BKŚS, 17 75.2]
idaṃ tāvan mahad duḥkhaṃ yad yakṣīkāmuko 'nayā | [BKŚS, 17 76.1]
ayaṃ nāsulabhībhūtaḥ śulkadoṣān na labhyate | [BKŚS, 17 76.2]
idaṃ tu duḥsahataraṃ yad imāṃ bakulāvalīm | [BKŚS, 17 77.1]
anātmajño balāt ko 'pi gale tāṃ lambayiṣyati | [BKŚS, 17 77.2]
vīṇāvādanaśulkeyaṃ sābhiyogāś ca nāgarāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 78.1]
prajāpatiś ca durlagnaḥ sarvathā śivam astv iti | [BKŚS, 17 78.2]
atha niṣkampakālindī salilasvacchakuṭṭimām | [BKŚS, 17 79.1]
jvalanmaṇiśilāstambhāṃ viśālāṃ prāviśaṃ sabhām | [BKŚS, 17 79.2]
sabhā nāgarakaiḥ sābhād bhinnaprabhavibhūṣaṇaiḥ | [BKŚS, 17 80.1]
upatyakāsthalī meroḥ phullaiḥ kalpadrumair iva | [BKŚS, 17 80.2]
atha haṃsa ivotsārya nalinīdalamaṇḍalam | [BKŚS, 17 81.1]
nirgataḥ kañcukī prerya tiraskariṇikāmbaram | [BKŚS, 17 81.2]
sa nāgarakasaṃghātam avocad vinayānataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 82.1]
vijñāpayati vaḥ śreṣṭhī svāgataṃ guṇarāgiṇām | [BKŚS, 17 82.2]
bhavadbhir varṇasampannair antaḥsārair idaṃ gṛham | [BKŚS, 17 83.1]
śātakumbhamayaiḥ pūtaṃ gaṅgāmbhaḥkalaśair iva | [BKŚS, 17 83.2]
yadi sarve samāyātā yāto vāgamanaśramaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 84.1]
tato gandharvadattāyai nirdeśo dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 84.2]
te parasparam ālokya vidrāṇavadanaprabhāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 85.1]
hrītāḥ sadiśam ākāśam apaśyan proṣitottarāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 85.2]
tataḥ kañcukinā vaktraṃ kṣaṇād dīnatayā kṛtam | [BKŚS, 17 86.1]
samare kātarasyeva sannacakṣuḥkapolakam | [BKŚS, 17 86.2]
pratyekaṃ ca mukhāny eṣām avalokya ciraṃ ciram | [BKŚS, 17 87.1]
sa yadā yātum ārabdhas tadāhūya mayoditaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 87.2]
samāptapratikarmā vā kalyā vā yadi sā tataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 88.1]
āgacchatu kim adyāpi dṛṣṭair nāgarakair iti | [BKŚS, 17 88.2]
etāvataiva dattasya tat tādṛṅmlānam ānanam | [BKŚS, 17 89.1]
jātam ucchvasitaṃ svinnakapolasthalapīvaram | [BKŚS, 17 89.2]
alapat sānudāsasya prītaḥ parijanas tataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 90.1]
yakṣīkāmuka vandyo 'si sarvathā śobhitaṃ tvayā | [BKŚS, 17 90.2]
vāṅmātreṇāpi bhavataś cirād ucchvasitā vayam | [BKŚS, 17 91.1]
avagrahe hi jīmūto visphūrjann api śobhate | [BKŚS, 17 91.2]
tad evaṃ yādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ yādṛśī cātidhīratā | [BKŚS, 17 92.1]
tādṛśaṃ yadi vijñānaṃ bhavet kiṃ na bhaved iti | [BKŚS, 17 92.2]
eko nāgarakaś caikam avocad darśitasmitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 93.1]
uddāmitamukhā loke sukhaṃ jīvanti nistrapāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 93.2]
ko hi vedajaḍaṃ muktvā chāndasaṃ chāttram atrapam | [BKŚS, 17 94.1]
madhye mahāmanuṣyāṇām evam uddāmayen mukham | [BKŚS, 17 94.2]
yakṣīkāmukaśabdo 'pi śabda evāsya kevalam | [BKŚS, 17 95.1]
kva ca priyaguṇā yakṣī guṇarddhiḥ kva cedṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 95.2]
yat kiṃcid api bālānāṃ cetastoṣāya kalpate | [BKŚS, 17 96.1]
utkaṭena hi nāmnāpi prāyas tuṣyanti ḍiṇḍikāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 96.2]
śrutvedam itareṇoktaṃ mā sma nindad bhavān imam | [BKŚS, 17 97.1]
ko jānāti manuṣyāṇāṃ caritaṃ gūḍhacāriṇām | [BKŚS, 17 97.2]
yakṣīkāntaḥ prakṛṣṭena dhārṣṭyenājñāpayann api | [BKŚS, 17 98.1]
yathā paricitaśrīkas tathā māṃ prati śobhate | [BKŚS, 17 98.2]
tato javanikāṃ prerya kanyā kañcukibhir vṛtā | [BKŚS, 17 99.1]
devī gandharvadattāgād abhibhūtasabhāprabhā | [BKŚS, 17 99.2]
kathayāmi kathaṃ rūpaṃ tasyāḥ saṃkṣiptam ucyate | [BKŚS, 17 100.1]
pravrajyām āsthitā nūnam idānīm apsarogaṇāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 100.2]
kalpitaṃ ca sabhāmadhye padmarāgaśilāmayam | [BKŚS, 17 101.1]
candralekheva saṃdhyābhram adhyāsta caturantakam | [BKŚS, 17 101.2]
tejaso 'bhibhavāt tasyāḥ saṃkucanti sma nāgarāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 102.1]
bālāyāḥ śaśilekhāyāḥ puṇḍarīkākarā iva | [BKŚS, 17 102.2]
sātha prajñāvacaḥśūnyāṃ rūpamātrakaśālinīm | [BKŚS, 17 103.1]
paribhūtavatī goṣṭhīṃ sabhāstambhāvalīm iva | [BKŚS, 17 103.2]
atha dakṣiṇam utkṣipya karaṃ kañcukinoditam | [BKŚS, 17 104.1]
śrūyatāṃ śreṣṭhino vākyaṃ bho nāgarakakuñjarāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 104.2]
āste gandharvadatteyam iyaṃ vīṇā ca sāritā | [BKŚS, 17 105.1]
yo vo vādayituṃ śaktaḥ sa kiṃ tiṣṭhati ḍhaukatām | [BKŚS, 17 105.2]
aśeṣair na ca kartavyā paripāṭir apārthikā | [BKŚS, 17 106.1]
sā hi yuṣmākam asyāś ca lajjākhedaprayojanā | [BKŚS, 17 106.2]
tataḥ svayaṃ bhavadbhiś ca yasmin vo bhāvanāhitā | [BKŚS, 17 107.1]
yuṣmān ātmānam etāṃ ca sa kleśān mocayatv iti | [BKŚS, 17 107.2]
atha nāgarakāḥ sarve vīṇādattakam abruvan | [BKŚS, 17 108.1]
tvaṃ naḥ pūjyaḥ pravīṇaś ca tasmād utthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 108.2]
sa yadā kampitaśirā necchati sma tadāparaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 109.1]
saṃbhāvitatamas teṣāṃ gatvā vīṇām avādayat | [BKŚS, 17 109.2]
tasmin doṣair asaṃkīrṇān guṇān madhuratottarān | [BKŚS, 17 110.1]
sampādayati śabdo 'bhūd uccakaiḥ sādhu sādhv iti | [BKŚS, 17 110.2]
tato gandharvadattāyāṃ pragītāyām abhūn mama | [BKŚS, 17 111.1]
are jñātaṃ mayedānīṃ tenaivāmī vṛthāśramāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 111.2]
purā vāmanarūpeṇa baliṃ chalayatā kila | [BKŚS, 17 112.1]
tripiṣṭapaṃ tribhiḥ krāntaṃ vikramaiś cakrapāṇinā | [BKŚS, 17 112.2]
taṃ ca viśvāvasur nāma gandharvagaṇasevitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 113.1]
krāmantaṃ gaganaṃ vegāt triś cakāra pradakṣiṇam | [BKŚS, 17 113.2]
tena ca svayam utpādya stuvatā garuḍadhvajam | [BKŚS, 17 114.1]
nārāyaṇastutiṃ nāma gītaṃ gītakam adbhutam | [BKŚS, 17 114.2]
nāradena tataḥ prāptaṃ nāradād vṛtraśatruṇā | [BKŚS, 17 115.1]
arjunena tatas tasmād virāṭasutayā kila | [BKŚS, 17 115.2]
parīkṣit prāpnuyān mātus tato 'pi janamejayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 116.1]
iti kramāgataṃ tātas tātād āgamitaṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 17 116.2]
gāndhāragrāmasambaddhaṃ kva gāndhāraḥ kva mānuṣāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 117.1]
svargān nānyatra gāndhāra ity āhur nāradādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 117.2]
tena yo 'yaṃ na jānāti na ced abhyupagacchati | [BKŚS, 17 118.1]
tad asaṃpādayann eva jāyate doṣavān asau | [BKŚS, 17 118.2]
ahaṃ punar idaṃ jānan sadyaḥ pariṇamatphalam | [BKŚS, 17 119.1]
puro nāgarakāṇāṃ ca yathāsāmarthyam utsahe | [BKŚS, 17 119.2]
mayi saṃkalpayaty evam asau nāgarakarṣabhaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 120.1]
smayamāno vilakṣyatvāt svam evābhajatāsanam | [BKŚS, 17 120.2]
tataḥ pratihate tasmin suhṛdmaṇḍalamaṇḍane | [BKŚS, 17 121.1]
raṅgo bhaṅgam agṛhṇāt sa nigṛhyajyeṣṭhamallavat | [BKŚS, 17 121.2]
atha māṃ janitotsāham uttiṣṭhāsantam āsanāt | [BKŚS, 17 122.1]
dṛṣṭvā saṃbhāvitājñānaṃ lajjayāgrāhi dattakaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 122.2]
anyena ca nimittena calito 'haṃ kilāsanāt | [BKŚS, 17 123.1]
tenoktaṃ saṃkaṭāsthānād anyatra sthīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 123.2]
tatas tam uktavān asmi kim idaṃ na tvayā śrutam | [BKŚS, 17 124.1]
pathā sakṛt pravṛttāyāḥ kiṃ karoty avaguṇṭhanam | [BKŚS, 17 124.2]
praviṣṭo 'haṃ suhṛdgoṣṭhīṃ yathaiva baṭucāpalāt | [BKŚS, 17 125.1]
tathā gandharvadattāpi dhṛṣṭam ājñāpitā mayā | [BKŚS, 17 125.2]
tad asyā baṭuvidyāyāḥ prāntam aprāpya mādṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 126.1]
hā kaṣṭaṃ vañcito 'smīti paścāt tāpena khedyate | [BKŚS, 17 126.2]
yatra cāmī na lajjante salajjāḥ suhṛdas tava | [BKŚS, 17 127.1]
tatra nirlajjatāślāghī lajjayaiva hi lajjate | [BKŚS, 17 127.2]
samarthayati mayy evaṃ dattako 'pi niruttaraḥ | [BKŚS, 17 128.1]
aho sāhasam ity uktvā tūṣṇīṃbhāvam upeyivān | [BKŚS, 17 128.2]
aham apy āsanaṃ tyaktvā tiryak paśyati dattake | [BKŚS, 17 129.1]
pārśve gandharvadattāyā dattam āsanam āsthitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 129.2]
atha kañcukinānītāṃ vīṇāṃ dṛṣṭvāham uktavān | [BKŚS, 17 130.1]
aparānīyatām ārya naitāṃ spṛśati mādṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 130.2]
udaraṃ dṛṣṭam etasyā lūtātantunirantaram | [BKŚS, 17 131.1]
jaḍatāṃ gamitā yena paṭutantrīparaṃparā | [BKŚS, 17 131.2]
smitadarśitadantāgrair anyataḥ kṣiptadṛṣṭibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 17 132.1]
mām ālokya tathābhūtam uktaṃ nāgarakair iti | [BKŚS, 17 132.2]
brāhmaṇaḥ pūjyatām eṣa nirlajjāgrapatākayā | [BKŚS, 17 133.1]
yena sāhasam ārabdhaṃ svaguṇākhyāpanopamam | [BKŚS, 17 133.2]
tantrīkiṇakaṭhorāgrā viśīrṇakarajātatāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 134.1]
karaśākhāś ca no jātā na ca saṃbhāvanedṛśī | [BKŚS, 17 134.2]
ayaṃ tu komalāgrābhis tantrīr aṅgulibhiḥ spṛśan | [BKŚS, 17 135.1]
kadā vādayitā vīṇāṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 135.2]
sarvathāyam abhiprāyo mayaitasyopalakṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 136.1]
prītim utpādayiṣyāmi tāval locanayor iti | [BKŚS, 17 136.2]
yāvad utsāryate vīṇā yāvac cānīyate 'parā | [BKŚS, 17 137.1]
tāvad gandharvadattāyā rūpaṃ paśyāmy avāritaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 137.2]
rathyācatvarayātrāsu vakṣyāmi janasaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 17 138.1]
īdṛśī tādṛśī dṛṣṭā rūpiṇī yuvatir mayā | [BKŚS, 17 138.2]
lūtātantutataṃ cāyaṃ vīṇākarparam āha yat | [BKŚS, 17 139.1]
kiṃ tat satyaṃ mṛṣety etad devair vijñāyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 139.2]
udveṣṭite ca tat tasmin dṛṣṭaṃ veṣṭanacarmaṇi | [BKŚS, 17 140.1]
tantucakraṃ bhayodbhrāntalūtāmaṇḍalasaṃkulam | [BKŚS, 17 140.2]
atha gandharvadattāyā jātam aṅgaṃ nirīkṣya mām | [BKŚS, 17 141.1]
vepathusvedaromāñcalajjāvidhuram ākulam | [BKŚS, 17 141.2]
aparāpi mayā vīṇā samāsphālya paṭukvaṇā | [BKŚS, 17 142.1]
keśadūṣitatantrīkā prathameva vivarjitā | [BKŚS, 17 142.2]
sānudāsas tato vīṇāṃ sugandhikusumārcitām | [BKŚS, 17 143.1]
kacchapākāraphalakām ādāya svayam āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 143.2]
māṃ ca pradakṣiṇīkṛtya savikāratanūruhaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 144.1]
gandharvadattām iva tām adadāt subhagasvanām | [BKŚS, 17 144.2]
mayā tu dhautapādena vīṇāṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇām | [BKŚS, 17 145.1]
abhuktāmbarasaṃvītaṃ pīṭhapṛṣṭham adhiṣṭhitam | [BKŚS, 17 145.2]
manāk saṃspṛṣṭamātrāś ca karaśākhāmukhaiḥ svayam | [BKŚS, 17 146.1]
tantrībandhā yathāsthānam asaran dhaivatādikam | [BKŚS, 17 146.2]
tatas tantrīṣu gāndhāre jṛmbhamānāsu mantharam | [BKŚS, 17 147.1]
gandharvadattām avadaṃ bhīru saṃgīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 147.2]
sā pragalbhāpi gāndhāram ākarṇyāmaragocaram | [BKŚS, 17 148.1]
tathā ca dhṛṣṭam ādiṣṭā bālāśālīnatāṃ gatā | [BKŚS, 17 148.2]
tāṃ ca pravartayan bhītāṃ trapājanitamūkatām | [BKŚS, 17 149.1]
tad eva gītakaṃ divyam ahaṃ mandam avādayam | [BKŚS, 17 149.2]
hṛte tasyās trapāsenau saṃdarśitapathā yathā | [BKŚS, 17 150.1]
lokaṃ pāvayituṃ puṇyā prāvartata sarasvatī | [BKŚS, 17 150.2]
vṛttibhir dakṣiṇādyābhis tad gītaṃ gītakaṃ tayā | [BKŚS, 17 151.1]
upary upari pāṇyantaiḥ pāṇibhir yojitaṃ mayā | [BKŚS, 17 151.2]
āsīd idaṃ tamobhūtam aprajñātam alakṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 17 152.1]
tadgītamātraviṣayaśrotramātrajagat tadā | [BKŚS, 17 152.2]
sabhāyāṃ gāḍhamūrcchāyāṃ mṛdu tad gītavādinam | [BKŚS, 17 153.1]
paṭubhir dundubhidhvānair abhibhūtaṃ vimāninām | [BKŚS, 17 153.2]
patitāsu saratnāsu divaḥ kusumavṛṣṭiṣu | [BKŚS, 17 154.1]
kañcukī cetanāprāptān abhāṣata sabhāsadaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 154.2]
bho bho nirmatsarāḥ santaḥ satyam ākhyāta sādhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 155.1]
gītaṃ yad anayānena kiṃ tat saṃvāditaṃ na hi | [BKŚS, 17 155.2]
athodyamitahastais taiḥ samastair uktam uccakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 17 156.1]
dharmyaśulkārjitām eṣa kanyakāṃ labhatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 156.2]
tiraskariṇikāṃ nītvā tataḥ kañcukināntarā | [BKŚS, 17 157.1]
bahiṣkṛtā nāgarakā nāstikās tridivād iva | [BKŚS, 17 157.2]
nirgacchanti hatacchāyās te khaṇḍitamanorathāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 158.1]
svabhyastaguṇavaiphalyaṃ guṇinaḥ kān na tāpayet | [BKŚS, 17 158.2]
savīṇādattako 'haṃ tu śreṣṭhinābhyantarīkṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 159.1]
parīkṣya bahuśo rājñā sacivo guṇavān iva | [BKŚS, 17 159.2]
abhāṣata ca nirgacchaṃs teṣu nāgarakarṣabhaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 160.1]
yakṣīkāmuka devas tvam amānuṣaparākramaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 160.2]
vayaṃ gandharvadattā ca sānudāsaś ca sānugaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 161.1]
kṛcchrām āpadam āpannā līlayaiva tvayoddhṛtāḥ | [BKŚS, 17 161.2]
kāśmaryaḥ khadirāḥ śākāś campakāś ca saveṇavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 162.1]
ātodyāṅgārtham utkhātāḥ prarohantu yathā purā | [BKŚS, 17 162.2]
agnihotrāṇi hūyantāṃ dvijāḥ saṃdhyām upāsatām | [BKŚS, 17 163.1]
kumāryaḥ pariṇīyantāṃ prasūyantāṃ kulastriyaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 163.2]
parivrājakanirgranthabhikṣupāśupatādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 164.1]
guruvaktrābhisaṃkrāntān svasiddhāntān adhīyatām | [BKŚS, 17 164.2]
śāntavīṇopasargatvāt sakīranagarāḥ sukham | [BKŚS, 17 165.1]
sacampāmagadhāś cāṅgāḥ svasthāṅgāḥ śeratām iti | [BKŚS, 17 165.2]
tato gṛhapatir dīnaḥ prārthanābhaṅgaśaṅkayā | [BKŚS, 17 166.1]
vīṇādattakam ālokya prāvocan nīcakaistarām | [BKŚS, 17 166.2]
praśastaṃ dinam adyaivaṃ tenāyaṃ pauruṣārjitaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 167.1]
ślāghyo gandharvadattāyāḥ karaḥ saṃskriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 17 167.2]
ahaṃ tu sābhilāṣo 'pi darśitālīkadhīr ataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 168.1]
avocaṃ smitasaṃkīrṇām anāsthāmantharāṃ giram | [BKŚS, 17 168.2]
dvijo 'haṃ merukailāsatulyāmalakulodbhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 169.1]
pariṇetuṃ na me yuktam asavarṇām imām iti | [BKŚS, 17 169.2]
athoktaṃ sānudāsena viśrabdhaṃ pariṇīyatām | [BKŚS, 17 170.1]
yuṣmākaṃ hi savarṇeyam utkṛṣṭā vā bhaved iti | [BKŚS, 17 170.2]
āsīc ca mama kiṃ mattaḥ kim unmattaḥ kim ārjavaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 171.1]
ayaṃ yasmād asaṃbaddham abuddhir iva bhāṣate | [BKŚS, 17 171.2]
ahaṃ ceyaṃ ca yady asya brāhmaṇāv iti niścayaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 172.1]
tato mat katham utkṛṣṭā brāhmaṇī brāhmaṇād iyam | [BKŚS, 17 172.2]
atha imāṃ brāhmaṇīm eṣa manyate kṣatriyaṃ tu mām | [BKŚS, 17 173.1]
tathā sati kathāpy eṣā kriyamāṇā virudhyate | [BKŚS, 17 173.2]
kiṃ tu saṃbhāvyate nāyam asaṃbaddhaṃ prabhāṣitum | [BKŚS, 17 174.1]
yena dharmārthaśāstrārthakṣuṇṇadhīr iva bhāṣate | [BKŚS, 17 174.2]
agrajo 'varajāṃ bhāryāṃ svīkurvan na praduṣyati | [BKŚS, 17 175.1]
te ca svā caiva nṛpater ity uktaṃ manunā yataḥ | [BKŚS, 17 175.2]
pratyākhyānaṃ ca nitarām iyaṃ nārhati ninditam | [BKŚS, 17 176.1]
yasmād akhaṇḍitājñena dāpitā guruṇaiva me | [BKŚS, 17 176.2]
yad ahaṃ grāhitas tena vijñānam atimānuṣam | [BKŚS, 17 177.1]
dāpitā yena tenaiva tena tenaiva dāpitā | [BKŚS, 17 177.2]
na cāvaśyaparigrāhyā kumārī ciram arhati | [BKŚS, 17 178.1]
sābhilāṣā viśeṣeṇa pratyākhyānakadarthanām | [BKŚS, 17 178.2]
tasmād alaṃ mamānena nirbandheneti niścitam | [BKŚS, 17 179.1]
arthitāṃ sānudāsasya tatheti samamānayam | [BKŚS, 17 179.2]
atha vaiśravaṇasyeva sūnorākhaṇḍalātmajaḥ | [BKŚS, 17 180.1]
karaṃ gandharvadattāyāḥ sasaṃskāram upādade | [BKŚS, 17 180.2]
mandaṃ pādatalena tālam anayā yat kuṭṭayantyāciraṃ gītaṃ mām abhi visphuratkuharitaṃ tāraiḥ subhugnabhruvā | [BKŚS, 17 181.1]
tenaiva pratanūkṛtām apaharann asyāḥ krameṇa trapāṃ nirvāṇān mahatāntareṇa subhagaṃ saṃsāram ajñāsiṣam | [BKŚS, 17 181.2]
{BKŚS, 18}
gandharvadattayā sārdhaṃ divasān dattakena ca | [BKŚS, 18 1.1]
yathā rativasantābhyāṃ smaraḥ sukham ayāpayam | [BKŚS, 18 1.2]
atha gandharvadattāyāṃ gatāyāṃ vandituṃ gurūn | [BKŚS, 18 2.1]
sānudāso namaskṛtya vadati sma kṛtāsanaḥ | [BKŚS, 18 2.2]
yuṣmākaṃ hi savarṇeyam utkṛṣṭā veti yan mayā | [BKŚS, 18 3.1]
yūyaṃ vijñāpitāḥ pūrvaṃ tad etad avadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 18 3.2]
āsīd ihaiva campāyāṃ mitravarmeti vāṇijaḥ | [BKŚS, 18 4.1]
nāmitro nāpi madhyasthaḥ sādhor yasyābhavad bhuvi | [BKŚS, 18 4.2]
tasya mitravatī nāma nāmnā susadṛśī priyā | [BKŚS, 18 5.1]
bhāryā maitrīva sādhor yā śatror api hitaiṣiṇī | [BKŚS, 18 5.2]

tataḥ sa satkṛto rājñā vasanābharaṇādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 20 412.1]
prītaḥ prītaṃ mahīpālaṃ praṇipatya tiro'bhavat | [BKŚS, 20 412.2]

tantreṇa saha gacchantu campāṃ hariśikhādayaḥ | [BKŚS, 20 413.2]
rājaputrasya nāgantuṃ na sthātuṃ tatra yujyate | [BKŚS, 20 414.1]

tāvanty eva sahasrāṇi tādṛśām eva vājinām | [BKŚS, 20 415.2]

pratipakṣakṣayaṃ ghoram akarot taṃ tapantakaḥ | [BKŚS, 20 428.1]

{BKŚS, 21}
tatra mitraprakāṇḍena gomukhena vinoditaḥ | [BKŚS, 21 1.1]

avimuktāvimuktatvāt puṇyā vārāṇasī purī | [BKŚS, 21 2.2]
ā prāgjyotiṣakaśmīradvārakātāmraparṇi yat | [BKŚS, 21 3.1]

sadāsīdāsam asmākaṃ dhanam ādīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 21 70.2]

yac ca brūtha kva yāsīti tatra vijñāpayāmi vaḥ | [BKŚS, 21 104.2]

tataḥ śaṅkeṣubhinnas tām abhāṣata dṛḍhodyamaḥ | [BKŚS, 21 136.1]

tṛtīyaparihārāya tyajāmi pṛthivīm iti | [BKŚS, 21 138.2]

kālenaitāvatā nūnam akṛtyaṃ kṛtyayā kṛtam | [BKŚS, 21 140.2]

bhagavatyā yad uktaṃ tat tattvataḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 21 158.2]

brahmasthalakavāsādi yad vṛttaṃ tan niveditam | [BKŚS, 21 159.2]

sukhānāṃ copahartāraṃ mahāpāśupataṃ patim | [BKŚS, 21 164.2]

athaiko brāhmaṇas teṣu dṛḍhodyamam abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 21 166.1]
madīyā duhitā brahman rūpiṇī pariṇīyatām | [BKŚS, 21 166.2]
dhanaṃ me dhanadasyeva saiva caikā sutā yataḥ | [BKŚS, 21 167.1]
tatas tasya ca tasyāś ca bhaved bhartā bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 21 167.2]
āsīc cāsya kim adyāpi syān na syād iti cintayā | [BKŚS, 21 168.1]
parivrājakavākyaṃ hi kṛtārthīkṛtam etayā | [BKŚS, 21 168.2]
pratijñāya ca tāṃ kanyāṃ dadānād brāhmaṇāt svayam | [BKŚS, 21 169.1]
samahādraviṇaskandhām upayeme dṛḍhodyamaḥ | [BKŚS, 21 169.2]
tamālikāpi saṃhārya keśān kāṣāyacīvarā | [BKŚS, 21 170.1]
dṛḍhodyamagṛhāsannā vasatī kālam akṣipat | [BKŚS, 21 170.2]
dṛḍhodyamo 'pi saṃtataṃ dvijātikarma sādhayan | [BKŚS, 21 171.1]
harottamāṅgalālitām upāsta jahnukanyakām | [BKŚS, 21 171.2]
tat tena yena kṛtaduṣkarapauruṣeṇa vākyaṃ na bhinnatamasaḥ kṛtam apramāṇam | [BKŚS, 21 172.1]
śūreṇa daivahariṇā prabhuṇā prasahya tasmāj jitaḥ puruṣakāragajādhirājaḥ | [BKŚS, 21 172.2]
{BKŚS, 22}
tataḥ kiṃcid vihasyoktaḥ parivrāḍ brahmacāriṇā | [BKŚS, 22 1.1]
yathā puruṣakārasya prādhānyaṃ tan niśāmyatām | [BKŚS, 22 1.2]
āsīd ujjayanīvāsī sārthakārthaparigrahaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 2.1]
vaṇik sāgaradattākhyaḥ sāgarāgādhamānasaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 2.2]
sāgaraṃ tena yātena muktapotena gacchatā | [BKŚS, 22 3.1]
aparaḥ prekṣitaḥ potas taraladhvajalakṣaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 3.2]
aṅgāpotam amuṃ yena potaṃ prerayateti saḥ | [BKŚS, 22 4.1]
yāvan niryāmakān āha tāvat potau samīyatuḥ | [BKŚS, 22 4.2]
tataḥ sāgaradattas taṃ potasvāminam uktavān | [BKŚS, 22 5.1]
yūyaṃ ye vā yatas tyā vā tan naḥ pratyucyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 5.2]
tenoktaṃ buddhavarmāhaṃ vaṇig rājagṛhālayaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 6.1]
bhavantaḥ ke kuto veti tataḥ so 'pi nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 22 6.2]
atha kāvyakathāpānatantrīgītadurodaraiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 7.1]
savinodau jagāhāte tau durgādhaṃ mahodadhim | [BKŚS, 22 7.2]
gatvā ca kāñcanadvīpam upāntānantakāñcanau | [BKŚS, 22 8.1]
prāptavantau parāvṛtya samudrataṭapattanam | [BKŚS, 22 8.2]
atha sāgaradattena buddhavarmeti bhāṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 9.1]
prītir naḥ sthiratāṃ yāyād yathā saṃpādyatāṃ tathā | [BKŚS, 22 9.2]
bhāryāyāṃ gurugarbhāyāṃ niragaccham ahaṃ gṛhāt | [BKŚS, 22 10.1]
tasyāś ca divasir ebhir jātam anyatarad dvayoḥ | [BKŚS, 22 10.2]
duhitā cet tato dattā bhavatputrāya sā mayā | [BKŚS, 22 11.1]
putraś cet tvaṃ tatas tasmai dadyāḥ svatanayām iti | [BKŚS, 22 11.2]
tenoktaṃ mahad āścaryam iyam eva hi no matiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 12.1]
athavā kim ihāścaryam ekam evāvayor vapuḥ | [BKŚS, 22 12.2]
iti tau kṛtasaṃbandhau pariṣvajya parasparam | [BKŚS, 22 13.1]
mahāmahiṣasārthābhyāṃ yathāsthānam agacchatām | [BKŚS, 22 13.2]
praṇipatya ca rājānāv avantimagadhādhipau | [BKŚS, 22 14.1]
tatprayuktātisatkārau yayatuḥ svagṛhān prati | [BKŚS, 22 14.2]
tatra satkriyamāṇau ca satkurvāṇau ca saṃtatam | [BKŚS, 22 15.1]
bandhubhir brāhmaṇādīṃś ca gamayāmāsatur dinam | [BKŚS, 22 15.2]
tataḥ sāgaradattasya paryaṅkam adhitiṣṭhataḥ | [BKŚS, 22 16.1]
utsaṅge dārikā nyastā virājatkundamālikā | [BKŚS, 22 16.2]
kasyeyaṃ kundamāleti sa bhāryām anuyuktavān | [BKŚS, 22 17.1]
sāpi kasyāparasyeti śanair ācaṣṭa lajjitā | [BKŚS, 22 17.2]
tena coktam idaṃ yādṛg bālikā kundamālikā | [BKŚS, 22 18.1]
yayoḥ syād īdṛśaḥ putraḥ pitarau tau saputrakau | [BKŚS, 22 18.2]
tasmād duhitṛmāteti mā gās tvaṃ bhīru bhīrutām | [BKŚS, 22 19.1]
na kīrtijananī vidyā nindyā bhavitum arhati | [BKŚS, 22 19.2]
tām ityādi samāśvasya payonidhisamāgamam | [BKŚS, 22 20.1]
buddhavarmasakhitvaṃ ca tasyai kathitavān asau | [BKŚS, 22 20.2]
kasyeyaṃ kundamāleti tām apṛcchad yataḥ pitā | [BKŚS, 22 21.1]
prasiddhā tasya nāmnāpi sā tataḥ kundamālikā | [BKŚS, 22 21.2]
buddhavarmāpi papraccha nirālāpāṃ kuṭumbinīm | [BKŚS, 22 22.1]
tasmin garbhe tavotpannaṃ yat tan naḥ kathyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 22.2]
atha vāmanam ekākṣaṃ rūkṣaṃ tundiladanturam | [BKŚS, 22 23.1]
lambauṣṭhaṃ bhugnapṛṣṭhaṃ ca sā taṃ putraṃ samarpayat | [BKŚS, 22 23.2]
so 'bravīt kiṃ vṛthaivāyaṃ dhṛtaḥ kurubhakas tvayā | [BKŚS, 22 24.1]
kasmād īkṣaṇikāṃ pṛṣṭvā garbha eva na pātitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 24.2]
yaḥ sa sāgaradattena saha saṃbandhakaḥ kṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 25.1]
vikṛtākṛtinānena sa pretena nirākṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 25.2]
saṃdiśed yadi nāmāsāv ahaṃ duhitṛvān iti | [BKŚS, 22 26.1]
tadā kiṃ pratisaṃdeśyaṃ mayāhaṃ putravān iti | [BKŚS, 22 26.2]
bhāryāṃ cāvocad āgacched dūto mālavakād yadi | [BKŚS, 22 27.1]
enaṃ kurubhakaṃ tasmai na kaścit kathayed iti | [BKŚS, 22 27.2]
ayaṃ kurubhakaḥ kasmād iti yat taṃ pitābravīt | [BKŚS, 22 28.1]
vyāharanti sma taṃ paurās tataḥ kurubhakākhyayā | [BKŚS, 22 28.2]
athātīte kvacit kāle buddhivarmā rahaḥ sthitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 29.1]
lekhaṃ sāgaradattena prasthāpitam avācayat | [BKŚS, 22 29.2]
sv asti rājagṛhe pūjyaṃ buddhavarmāṇam ūrjitam | [BKŚS, 22 30.1]
ujjayanyāḥ pariṣvajya vijñāpayati sāgaraḥ | [BKŚS, 22 30.2]
sakhyās te duhitā jātā śreyolakṣaṇabhūṣaṇā | [BKŚS, 22 31.1]
rūpeṇa sadṛśī yasyāḥ pramadā na bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 22 31.2]
tavāpi yadi bhāryāyāḥ putro jātaḥ śivaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 22 32.1]
kanyā ced vāmaśīlena devena muṣitā vayam | [BKŚS, 22 32.2]
nirnimittāpi hi prītir yā na saṃbandhabṛṃhitā | [BKŚS, 22 33.1]
śrīr utsāhasanātheva prayāti sthiratām iti | [BKŚS, 22 33.2]
tataḥ satkṛtya taṃ dūtam apṛcchad gṛhiṇīṃ vaṇik | [BKŚS, 22 34.1]
tasminn evaṃ gate kārye brūhi kiṃ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 34.2]
tayoktaṃ dvyaṅgulaprajñā jānīyur vā striyaḥ kiyat | [BKŚS, 22 35.1]
kiṃ tu pṛṣṭeti vakṣyāmi pṛṣṭadhṛṣṭā hi mādṛśī | [BKŚS, 22 35.2]
satyānṛtaṃ vaṇigvṛttaṃ parityājyaṃ na vāṇijaiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 36.1]
sahajaṃ hi tyajan vṛttaṃ durvṛtta iti nindyate | [BKŚS, 22 36.2]
putras tāvat tavotpannas tatra kānṛtavāditā | [BKŚS, 22 37.1]
ye punas tasya doṣās tān mithyā bhaṇa guṇā iti | [BKŚS, 22 37.2]
ākhyāyante hi sarvārthāḥ kṛtrimair eva nāmabhiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 38.1]
āhur madhurakaṃ kecit taṃ tādṛṅmārakaṃ viṣam | [BKŚS, 22 38.2]
kārye hi guruṇi prāpte mithyā satyam apīṣyate | [BKŚS, 22 39.1]
aśvatthāmā hato drauṇir ity ūce kiṃ na pāṇḍavaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 39.2]
dhanagardhaparādhīnāḥ kālahuṃkāradāruṇe | [BKŚS, 22 40.1]

sāṃyātrikapates tasya duhitā bhavato gṛhe | [BKŚS, 22 41.1]
na vināmbhodhisāreṇa praveṣṭā dhanarāśinā | [BKŚS, 22 41.2]
tasmān mā smāvamanyadhvam adhanyair durlabhāṃ śriyam | [BKŚS, 22 42.1]
kṛcchrāyāsaśataprāpyāṃ na kṛcchrādhigatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 42.2]
ityādivacanaṃ tasyāḥ sūktam ity abhinandya saḥ | [BKŚS, 22 43.1]
dadau sāgaradattāya saṃdeśaṃ dūtasaṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 22 43.2]
vaktavyaḥ suhṛd asmākam asmākam api dārakaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 44.1]
utpannas tādṛśo yasya kathitā katham ākṛtiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 44.2]
athavā ye guṇāḥ ke'pi tasya śārīramānasāḥ | [BKŚS, 22 45.1]
svayam evāsi tān dṛṣṭā kiṃ nas taiḥ kathitair iti | [BKŚS, 22 45.2]

dūtaṃ prasthāpayāmāsa sapātheyapradeśanam | [BKŚS, 22 46.2]

atha dūtaḥ sphuṭālāpo buddhavarmāṇam uktavān | [BKŚS, 22 47.2]
ahaṃ sāgaradattena sakalatreṇa bhāṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 48.1]
jāmātaram anālokya mā smāgacchad bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 22 48.2]

taṃ me dārakam ākhyāta tadīyāṃś ca guṇān iti | [BKŚS, 22 49.2]

āste mātulaśāle 'sau tāmraliptyāṃ paṭhann iti | [BKŚS, 22 50.2]

adyāpi ca na paśyāmo vayaṃ jāmātur ākṛtim | [BKŚS, 22 53.2]

idam apy atidurbaddhaṃ savyājam iva vācakam | [BKŚS, 22 55.2]

tān uktvā gṛhiṇīm ūce buddhavarmā sasaṃbhramaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 59.2]

dūrāśāgrastacittena pramadāvacanaṃ kṛtam | [BKŚS, 22 60.2]

sutarām upacīyante śarīrāvayavā iva | [BKŚS, 22 62.2]

athavā paṇḍitenaivam upāyaś cintyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 63.2]

yady asau rocate tubhyaṃ tataḥ prastūyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 64.2]

tatas tair vismitair uktam anindyā kundamālikā | [BKŚS, 22 78.1]
saha bālavasantena yad anena sameṣyati | [BKŚS, 22 78.2]
guṇānāṃ tv etadīyānām anveṣaṇam anarthakam | [BKŚS, 22 79.1]

tatrāsya śvaśurau syālāḥ syālabhāryāś ca sātmajāḥ | [BKŚS, 22 298.1]
āptāś ca śreṣṭhinaḥ paurāḥ paritaḥ samupāviśan | [BKŚS, 22 298.2]
sāthāgacchad vaṇikkanyā madhurābharaṇakvaṇā | [BKŚS, 22 299.1]
vācālakalahaṃseva niṣkalaṅkāmbarā śarat | [BKŚS, 22 299.2]
guravaḥ satkṛtā mūrdhnā vācā savayasas tayā | [BKŚS, 22 300.1]
yajñaguptaḥ punar dṛṣṭyā sarāgāñjanagarbhayā | [BKŚS, 22 300.2]
adhyāsya ca puraḥ pitror asau vāmanam āsanam | [BKŚS, 22 301.1]
vivāhādiyathāvṛttam ātmavṛttaṃ nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 22 301.2]
āsīc ca yajñaguptasya dhig dhiṅ me viphalāḥ kalāḥ | [BKŚS, 22 302.1]
dvyaṅgulaprajñayā yo 'haṃ vañcitaḥ kulakanyayā | [BKŚS, 22 302.2]
athavā dvyaṅgulaprajñāḥ puruṣā eva mādṛśāḥ | [BKŚS, 22 303.1]
kuśāgrīyadhiyo yoṣā yāsāṃ karmesam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 22 303.2]
kim ataḥ paramāścaryaṃ yan nāgarikayānayā | [BKŚS, 22 304.1]
tiṣṭhatāṃ gatisaṃsthāne svaro 'pi parivartitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 304.2]
virāṭanagare pārthaiḥ kathaṃ mūḍhātmabhiḥ sthitam | [BKŚS, 22 305.1]
iti ye vicikitseyus teṣām eṣā nidarśanam | [BKŚS, 22 305.2]
sarvathā guruvākyena yan mayā caritaṃ mahat | [BKŚS, 22 306.1]
tasmād asmy anayaivādya mocitaḥ pātakād iti | [BKŚS, 22 306.2]
vṛttāntaṃ caitad ākarṇya prahṛṣṭena mahībhṛtā | [BKŚS, 22 307.1]
sahajāmātṛkānītā svagṛhaṃ kundamālikā | [BKŚS, 22 307.2]
tasmin bahumahāgrāmaṃ dānaṃ bahusuvarṇakam | [BKŚS, 22 308.1]
sa dattvā yajñaguptāya sasmitas tām abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 22 308.2]
yathā dvijātikarmabhyo na hīyate patis tava | [BKŚS, 22 309.1]
tvayā dhīratayā putri tathā saṃpādyatām iti | [BKŚS, 22 309.2]
tayātidhairyāṅkuśavāriterṣyayā dvijātikanyāṃ pariṇāyitaḥ patiḥ | [BKŚS, 22 310.1]
na hi kṣitīśān avilaṅghyaśāsanān vilaṅghayanti priyajīvitaśriyaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 310.2]
dvijātikanyāṃ ratiputrakāmyayā sukhāya śuddhāya ca kundamālikām | [BKŚS, 22 311.1]
niṣevamānaḥ sukṛtaṃ ca saṃtataṃ nināya vipraḥ saphalaṃ samāśatam | [BKŚS, 22 311.2]
paugaṇḍāya vitīrṇayāpi vidhinā yasmād vaṇikkanyayā citropāyaparaṃparācaturayā prāptaḥ patir vāñchitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 312.1]
saṃtoṣakṣatasattvasattvadayitaḥ saṃsevitaḥ kātarais tasmāt pauruṣamārutena balinā daivādrir unmūlitaḥ | [BKŚS, 22 312.2]
{BKŚS, 23}
ity ākhyāya kathitau ca mithaḥ pravrajitau gatau | [BKŚS, 23 1.1]
drutapravahaṇārūḍho gomukhaś ca parāgataḥ | [BKŚS, 23 1.2]
mām avocat sa vanditvā prītidāsaḥ punarvasuḥ | [BKŚS, 23 2.1]
sarvanāgarakaśreṇigrāmaṇīr dṛśyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 2.2]
atha praṇatam adrākṣam anulbaṇavibhūṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 23 3.1]
yuvānam api vainītyāllajjitasthaviraṃ naram | [BKŚS, 23 3.2]
gomukhākhyātamāhātmyaṃ taṃ cāliṅgitavān aham | [BKŚS, 23 4.1]
saṃbhāvitaguṇāḥ sadbhir arhanty eva ca satkriyām | [BKŚS, 23 4.2]
atha yānaṃ samāruhya tat punarvasuvāhakam | [BKŚS, 23 5.1]
sāṃyātrika ivāmbhodhiṃ tadāvāsam avātaram | [BKŚS, 23 5.2]
sevitāhāraparyantaśarīrasthitisādhanaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 6.1]
dinaśeṣaṃ nayāmi sma gītiśrutivinodanaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 6.2]

katham eṣa tvayā prāptaḥ suhṛd ity atha so 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 23 7.2]
śrūyatām asty ahaṃ yuṣmān vanditvā punar āgataḥ | [BKŚS, 23 8.1]
na ca kaṃcana paśyāmi yogyam āśrayadāyinam | [BKŚS, 23 8.2]
tataś cintitavān asmi dhanavidyādidāyinām | [BKŚS, 23 9.1]

rājadvāraṃ vigāhante samudram iva sindhavaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 10.2]

nigrahānugrahaprāptalokakolāhalākulam | [BKŚS, 23 12.1]

āśrayaprārthanā tasmān nāsmin sampadyate mṛṣā | [BKŚS, 23 13.2]
ayam anyaḥ suveṣo 'pi kīnāśavirasākṛtiḥ | [BKŚS, 23 14.1]
tena saṃbhāvyate nāsmāt prārthanāphalam aṇv api | [BKŚS, 23 14.2]
puruṣaṃ puruṣaṃ tatra ciram itthaṃ vicārayan | [BKŚS, 23 15.1]
abhyantarāt pratīhāraṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi nirgatam | [BKŚS, 23 15.2]
svastikāranamaskārajyotkārān sa ca kāryiṇām | [BKŚS, 23 16.1]
pratimānitavān sarvān sakṛn namitamastakaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 16.2]
atha vijñāpanāmātraṃ paśyadbhiḥ kāryasādhanam | [BKŚS, 23 17.1]
kāryibhir yugapat tatra kāryavijñāpanā kṛtā | [BKŚS, 23 17.2]
tebhyas tenāpi sāmānyam ekam evottaraṃ kṛtam | [BKŚS, 23 18.1]
bhavataḥ sumukho rājā mā tvariṣṭa bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 23 18.2]
sa pratīhāraveṣaṃ ca vārabāṇādim aṅgataḥ | [BKŚS, 23 19.1]
avatārya samīpasthe nyastavān paricārake | [BKŚS, 23 19.2]
taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā samāptaiva samāśrayagaveṣaṇā | [BKŚS, 23 20.1]

svastikṛtvā tatas tasmai svagṛhān pratigacchate | [BKŚS, 23 21.1]

gṛhe ca kṛtasatkāram asau mām anuyuktavān | [BKŚS, 23 22.1]
āgacchati kutaḥ kiṃ vā mad icchati bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 23 22.2]
mayoktaṃ bhrātarāv āvāṃ dvijau dvāv āgamārthinau | [BKŚS, 23 23.1]
vidyāsthānam idaṃ śrutvā avantideśāt samāgatau | [BKŚS, 23 23.2]
iha vāsitum icchāvo yuṣmatkṛtaparigrahau | [BKŚS, 23 24.1]

vyasanī ca svatantraś ca so 'smākam adhunā suhṛt | [BKŚS, 23 33.2]

sarasīvāmiṣāsvādagṛddhair bakakadambakaiḥ | [BKŚS, 23 35.2]
tatrānyatamayor akṣān dīvyator akṣadhūrtayoḥ | [BKŚS, 23 36.1]

tayor ekatareṇoktaṃ madhyasthaḥ pṛcchyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 38.1]

yo 'haṃ trailokyasāreṇa paṇena paṇavān iti | [BKŚS, 23 57.2]
atha nikṣipya sakrodhaṃ yauṣmākaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhuvi | [BKŚS, 23 58.1]
