tvadanyasya gṛhe nānnam aryajyeṣṭhena sevitam | [BKŚS, 23 84.1]
parapākanivṛttā hi sādhuvṛttā dvijātayaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 84.2]
ādarārādhitaś cāyaṃ tvadīyaṃ paribhuktavān | [BKŚS, 23 85.1]
ārādhanānurodho hi caritaṃ mahatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 85.2]
pratyākhyānavicittas tu tam āha sma punarvasuḥ | [BKŚS, 23 86.1]
yady evaṃ jagadīśānāṃ kiṃ nāsti bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 86.2]
acirāc ca tadānītau saṃbhāvyaguṇasaṃpadau | [BKŚS, 23 87.1]
ākārakṣiptanāsatyāv apaśyaṃ puruṣau puraḥ | [BKŚS, 23 87.2]
tau ca māṃ ciram ālokya vadanaṃ ca parasparam | [BKŚS, 23 88.1]
prasārya sabhujān pādāñ jayety uktvā bhuvaṃ gatau | [BKŚS, 23 88.2]
tau cāhūya mayāyātau spṛṣṭapṛṣṭhau sabhājitau | [BKŚS, 23 89.1]
vanditvā punar abrūtāṃ brūta kiṃ kriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 89.2]
tatas tau gomukhenoktau bhavantau kila ballavau | [BKŚS, 23 90.1]
satyaṃ ced idam āryasya pākaḥ saṃsādhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 90.2]
tau ca prītau pratijñāya nikartya nakhamūrdhajān | [BKŚS, 23 91.1]
snātau soṣṇīṣamūrdhānau mahānasam agacchatām | [BKŚS, 23 91.2]
athavā tiṣṭhati vyāsaḥ samāsaḥ śrūyatām ayam | [BKŚS, 23 92.1]
sarvā tābhyām apūrveva prakriyā samprasāritā | [BKŚS, 23 92.2]
yāvatyā cāparaḥ sthālīm adhiśrayati ballavaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 93.1]
tāvatyā velayā tābhyāṃ pāka eva samāpitaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 93.2]
tato nirvartitasnānadevatānalatarpaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 94.1]
āhārasthānam adhyāsi viprapaṅktinirantaram | [BKŚS, 23 94.2]
pañca tittirayaḥ pakvāś catvāraḥ kukkuṭā iti | [BKŚS, 23 95.1]
āhāro yaiḥ praśastas tair aśitaṃ prākṛtāśanam | [BKŚS, 23 95.2]
āhāraṃ yadi severan sakṛt tam amṛtāśanam | [BKŚS, 23 96.1]
samutsṛṣṭāmṛtāhārā bhaveyur nāmarās tadā | [BKŚS, 23 96.2]
tataḥ samāpitāhāraḥ karṇe gomukham abravam | [BKŚS, 23 97.1]
sūdābhyāṃ bhuktabhaktābhyām ayutaṃ dīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 97.2]
sa gatvā sahitas tābhyāṃ cirāc cāgatya kevalaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 98.1]
smitasaṃsūcitaprītir upākramata bhāṣitum | [BKŚS, 23 98.2]
mayā yāv uditāv etau na yuvām etad arhatha | [BKŚS, 23 99.1]
avasthāsādṛśaṃ kiṃtu yat kiṃcid gṛhyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 99.2]
tayor ekatareṇātha bhartur dauḥsthityavartinaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 100.1]
na yuktaṃ dhanam ādātum āvābhyām iti bhāṣitam | [BKŚS, 23 100.2]
sa kruddhenetareṇokto dhik tvāṃ dīnatarāśayam | [BKŚS, 23 101.1]
jitatrailokyavitteśaṃ vitteśaṃ yo 'nukampase | [BKŚS, 23 101.2]
mahāpadmasahasrāṇi yat prasādād vimāninām | [BKŚS, 23 102.1]
susthitāni bhaviṣyanti dauḥsthityaṃ tasya kīdṛśam | [BKŚS, 23 102.2]
prayacchaty ayutaṃ yaś ca pākasyaikasya niṣkrayam | [BKŚS, 23 103.1]
duḥsthitas tādṛśo yasya susthitas tasya kīdṛśaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 103.2]
evamādi bruvann eva sa mālyam iva tad dhanam | [BKŚS, 23 104.1]
dhārayitvā kṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnā prasthāya prāptavān gṛham | [BKŚS, 23 104.2]
athainaṃ pṛṣṭavān asmi paṭukautūhalākulaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 105.1]
divyam aiśvaryam āgāmi kathaṃ veda bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 23 105.2]
tatas tenoktam asyaiva brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ | [BKŚS, 23 106.1]
śatayajñādhikaśrīkaḥ pañcayajñaḥ pitābhavat | [BKŚS, 23 106.2]
cikitsāsūdaśāstrajñaḥ śilpitve 'py aśaṭho 'bhavat | [BKŚS, 23 107.1]
dvitīya iva tasyātmā devavān iti ballavaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 107.2]
śarīram etad āyattaṃ mameti kṛtabuddhinā | [BKŚS, 23 108.1]
rājñā tasmai svarājyasya daśamo 'ṃśaḥ prakalpitaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 108.2]
nandopanandanāmānau tasya sūdapateḥ sutau | [BKŚS, 23 109.1]
īdṛśākāravijñānāv āvām eva ca viddhi tau | [BKŚS, 23 109.2]
bālābhyām eva cāvābhyāṃ sūdaśāstracikitsite | [BKŚS, 23 110.1]
sahajñānaprayogābhyāṃ kulavidyeti śikṣite | [BKŚS, 23 110.2]
ekadā nau pitāvocat putrakau śṛṇutaṃ hitam | [BKŚS, 23 111.1]
śrotāraṃ guruvākyānāṃ na spṛśanti vipattayaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 111.2]
padavākyapramāṇāni kāvyāni vividhāni ca | [BKŚS, 23 112.1]
bhavadbhyāṃ śikṣitavyāni citrādiś ca kalāgaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 112.2]
kadācid ajitaṃ jetuṃ yāto yātavyamaṇḍalam | [BKŚS, 23 113.1]
śāstrakāvyakathālāpair vinodaṃ prabhur icchati | [BKŚS, 23 113.2]
vijñāya tu tadāsthānam asaṃnihitapaṇḍitam | [BKŚS, 23 114.1]
vinodaṃ tasya kuryātaṃ śāstrālāpādibhir yuvām | [BKŚS, 23 114.2]
pragalbhāḥ pratibhāvanto bahuvṛttāntapaṇḍitāḥ | [BKŚS, 23 115.1]
prakāśitamanovṛttair bhṛtyāḥ krīḍanti bhartṛbhiḥ | [BKŚS, 23 115.2]
ekavidyaḥ punas tatra pragalbho 'pi tapasvikaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 116.1]
svavidyālāpaparyāyakhinnaś ciram udīkṣate | [BKŚS, 23 116.2]
abhyastabahuvidyaś ca nirviparyāyamānasaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 117.1]
gatasaṃśayaduḥkhatvāt sukhināṃ parameśvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 23 117.2]
utsāhena ca śikṣethām āyuraiśvaryalakṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 23 118.1]
dīrghāyurvittavanto hi saṃsevyāḥ sevakair iti | [BKŚS, 23 118.2]
tac ca pitrājñayāśeṣam āvābhyām anuśīlitam | [BKŚS, 23 119.1]
ramyāsvādaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca ko 'vamanyeta bheṣajam | [BKŚS, 23 119.2]
tad vidyādharacakrasya cakravartī bhaviṣyati | [BKŚS, 23 120.1]
jyaiṣṭhacandrasahasrāṃśudīrghāyuś ceti nau matiḥ | [BKŚS, 23 120.2]
tena prasāritāṅgābhyām āvābhyām eṣa vanditaḥ | [BKŚS, 23 121.1]
na hi vandanasāmānyam arhanti bahuvanditāḥ | [BKŚS, 23 121.2]
bahavo hīha tiṣṭhanti brāhmaṇās tīrthakukkuṭāḥ | [BKŚS, 23 122.1]
śiraḥspandanamātreṇa tān āvāṃ pūjayāvahe | [BKŚS, 23 122.2]
tasmād yasmād asaṅgena sarvatrāgamacakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 23 123.1]
jyeṣṭhasya dṛṣṭam aiśvaryam ataḥ śraddhīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 23 123.2]
prajñaptikauśikasutapramukhair uktaṃ nandasya niścitataraṃ vacanāt tad āsīt | [BKŚS, 23 124.1]
bhāvaṃ hi saṃśayatamaḥpaṭalāpinaddham udbhāvayanty avitathā vacanapradīpāḥ | [BKŚS, 23 124.2]
{BKŚS, 24}
atha nandopanandābhyāṃ sevyamānaḥ svakarmaṇā | [BKŚS, 24 1.1]
punarvasugṛhe stokān divasān avasaṃ sukhī | [BKŚS, 24 1.2]
kadācin mandirāgrasthaḥ kurvann āśāvalokanam | [BKŚS, 24 2.1]
śramaṇāṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi śiṣyāsaṃghapuraḥsarīm | [BKŚS, 24 2.2]
kavibhis tair anātmajñair buddhir āyāsyate vṛthā | [BKŚS, 24 3.1]
ye tasyā varṇasaṃsthāne varṇayanti hatatrapāḥ | [BKŚS, 24 3.2]
sarvathā taṃ vidhātāraṃ dhig yat kiṃcanakāriṇam | [BKŚS, 24 4.1]
yenākāraviruddho 'syām ācāro durbhagaḥ kṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 4.2]
sarvo hi viniyogārtham arthaḥ sarveṇa sṛjyate | [BKŚS, 24 5.1]
ghaṭayitvā ghaṭaḥ kena loṣṭena śakalīkṛtaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 5.2]
dhātrā punar iyaṃ sṛṣṭā komaleva mṛṇālinī | [BKŚS, 24 6.1]
śoṣitā tuhineneti dhik tasya khalatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 6.2]
tatas tāṃ ciram ālokya nirnimiṣeṇa cakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 24 7.1]
gomukhaḥ sphuritotsāhaḥ pṛcchati sma punarvasum | [BKŚS, 24 7.2]
alaṃkṛtapurīmārgair ūrugauravamantharaiḥ | [BKŚS, 24 8.1]
eṣā pravrajitā bhadra kva gacchati gatair iti | [BKŚS, 24 8.2]
tenoktam ṛṣidatteyam ārhataṃ dharmam āsthitā | [BKŚS, 24 9.1]
vītarāgatayā siddhān atiśete jinān api | [BKŚS, 24 9.2]
eṣā bālasakhīṃ dṛṣṭvā satataṃ rājadārikām | [BKŚS, 24 10.1]
kanyakāntaḥpurād eti yāti svaśayanāsanam | [BKŚS, 24 10.2]
ityādi kathayitvāsāv ṛṣidattām avandata | [BKŚS, 24 11.1]
ambike sahaśiṣyāyās te namo 'stu namo 'stv iti | [BKŚS, 24 11.2]
taṃ ca pravrajitāvocad asaṃbhāṣyo bhavān iti | [BKŚS, 24 12.1]
kimartham iti tenokte tayoktam avadhīyatām | [BKŚS, 24 12.2]
jñānādhikṣiptasarvajñau rūpavismāritasmarau | [BKŚS, 24 13.1]
dvijau jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhākhyau tvadgṛhe kila tiṣṭhataḥ | [BKŚS, 24 13.2]
tatsaṃdarśanasaṃbhāṣājanitaṃ ca sukhaṃ tvayā | [BKŚS, 24 14.1]
draviṇaṃ kṛpaṇeneva pracchannam upabhujyate | [BKŚS, 24 14.2]
suhṛtsādhāraṇaṃ yasya sukhaṃ sa paramaṃ sukhī | [BKŚS, 24 15.1]
sukhasaṃvaraṇāyāsād viparītas tu duḥkhitaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 15.2]
suhṛdbhiḥ kupitais tasmād asaṃbhāṣyaḥ kṛto bhavān | [BKŚS, 24 16.1]
teṣām atrānayopāyaḥ samarthaś cintyatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 16.2]
athoccair gomukhenoktam acireṇa punarvasuḥ | [BKŚS, 24 17.1]
sahanandopanandaśca jināyatanamaṇḍapam | [BKŚS, 24 18.2]
arhatas tatra vanditvā saṃghaṃ cīvaravāsasam | [BKŚS, 24 19.1]
ṛṣidattāṃ ca tad datte viṣṭare samupāviśam | [BKŚS, 24 19.2]
avalambitabāhus tu muktakakṣaś ca gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 20.1]
sthitvā devakuladvāre jinastotram udāharat | [BKŚS, 24 20.2]
namo 'stu sarvasiddhebhyaḥ sādhubhyaś ca namo 'stu vaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 21.1]
ṛṣabhapramukhebhyaś ca sarvajñebhyo namo 'stv iti | [BKŚS, 24 21.2]
sādhu śrāvaka dhanyo 'si yaḥ sarvajñaṃ namasyasi | [BKŚS, 24 22.1]
ityādi bahu nirgranthāḥ prītyāstuvata gomukham | [BKŚS, 24 22.2]
athāyam ṛṣidattāyāḥ pādau gāḍhaṃ nipīḍayan | [BKŚS, 24 23.1]
abravīt suprasannau me bhavantau bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 23.2]
tayā tv asya prayuktāśīr asmākaṃ laghuśāsane | [BKŚS, 24 24.1]
śrāvakasyāpi saṃvādyā pratipattir bhavatv iti | [BKŚS, 24 24.2]
athoktam upanandena vīṇāgoṣṭhī pravartyatām | [BKŚS, 24 25.1]
eṣa saṃnihitaḥ saṃghaḥ sakalaḥ suhṛdām iti | [BKŚS, 24 25.2]
anyenoktam anāyāte pravīṇe gaṅgarakṣite | [BKŚS, 24 26.1]
asaṃnihitahaṃseva nalinī nīravā sabhā | [BKŚS, 24 26.2]
tasmān mahāpratīhāraṃ bhavanto gaṅgarakṣitam | [BKŚS, 24 27.1]
udīkṣantām iti tataḥ samprāpto gaṅgarakṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 27.2]
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nāgarair uktam āryajyeṣṭhasya vāsya vā | [BKŚS, 24 28.1]
ākhyāta nipuṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā kataro rūpavān iti | [BKŚS, 24 28.2]
āsīc ca mama yat satyaṃ satyam evāsmi rūpavān | [BKŚS, 24 29.1]
gaṅgarakṣitarūpeṇa rūpaṃ me sadṛśaṃ yataḥ | [BKŚS, 24 29.2]
yadīyam etadīyena rūpeṇāpy upacaryate | [BKŚS, 24 30.1]
upamānam upādeyaḥ so 'pi rūpavatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 30.2]
vanditvā jinam agranthān ṛṣidattāṃ ca māṃ ca saḥ | [BKŚS, 24 31.1]
upāviśat punaś coktam upanandena pūrvavat | [BKŚS, 24 31.2]
tataḥ pravrajitāha sma śreṣṭhini priyadarśane | [BKŚS, 24 32.1]
anāyāte sadaḥ sarvam idam apriyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 24 32.2]
ataḥ pratīkṣyatāṃ śreṣṭhī kṣaṇam ity uditekṣayā | [BKŚS, 24 33.1]
ayam āyāta ity ākhyan nāgarāḥ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 24 33.2]
āsīc ca mama taṃ dṛṣṭvā naivāyaṃ priyadarśanaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 34.1]
eṣā puruṣaveṣeṇa bhūṣitā priyadarśanā | [BKŚS, 24 34.2]
straiṇībhir gatisaṃsthānavāṇībhir vyaktam etayā | [BKŚS, 24 35.1]
kṣiptatrailokyasaundaryam ākhyātaṃ straiṇam ātmanaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 35.2]
sā tu vanditadevādiḥ sādaraṃ mām avandata | [BKŚS, 24 36.1]
ciraṃ sundari jīveti mayāpi prativanditā | [BKŚS, 24 36.2]
tataḥ krodhāruṇākṣeṇa gomukhenāham īkṣataḥ | [BKŚS, 24 37.1]
citraṃ nāgarakaiḥ kaiścil lajjitaiḥ kaiścid ambaram | [BKŚS, 24 37.2]
ṛṣidattā punaḥ sāsraṃ savikāsacalekṣaṇā | [BKŚS, 24 38.1]
sagomukham apaśyan mām ā śiraścaraṇaṃ ciram | [BKŚS, 24 38.2]
atha prapañcam ākṣeptum etaṃ sapadi gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 39.1]
abhāṣata suhṛdvargaṃ goṣṭhī prastūyatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 39.2]
upanandas tataḥ pūrvaṃ tathā vīṇām avādayat | [BKŚS, 24 40.1]
yathā vigatarāgād yair nirgranthair api mūrchitam | [BKŚS, 24 40.2]
upanandāt tato nandaṃ nandād api punarvasum | [BKŚS, 24 41.1]
punarvasor agād vīṇā kramāt taṃ gaṅgarakṣitam | [BKŚS, 24 41.2]
upanandādikānāṃ ca jitanāradaparvatam | [BKŚS, 24 42.1]
parājayata dūreṇa pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ paraḥ paraḥ | [BKŚS, 24 42.2]
kramaprāptā tato vīṇā gomukhaṃ gaṅgarakṣitāt | [BKŚS, 24 43.1]
sarasvatīva vittāḍhyād īśvarād durgataṃ gatā | [BKŚS, 24 43.2]
gomukhas tu tato vīṇām avādayata līlayā | [BKŚS, 24 44.1]
yathā nāgarikair dīnair īkṣito gaṅgarakṣitaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 44.2]
gomukhāṅkāt tato vīṇā yāti sma priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 24 45.1]
kulaṭeva priyotsaṅgāt kāminaṃ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 24 45.2]
tataḥ pravādite tasmin pragīte cātimānuṣam | [BKŚS, 24 46.1]
vailakṣyād gomukhasyāsīd abhiprāyaḥ palāyitum | [BKŚS, 24 46.2]
kiṃtu nāradaśiṣyo 'yaṃ suto vā tumbaror iti | [BKŚS, 24 47.1]
yat satyam aham apy āsam adbhutaśrutivismitaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 47.2]
muktavīṇe tatas tatra śanair māṃ gomukho 'bravīt | [BKŚS, 24 48.1]
adhunā prāptaparyāyaṃ vādanaṃ bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 48.2]
hasitvā tam athāvocam adyāpi hi śiśur bhavān | [BKŚS, 24 49.1]
yo māṃ yatra kvacit tucche pravartayati vastuni | [BKŚS, 24 49.2]
nagnaśramaṇakānāṃ ca kirāṭānāṃ ca saṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 24 50.1]
vīṇāṃ vādayamānasya mādṛśaḥ kīdṛśaṃ phalam | [BKŚS, 24 50.2]
iti śrutvedam ukto 'ham anena kṛtamanyunā | [BKŚS, 24 51.1]
campāyāṃ kīdṛśaṃ kāryam abhavad bhavatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 51.2]
tatas tam uktavān asmi śrūyatām yadi na śrutam | [BKŚS, 24 52.1]
prāptir gandharvadattāyās tatra kāryam abhūd iti | [BKŚS, 24 52.2]
athāyam avadat tatra devīprāptiḥ phalaṃ yadi | [BKŚS, 24 53.1]
ihāpi gomukhaprāptiḥ phalam uttamam iṣyatām | [BKŚS, 24 53.2]
yuṣmadanyo na māṃ kaścid vīṇayā jitavān iti | [BKŚS, 24 54.1]
idaṃ me śreṣṭham āgamya śreṣṭhināpahṛtaṃ yaśaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 54.2]
so 'yam asmadyaśaścauro yadi nāśu nigṛhyate | [BKŚS, 24 55.1]
tyajāmy eṣa tataḥ prāṇān duḥkhabhārāturān iti | [BKŚS, 24 55.2]
mama tv āsīd asaṃdigdhaṃ sarvam atropapadyate | [BKŚS, 24 56.1]
maraṇābhyadhikakleśo mānabhaṅgo hi māninām | [BKŚS, 24 56.2]
śāstrārthajñānamattasya nigṛhītasya vādinaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 57.1]
kāntayā ca vimuktasya duḥkhaṃ kenopamīyate | [BKŚS, 24 57.2]
tasmād etad iha nyāyyam iti niścitya sādaram | [BKŚS, 24 58.1]
vyavasthāpayituṃ tantrīr ārabhe durvyavasthitāḥ | [BKŚS, 24 58.2]
tataḥ pṛthulitair netraiḥ pulakāliṅgitatvacaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 59.1]
anyonyasya niraikṣanta vadanāni sadaḥsadaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 59.2]
tantrīṣu karaśākhāgraiḥ parāmṛṣṭāsu te tataḥ | [BKŚS, 24 60.1]
hā hā kim idam ity uktvā pustanyastā ivābhavan | [BKŚS, 24 60.2]
athaitasyām avasthāyāṃ mayā vīṇā ca saṃhṛtā | [BKŚS, 24 61.1]
taiś ca muktāyatocchvāsair jīvaloko 'valokitaḥ | [BKŚS, 24 61.2]
harṣāruṇaparāmṛṣṭaṃ vikasadviśadaprabham | [BKŚS, 24 62.1]
abhrājata tataḥ sadyo gomukhānanapaṅkajam | [BKŚS, 24 62.2]

ayam eva mamāpy arthaḥ saphalīkriyatām iti | [BKŚS, 24 67.2]

prārthanā pratipanneti gomukhenoditaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 24 69.2]

tatra nandādibhir mitrair ārādhanaviśāradaiḥ | [BKŚS, 25 1.1]

jvarasya parivāro 'yam aṅgam asyāḥ prabādhate | [BKŚS, 25 89.2]

lāvaṇyam iva gātreṣu tad asyāḥ prāsphurat sphuṭam | [BKŚS, 25 90.2]
tatas tām uktavān asmi dhik tvāṃ niṣkaruṇāśayām | [BKŚS, 25 91.1]
śītajvarārtam aṅgair yā na pīḍayasi mām iti | [BKŚS, 25 91.2]
athāśliṣyaṃ tathā sā māṃ nādṛśyata yathā pṛthak | [BKŚS, 25 92.1]
viralevāruṇālokaṃ niśāntaśaśicandrikā | [BKŚS, 25 92.2]
tatas tāv āvayoś caṇḍau tathāśleṣacikitsayā | [BKŚS, 25 93.1]
apāyātāṃ muhūrtena kṛtrimākṛtrimau jvarau | [BKŚS, 25 93.2]
yātāyām atha yāminyāṃ buddhvā vṛttāntam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 25 94.1]
saṃghaḥ saṃhatya tāṃ svasmān nivāsān niravāsayat | [BKŚS, 25 94.2]
atha pravahaṇārūḍhām ṛṣidattāṃ mayā saha | [BKŚS, 25 95.1]
anayan muditaḥ śreṣṭhī gṛhaṃ maṅgalasaṃkulam | [BKŚS, 25 95.2]
tatrāvayoḥ sasumanāḥ sumanāḥ priyadarśanaḥ | [BKŚS, 25 96.1]
prītanāgarakānīkaṃ karagraham akārayat | [BKŚS, 25 96.2]
tad evam ṛṣidattā vaḥ saṃvṛttā paricārikā | [BKŚS, 25 97.1]
athavā kiṃ vikalpena svayam ālokyatām iti | [BKŚS, 25 97.2]
tathāpi kathitaṃ tena naiva saṃśayam atyajam | [BKŚS, 25 98.1]
duḥśraddhānaṃ hi sahasā kākatālīyam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 25 98.2]
mālālaṃkāravastrādi gṛhopakaraṇāni ca | [BKŚS, 25 99.1]
prasthāpya prāk tadārhāṇi tāṃ didṛkṣus tato 'gamam | [BKŚS, 25 99.2]
tatra cāsau mayā dṛṣṭā citrāṃśukavibhūṣaṇā | [BKŚS, 25 100.1]
nānāpuṣpāṃ hasantīva vasantopavanaśriyam | [BKŚS, 25 100.2]
pratimāḥ kāṣṭhamayyo 'pi śobhante bhūṣitās tathā | [BKŚS, 25 101.1]
lajjitāsurakanyāsu tādṛśīṣu tu kā kathā | [BKŚS, 25 101.2]
pravrajyāyāṃ punar yasyāḥ kāntir yāsīd akṛtrimā | [BKŚS, 25 102.1]
durlabhāṇi kvacit tasyā vācakāny akṣarāṇy api | [BKŚS, 25 102.2]
āsīc ca mama duḥśliṣṭaṃ kāntarūpavirūpayoḥ | [BKŚS, 25 103.1]
alaṃkārakalāpasya gurusārasya dhāraṇam | [BKŚS, 25 103.2]
alaṃkārāvṛtā tāvat kāntarūpasya cārutā | [BKŚS, 25 104.1]
na śakyā sarvathā draṣṭuṃ janair lolekṣaṇair api | [BKŚS, 25 104.2]
virūpasya tu vairūpyaṃ yat pracchādanam arhati | [BKŚS, 25 105.1]
prakāśayati tal loke paṭumaṇḍanaḍiṇḍimaḥ | [BKŚS, 25 105.2]
athādhiṣṭhitaparyaṅkam ṛṣidattopagamya mām | [BKŚS, 25 106.1]
avandata prahṛṣṭāpi pravrajyātyāgalajjitā | [BKŚS, 25 106.2]
tatas tām uktavān asmi sakhyāḥ kiṃ kāryam āśiṣā | [BKŚS, 25 107.1]
sarāgaiva satī yā tvaṃ vītarāgagatiṃ gatā | [BKŚS, 25 107.2]
mokṣaḥ kāruṇikair uktaḥ siddhair duḥkhakṣayaḥ kila | [BKŚS, 25 108.1]
kṣīṇaduḥsahaduḥkhatvān mokṣaṃ prāptāsi sarvathā | [BKŚS, 25 108.2]
sarvathā subhagatāmahoddhataḥ kiṃkaro bhavatu gomukhas tava | [BKŚS, 25 109.1]
yoṣito hi jitadṛṣṭabhartṛkās toṣayanti jananīsakhījanam | [BKŚS, 25 109.2]
{BKŚS, 26}
ityādikuṭilālāpakalāpagamitatrapām | [BKŚS, 26 1.1]
tām āmantrya svam āvāsam agacchaṃ sahagomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 1.2]
ekadā punar āyātas tayānuṣṭhitasatkriyaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 2.1]
vipaṇer gṛham āyātam apaśyaṃ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 26 2.2]
kañcukaṃ muñcatas tasya mayā dṛṣṭaḥ payodharaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 3.1]
payodharāntarālakṣyaḥ śaśīva parimaṇḍalaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 3.2]
āsīc ca mama yoṣaiṣā yatas tuṅgapayodharā | [BKŚS, 26 4.1]
stanakeśivatītvaṃ hi prathamaṃ strītvalakṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 26 4.2]
lokas tu yad imāṃ sarvaḥ pratipannaḥ pumān iti | [BKŚS, 26 5.1]
bhrāntijñānam idaṃ tasya kiṃcit sādṛśyakāritam | [BKŚS, 26 5.2]
athavā kiṃ vikalpena mamātimiracakṣuṣaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 6.1]
na hi dṛṣṭena dṛṣṭārthe draṣṭur bhavati saṃśayaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 6.2]
ityādibahusaṃkalpam animeṣavilocanam | [BKŚS, 26 7.1]
apaśyad ṛṣidattā māṃ paśyantaṃ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 26 7.2]
athāsau gadgadālāpā prītibāṣpāvṛtekṣaṇā | [BKŚS, 26 8.1]
ātmānaṃ cetayasveti priyadarśanam abravīt | [BKŚS, 26 8.2]
asāv api tam uddeśaṃ prakāśya jhagiti tviṣā | [BKŚS, 26 9.1]
taḍidguṇa ivāmbhodaṃ prāviśan mandirodaram | [BKŚS, 26 9.2]
ṛṣidattām athāpaśyaṃ krodhavisphāritekṣaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 10.1]
yayāpakramitaḥ śreṣṭhī mama locanagocarāt | [BKŚS, 26 10.2]
utthāya ca tataḥ sthānāt sakāmakrodhagomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 11.1]
punarvasugṛhaṃ prāpya paryaṅkaśaraṇo 'bhavam | [BKŚS, 26 11.2]
tataḥ kramaṃ parityajya kāmāvasthāparaṃparā | [BKŚS, 26 12.1]
tumulāyudhiseneva yugapad mām abādhata | [BKŚS, 26 12.2]
athācirāgataśrīko yathā bālaḥ pṛthagjanaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 13.1]
tathājñāpitavān asmi gomukhaṃ rūkṣayā girā | [BKŚS, 26 13.2]
api pravrajitābhartaḥ priyā me priyadarśanā | [BKŚS, 26 14.1]
akṛtapratikarmaiva kṣipram ānīyatām iti | [BKŚS, 26 14.2]
sa tu mām abravīt trastaḥ kā nāma priyadarśanā | [BKŚS, 26 15.1]
tyājitāḥ stha yayā sadyaś cetasaḥ sthiratām iti | [BKŚS, 26 15.2]
mayoktaṃ tava yaḥ syālaḥ puruṣaḥ priyadarśanaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 16.1]
ayam eva jagatsāraḥ pramadā priyadarśanā | [BKŚS, 26 16.2]
yac ca vakṣyasi sarvasyāṃ vārāṇasyām ayaṃ pumān | [BKŚS, 26 17.1]
bhavataḥ katham ekasya pramadeti tad ucyate | [BKŚS, 26 17.2]
ṛṣidattā virakteti paricchinnā purā tayā | [BKŚS, 26 18.1]
adhunā bhavataḥ kāntā jātety atra kim ucyate | [BKŚS, 26 18.2]
gatānugatiko lokaḥ pravṛtto hi yathā tathā | [BKŚS, 26 19.1]
paramārthaṃ punar veda sahasraikaḥ pumān iti | [BKŚS, 26 19.2]
tenoktaṃ janatāsiddhaṃ viruddham api na tyajet | [BKŚS, 26 20.1]
kriyate chagalaḥ śvāpi saṃhatya bahubhir balāt | [BKŚS, 26 20.2]
tena yuṣmadvidhaiḥ prājñair na vācyaṃ sad apīdṛśam | [BKŚS, 26 21.1]
aśraddheyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ pratyakṣam api yad bhavet | [BKŚS, 26 21.2]
śrūyatāṃ ca kathā tāvad arthasyāsya prakāśikā | [BKŚS, 26 22.1]
pramāṇaṃ hi pramāṇajñaiḥ purākalpe 'pi vartitam | [BKŚS, 26 22.2]
babhūva kauśiko nāma vedavedāṅgaviddvijaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 23.1]
satyavratatayā loke prasiddhaḥ satyakauśikaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 23.2]
kadācid abhiṣekāya tena yātena jāhnavīm | [BKŚS, 26 24.1]
saśiṣyaparivāreṇa tarantī prekṣitā śilā | [BKŚS, 26 24.2]
mahatāsau prayatnena śiṣyān anvaśiṣat tataḥ | [BKŚS, 26 25.1]
nāyam artho mahānarthaḥ prakāśyaḥ putrakair iti | [BKŚS, 26 25.2]
athaikaś capalas teṣāṃ baṭuḥ piṅgalanāmakaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 26.1]
vipaṇau mantrayāṃcakre kasyacid vaṇijaḥ puraḥ | [BKŚS, 26 26.2]
śreṣṭhi kiṃ na śṛṇoṣy ekam āścaryaṃ kathayāmi te | [BKŚS, 26 27.1]
tarantīṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi sopādhyāyaḥ śilām iti | [BKŚS, 26 27.2]
athāntaḥpurikā dāsī kimapi kretum āgatā | [BKŚS, 26 28.1]
etadālāpam ākarṇya rājapatnyai nyavedayat | [BKŚS, 26 28.2]
tayāpi kathitaṃ rājñe sa tāṃ pṛṣṭvā paraṃparām | [BKŚS, 26 29.1]
baṭunākhyātam āhvāyya pṛṣṭavān satyakauśikam | [BKŚS, 26 29.2]
satyaṃ brūhīti no vācyaḥ satyavādivrato bhavān | [BKŚS, 26 30.1]
mithyā brūhīti no vācyaḥ kāmī mithyāvrato hi saḥ | [BKŚS, 26 30.2]
kiṃtu yat piṅgalenoktam etad yuktaṃ parīkṣitum | [BKŚS, 26 31.1]
pramadāt satyam apy ete vadanti baṭavo yataḥ | [BKŚS, 26 31.2]
saśiṣyaiḥ kila yuṣmābhis tarantī prekṣitā śilā | [BKŚS, 26 32.1]
kim etat satyam āhosvin mṛṣety ākhyāyatām iti | [BKŚS, 26 32.2]
āsīc cāsya dhig etāṃ me ninditāṃ satyavāditām | [BKŚS, 26 33.1]
duḥśraddhānam aniṣṭaṃ ca yan mayā vācyam īdṛśam | [BKŚS, 26 33.2]
na satyam api tad vācyaṃ yad uktam asukhāvaham | [BKŚS, 26 34.1]
iti satyapravādo 'yaṃ na tyājyaḥ satyavādibhiḥ | [BKŚS, 26 34.2]
tasmāt satyam idaṃ tyaktvā mṛṣāvādaśatādhikam | [BKŚS, 26 35.1]
asatyam abhidhāsyāmi satyavādaśatādhikam | [BKŚS, 26 35.2]
athāvocat sa rājānaṃ rājan mithyā baṭor vacaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 36.1]
agniṃ paśyati yaḥ śītaṃ plavamānāṃ śilām asau | [BKŚS, 26 36.2]
kaḥ śraddadhyād baṭor vācaṃ nisargādhīracetasaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 37.1]
capalasyopamānaṃ hi prathamaṃ baṭumarkaṭāḥ | [BKŚS, 26 37.2]
viṣaṇṇam iti viśvāsya rājānaṃ satyakauśikaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 38.1]
viruddhavādinaṃ kruddhaḥ piṅgalaṃ niravāsayat | [BKŚS, 26 38.2]
tad evaṃ lokavidviṣṭam anuyukto 'pi bhūbhṛtā | [BKŚS, 26 39.1]
satyam satyapratijño 'pi nāvadat satyakauśikaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 39.2]
yuṣmākaṃ punar ajñātaśīlacāritrajanmanām | [BKŚS, 26 40.1]
viruddham idam īdṛk kaḥ śraddadhyād vadatām iti | [BKŚS, 26 40.2]
sa mayokto bhavān eva duḥśraddhānasya bhāṣitā | [BKŚS, 26 41.1]
yasyāsmin pramadāratne pumān iti viparyayaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 41.2]
kiṃ cānena pralāpena strīratnaṃ priyadarśanām | [BKŚS, 26 42.1]
acirāt svīkariṣyāmi krośatāṃ tvādṛśām iti | [BKŚS, 26 42.2]
evaṃ ca mama vṛttāntaṃ vijānann api gomukhaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 43.1]
vaidyarājaṃ samāhūya vaidyarājam upāgamat | [BKŚS, 26 43.2]
sa mamālāpam ākarṇya kāyacchāyāṃ vilokya ca | [BKŚS, 26 44.1]
pradhārya cāparair vaidyaiḥ śanakair idam abravīt | [BKŚS, 26 44.2]
mānaso 'sya vikāro 'yam īpsitālābhahetukaḥ | [BKŚS, 26 45.1]
tenāsmai rucitaṃ yat tad āśu saṃpādyatām iti | [BKŚS, 26 45.2]
atha nandopanandābhyāṃ saṃskāryāhāram ādarāt | [BKŚS, 26 46.1]
māṃ punarvasuhastena gomukhaḥ prāg abhojayat | [BKŚS, 26 46.2]
sa cāhāraḥ susaṃskāro lobhano 'py amṛtāśinām | [BKŚS, 26 47.1]
triphalākvāthavaddveṣān mamāṅgāni vyadhūnayat | [BKŚS, 26 47.2]
tato nandopanandābhyāṃ bhojyamānaḥ krameṇa tau | [BKŚS, 26 48.1]
saviṣādau karomi sma viṣādāv iva vairiṇau | [BKŚS, 26 48.2]
teṣu vandhyaprayatneṣu gomukhaḥ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 26 49.1]
lajjāmandapadanyāsaṃ namitānanam ānayat | [BKŚS, 26 49.2]
sa māṃ samānaparyaṅkamadhyam adhyāsitas tataḥ | [BKŚS, 26 50.1]
grāsān agrāsayat ṣaḍ vā sapta vā gomukhājñayā | [BKŚS, 26 50.2]
ye tatpāṇisarojasaṅgasubhagā grāsā mayā svāditās taiḥ sadyas tanutām anīyata sa me saṃkalpajanmā jvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 26 51.1]
śailendrāḥ śuciśukrabhānudahanapluṣṭopalādhityakā mandair apy udabindubhir navatarair ujhanti saṃtaptatām | [BKŚS, 26 51.2]
{BKŚS, 27}
tataḥ samāpitāhāraḥ suhṛdām eva saṃnidhau | [BKŚS, 27 1.1]
priyadarśanam āliṅgam anaṅgonmūlitatrapaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 1.2]
atha krodhāruṇamukho gomukhaḥ priyadarśanam | [BKŚS, 27 2.1]
pāṇāv ākṛṣya tvaritaḥ svagṛhān pratiyātavān | [BKŚS, 27 2.2]
sa mayoktaḥ samāyātaḥ krodhavistīrṇacakṣuṣā | [BKŚS, 27 3.1]
pāṇḍityāndhaka mitrāre mā sma tiṣṭhaḥ puro mama | [BKŚS, 27 3.2]
pipāsor madhuśauṇḍasya madhuśuktiṃ haret karāt | [BKŚS, 27 4.1]
yasya yas tasya kas tasmād arātir aparaḥ paraḥ | [BKŚS, 27 4.2]
ity uktaḥ sa viṣādena tyājitaś campakābhatām | [BKŚS, 27 5.1]
rāhuṇeva tuṣārāṃśur agamad dhūmadhūmratām | [BKŚS, 27 5.2]
taṃ ca dīrgham ahaḥśeṣam āyatāṃ ca vibhāvarīm | [BKŚS, 27 6.1]
pravṛddhair gamayāmi sma niṣādāsanacaṅkramaiḥ | [BKŚS, 27 6.2]
suhṛdvṛndavṛtaḥ prāyo dveṣyāśeṣavinodanaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 7.1]
priyadarśanasaṃprāpter upāyam agaveṣayam | [BKŚS, 27 7.2]
evaṃprāye ca vṛttānte dhavaloṣṇīṣakañcukau | [BKŚS, 27 8.1]
vismitau ciram ālokya sthavirau mām avocatām | [BKŚS, 27 8.2]
kiṃnimittam api brahman brahmadattaḥ prajeśvaraḥ | [BKŚS, 27 9.1]
bhavantam icchati draṣṭum iṣṭaṃ ced gamyatām iti | [BKŚS, 27 9.2]
idam ākarṇya yat satyam īṣad ākulamānasaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 10.1]
gomukhasya smarāmi sma vicāracaturaṃ manaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 10.2]
kiṃ gacchāni na gacchāni gacchataḥ kiṃ bhaved iti | [BKŚS, 27 11.1]
vitarkya kṣaṇam āsīn me saṃdehacchedanī matiḥ | [BKŚS, 27 11.2]
yo bandhavyo 'thavā vadhyo na sa kañcukidūtakaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 12.1]
sa hi śṛṅkhalanistriṃśapāṇibhiḥ parivāryate | [BKŚS, 27 12.2]
ye ca kecij janā yeṣāṃ viṣaye sukham āsate | [BKŚS, 27 13.1]
rājñām ājñām avajñāya teṣāṃ jīvanti te katham | [BKŚS, 27 13.2]
amandaspandam etac ca kāṅkṣitām akṣi dakṣiṇam | [BKŚS, 27 14.1]
ākhyatīva priyāprāptiṃ mahyaṃ tad gamanaṃ hitam | [BKŚS, 27 14.2]
niścityetyādi nirgatya gṛhāt pravahaṇaṃ bahiḥ | [BKŚS, 27 15.1]
kañcukyānītam adrākṣam ārukṣaṃ cāviśaṅkitaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 15.2]
paurasaṃghātasaṃbādhaṃ rājamārgaṃ vyatītya ca | [BKŚS, 27 16.1]
rājadvāraṃ vrajāmi sma citramaṅgalamaṇḍalam | [BKŚS, 27 16.2]
gomukhākhyāpitābhikhyaṃ tad adhyāsya kṣaṇaṃ tataḥ | [BKŚS, 27 17.1]
prāvikṣaṃ prathamāṃ kakṣāṃ dvāḥsthavṛndābhinanditaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 17.2]
samṛddhiḥ srūyatāṃ tasyāḥ kṛtaṃ vā tatpraśaṃsayā | [BKŚS, 27 18.1]
ko hi varṇayituṃ śakto naro meror adhityakām | [BKŚS, 27 18.2]
tām atikramya pañcānyāḥ prakṛṣṭatararamyatāḥ | [BKŚS, 27 19.1]
saptamyāṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi mahāsthānaṃ mahīpateḥ | [BKŚS, 27 19.2]
śrutismṛtipurāṇādigranthasāgarapāragaiḥ | [BKŚS, 27 20.1]
dhanurvedāditattvajñaiḥ kalādakṣaiś ca sevitam | [BKŚS, 27 20.2]
viruddhaṃ bibhrataṃ mūrtyā candramaḥsavitṛprabhām | [BKŚS, 27 21.1]
sukhasevyaṃ durīkṣaṃ ca taptāṃśum iva haimanam | [BKŚS, 27 21.2]
svastikṛtvā tatas tasmai jātarūpāṅgam ānasam | [BKŚS, 27 22.1]
adhyatiṣṭhaṃ nṛpādiṣṭaṃ nirvikārāmbarāvṛtam | [BKŚS, 27 22.2]
nṛpas tu māṃ ciraṃ dṛṣṭvā snehasnigdhāyatekṣaṇaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 23.1]
tatas tārakarājākhyaṃ senābhṛtāram aikṣata | [BKŚS, 27 23.2]
sa tu mām abhitaḥ sthitvā kāryamātrasya vācakaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 24.1]
avocad vacanaṃ cāru vispaṣṭamadhurākṣaram | [BKŚS, 27 24.2]
āryajyeṣṭha manas tāvad avikṣiptaṃ kuru kṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 27 25.1]
rājā manmukhasaṃkrāntair vākyais tvām eṣa bhāṣate | [BKŚS, 27 25.2]
yeyaṃ bhāgīrathīśubhrā kāśibhūpatisaṃtatiḥ | [BKŚS, 27 26.1]
sā kim ākhyāyate tubhyaṃ prathitā pṛthivīva yā | [BKŚS, 27 26.2]
asyām asya prasūtasya brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ | [BKŚS, 27 27.1]
ye guṇās te 'pi te buddhāḥ śiśirāṃśor ivāṃśavaḥ | [BKŚS, 27 27.2]
asyāsīt kāliyo nāma śreṣṭhī prāṇapriyaḥ suhṛt | [BKŚS, 27 28.1]

{BKŚS, 28}
evaṃ vārāṇasīstaṃ māṃ dāramitrair upāsitam | [BKŚS, 28 1.1]
upātiṣṭhanta kāśikyāḥ śreṇayaḥ paṇyapāṇayaḥ | [BKŚS, 28 1.2]
tāṃś ca bhāṣitavān asmi sarvavṛttāntakovidaḥ | [BKŚS, 28 2.1]
ayam āryakaniṣṭho vaḥ śreṇiśreṣṭhī bhavatv iti | [BKŚS, 28 2.2]
atha yāte kvacit kāle saudhe sapriyadarśanaḥ | [BKŚS, 28 3.1]
sopāne tāram aśrauṣaṃ haṃsānām iva nisvanam | [BKŚS, 28 3.2]
mama tv āsīn na haṃsānāṃ nūpurāṇām ayaṃ dhvaniḥ | [BKŚS, 28 4.1]
padamantharasaṃcāro yac cāvicchinnasaṃtatiḥ | [BKŚS, 28 4.2]
na caiṣa kulanārīṇām upapattyā virudhyate | [BKŚS, 28 5.1]
utsavābhyudayeṣv eva tā hi bibhrati bhūṣaṇam | [BKŚS, 28 5.2]
tenāntaḥpurasaṃcāravārastrīcaraṇocitaḥ | [BKŚS, 28 6.1]
kimartham api sopāne caraty ābharaṇadhvani | [BKŚS, 28 6.2]
evaṃ ca vimṛśann eva tārābharaṇaśiñjitāḥ | [BKŚS, 28 7.1]
citrāṃśukadharā nārīr apaśyaṃ rūḍhayauvanāḥ | [BKŚS, 28 7.2]
tāsāṃ kumudikā nāma lokalocanakaumudī | [BKŚS, 28 8.1]
pragalbhāpi vinīteva vanditvā mām abhāṣata | [BKŚS, 28 8.2]

atha svayānam āropya sā priyāṃ priyadarśanām | [BKŚS, 28 111.1]
kañcukyādicamūguptā nagaropavanaṃ gatā | [BKŚS, 28 111.2]
ahaṃ tu tad dinaṃ nītvā kṛcchrān mandiraniṣkuṭe | [BKŚS, 28 112.1]
harmyamūrdhānam ārohaṃ rājaputrīdidṛkṣayā | [BKŚS, 28 112.2]
atha pravahaṇenāsau nabhasvatpaṭuraṃhasā | [BKŚS, 28 113.1]
madgṛhadvāram āgacchad dūrād unnamitānanā | [BKŚS, 28 113.2]
sā ca māṃ tatra paśyantī saṃtataṃ priyadarśanām | [BKŚS, 28 114.1]
gāḍhaṃ niṣpīḍayantī ca ciram aṅgaṃ nyapīḍayat | [BKŚS, 28 114.2]
vandanāchadmanā paścān māyy ātmānaṃ nidhāya sā | [BKŚS, 28 115.1]
cetovinimayaṃ kṛtvā pravṛttā śibikām iti | [BKŚS, 28 115.2]
ārādhayāmi nṛpasūnukṛte nu gaurīṃ kiṃ khānayāmi caturais tvaritaṃ suruṅgām | [BKŚS, 28 116.1]
ityādyupāyaśatacintanatāntacetāḥ kṛcchrān niśām anayam apratilabdhanidraḥ | [BKŚS, 28 116.2]
